  sa bhagavān sṛṣṭvā idam jagat  tasya ca sthitim cikīrṣuḥ marīḍī ādīn agre sṛṣṭvā prajāpatīn pravṛtti lakṣaṇam dharmam grāhayāmāsa veda uktam tatas  anyān ca sanaka sanandana ādīn utpādya nivṛtti lakṣaṇam dharmam jñāna vairāgya lakṣaṇam grāhayāmāsa dvividhaḥ  hi veda uktaḥ  dharmaḥ pravṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ  nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ  ca jagataḥ sthiti kāraṇam prāṇinām sākṣāt  abhyudaya niḥśreyasa hetuḥ  yaḥ sa dharmaḥ  brāhmaṇa ādyaiḥ  varṇibhiḥ  āśramibhiḥ  ca śreyaḥ  arthibhiḥ  anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ dīrgheṇa kālena anuṣṭhātṝṇām kāma udbhavāt  dhīyamāna viveka jñāna hetukena adharmeṇa abhibhūyamāne dharme pravardhamāne ca adharme jagataḥ sthitim paripipālayiṣuḥ sa ādikartā nārāyaṇa ākhyaḥ  viṣṇuḥ  bhaumasya brahmaṇaḥ  brāhmaṇa tvasya ca abhirakṣaṇa artham devakyām vasudevāt  aṃśena kṛṣṇaḥ kila sambabhūva brāhmaṇa tvasya hi rakṣaṇena rakṣitaḥ syāt  vaidikaḥ  dharmaḥ tad adhīna tvāt  varṇa āśrama bhedānām sa ca bhagavān jñāna aiśvarya śakti bala vīrya tejobhiḥ sadā sampannas triguṇa ātmikām vaiṣṇavīm svām māyām mūlaprakṛtim vaśīkṛtya ajaḥ avyayaḥ  bhūtānām īśvaraḥ  nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvaḥ  api san sva māyayā dehavān iva jāta iva ca loka anugraham kurvan lakṣyate sva prayojana abhāve api bhūta anujighṛkṣayā vaidikam hi dharma dvayam arjunāya śoka moha mahodadhau nimagnāya upadideśa guṇa adhikaiḥ  hi gṛhītaḥ  anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ  ca dharmaḥ pracayam gamiṣyati iti tam dharmam bhagavatā yathā upadiṣṭam vedavyāsaḥ sarvajñaḥ  bhagavān gīta ākhyaiḥ saptabhiḥ śloka śataiḥ  upanibabandha tad  idam gītā śāstram samasta veda artha sāra saṅgraha bhūtam durvijñayā artham tad artha āviṣkaraṇāya anekaiḥ  vivṛta pada padārtha vākya vākya artha nyāyam api atyanta viruddha an ekārtha tvena laukikaiḥ  gṛhyamāṇam upalabhya aham vivekataḥ  artha nirdhāraṇa artham saṃkṣepataḥ  vivaraṇam kariṣyāmi tasya asya gītā śāstrasya saṃkṣepataḥ prayojanam param niḥśreyasam sa hetukasya saṃsārasya atyanta uparama lakṣaṇam tad  ca sarva karma sannyāsa pūrvakād ātma jñāna niṣṭhā rūpād dharmāt  bhavati tathā imam eva gīta artha dharmam uddiśya bhagavatā eva uktam sa hi dharmaḥ su paryāptaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ pada vedane iti  anugītāsu tatra eva ca uktam na eva dharmī na ca adharmī na ca eva hi śubha aśubhī yaḥ syāt  ekāyane līnas tūṣṇīm kiṃcid  acintayan jñānam saṃnyāsa lakṣaṇam iti ca iha api ca ante uktam arjunāya sarva dharmān parityajya mām ekam śaraṇam vraja iti abhyudaya arthaḥ  api yaḥ pravṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ  dharmaḥ  varṇān āśramān   ca uddiśya vihitaḥ sa deva ādi sthāna prāpti hetuḥ  api san īśvara arpaṇa buddhyā anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ sattva śuddhaye bhavati phala abhisandhi varjitaḥ śuddha sattvasya ca jñāna niṣṭhā yogya tā prāpti dvāreṇa jñāna utpatti hetu tvena ca niḥśreyasa hetu tvam api pratipadyate tathā ca imam eva artham abhisandhāya vakṣyati brahmaṇi  ādhāya karmāṇi yoginaḥ karma kurvanti saṅgam tyaktvā ātma śuddhaye iti imam dvi prakāram dharmam niḥśreyasa prayojanam parama artha tattvam ca vāsudeva ākhyam para brahma abhidheya bhūtam viśeṣataḥ abhivyañjayat  viśiṣṭa prayojana sambandha abhidheyavat  gīta aśāstram yatas  tad artha vijñānena samasta puruṣa artha siddhiḥ atas  tad vivaraṇe yatnaḥ kriyate mayā atra ca dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍava anīkam iti  ārabhya yāvat  na yotsya iti govindam uktvā tūṣṇīm babhūva ha iti  etad antar  prāṇinām śoka moha ādi saṃsāra bīja bhūta doṣa udbhava kāraṇa pradarśana artha tvena vyākhyeyaḥ  granthaḥ tathā hi arjunena rājya guru putra mitra suhṛd sva jana saṃbandhi bāndhaveṣu aham eteṣām mama ete iti  evam bhrānti pratyaya nimitta sneha viccheda ādi nimittau ātmanaḥ śoka mohau pradarśitau katham bhīṣmam aham saṃkhye iti  ādinā śoka mohābhyām hi  abhibhūta viveka vijñānaḥ svata eva kṣatra dharme yuddhe pravṛttaḥ  api tasmāt  yuddhāt  upararāma para dharmam ca bhikṣā jīvana ādikam kartum pravavṛte tathā ca sarva prāṇinām śoka moha ādi doṣa āviṣṭa cetasām svabhāvata eva svadharma parityāgaḥ pratiṣiddha sevā ca syāt  svadharme pravṛttānām api teṣām vāc manaḥ kāya ādīnām pravṛttiḥ phala abhisaṃdhi pūrvikā eva sā ahaṃkārā ca bhavati tatra evam sati dharma adharma upacayāt  iṣṭa aniṣṭa janma sukha duḥkha ādi prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ saṃsāraḥ  anuparataḥ  bhavati iti  atas  saṃsāra bīja bhūtau śoka mohau tayoś ca sarva karma saṃnyāsa pūrvakād ātma jñānāt na anyatas  nivṛttiḥ  iti tad upadidikṣuḥ sarva loka anugraha artham arjunam nimittīkṛtya āha bhagavān vāsudevaḥ aśocyān ityādi atra kecid  āhuḥ sarva karma saṃnyāsa pūrvakād ātma jñāna niṣṭhā mātrāt  eva kevalāt  kaivalyam na prāpyata eva kim tarhi agnihotra ādi śrauta smārta karma sahitāt  jñānāt  kaivalya prāptiḥ  iti sarvāsu gītāsu niścitaḥ  artha  iti jñāpakam ca āhuḥ  asya arthasya atha ced  tvam imam dharmyam saṃgrāmam na kariṣyasi karmaṇi  eva adhikāra s te kuru karma eva tasmāt  tvam iti  ādi hiṃsā ādi yukta tvāt  vaidikam karma adharmāya iti iyam api  āśaṅkā na kāryā katham kṣātram karma yuddha lakṣaṇam guru bhrātṛ putra ādi hiṃsā lakṣaṇam atyantam krūram api svadharma iti kṛtvā na adharmāya tad akaraṇe ca tatas  svadharmam kīrtim ca hitvā pāpam avāpsyasi iti bruvatā yāvat  jīvādi śruti coditānām paśu ādi hiṃsā lakṣaṇānām ca karmaṇām prāk  eva na adharma tvam iti su niścitam uktam bhavati iti tad  asat  jñāna karma niṣṭhayoḥ  vibhāga vacanāt  buddhi dvaya āśrayayoḥ aśocyān iti  ādinā bhagavatā yāvat  svadharmam api ca avekṣya iti  etad antena granthena yad parama artha ātma tattva nirūpaṇam kṛtam tad  sāṃkhyam tad viṣayā buddhiḥ  ātmanaḥ  janma ādi ṣaṣ vikriyā abhāvāt  akartā ātmā iti prakaraṇa artha nirūpaṇāt  yā jāyate sā sāṃkhya buddhiḥ sā yeṣām jñāninām ucitā bhavati te sāṃkhyāḥ etasyāḥ  buddheḥ  janmanaḥ prāk  ātmanaḥ  deha ādi vyatiriktatva kartṛtva bhoktṛtva bhoktṛtva ādi apekṣaḥ  dharma adharma viveka pūrva kaḥ  mokṣa sādhana anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇaḥ  yogaḥ tad viṣayā buddhiḥ yoga buddhiḥ sā yeṣām karmiṇām ucitā bhavati te yoginaḥ tathā ca bhagavatā vibhakte dve buddhī nirdiṣṭe eṣā te abhihitā sāṃkhye buddhiḥ  yoge tu  imām śṛṇu iti tayoś ca sāṃkhya buddhi āśrayām jñāna yogena niṣṭhām sāṃkhyānām vibhaktām vakṣyati purā veda ātmanā mayā proktā iti tathā ca yoga buddhi āśrayām karma yogena niṣṭhām vibhaktām vakṣyati karma yogena yoginām iti evam sāṃkhya buddhim yoga buddhim ca āśritya dve niṣṭhe vibhakte bhagavatā eva ukte jñāna karmaṇoḥ kartṛtva ākartṛtva ekatva anekatva buddhi āśrayayoḥ yugapad eka puruṣa āśrayatva asaṃbhavam paśyatā yathā etad vibhāga vacanam tathā eva darśitam śātapathīye brāhmaṇe etam eva pravrājinaḥ  lokam icchantaḥ  brāhmaṇāḥ pravrajanti iti sarva karma saṃnyāsam vidhāya tad śeṣeṇa kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥ  yeṣām naḥ ayam ātmāyam lokaḥ iti tatra eva ca prāk  dāra parigrahāt  puruṣa ātmaḥ prākṛtaḥ  dharma jijñāsā uttara kālam lokatraya sādhanam putram dvi prakāram ca vittam mānuṣam dvi prakāram ca tatra mānuṣam karma rūpam pitṛ loka prāpti sādhanam vidyām ca daivam vittam deva loka prāpti sādhanam saḥ  akāmayata iti avidyā kāmavata eva sarvāṇi karmāṇi śrauta ādīni darśitāni tebhyaḥ  vyutthāya pravrajanti iti vyutthānam ātmānam eva lokam icchataḥ  akāmasya vihitam tad  etad  vibhāga vacanam anupapannam syāt  yadi śrauta karma jñānayoḥ samuccayaḥ  abhipretaḥ syāt  bhagavataḥ na ca arjunasya praśna upapannaḥ  bhavati jyāyasī ced  karmaṇas te iti  ādiḥ eka puruṣa anuṣṭheyatva asaṃbhavam buddhi karmaṇoḥ bhagavatā pūrvam anuktam katham arjunaḥ  aśrutam buddhā ca karmaṇaḥ  jyāyaḥ tvam bhagavati  adhyāropayet  mṛṣā eva jyāyasī ced  karmaṇas te matā buddhiḥ iti kim ca yadi buddhi karmaṇoḥ sarveṣām samuccaya uktaḥ syāt  arjunasya api sa ukta eva iti yad  chrāya etayoḥ  ekam tad  me brūhi su niścitam iti katham ubhayoḥ  upadeśe sati anyatara viṣaya eva praśnaḥ syāt  na hi pitta praśamana arthinaḥ vaidyena madhuram śītalam ca bhoktavyam iti  upadiṣṭe tayoḥ  anyatarat pitta praśamana kāraṇam brūhi iti praśnaḥ saṃbhavati atha arjunasya bhagavat ukta vacana artha vivekānavadhāraṇa nimittaḥ praśnaḥ kalpyeta tathā api bhagavatā praśna anurūpam prativacanam deyam mayā buddhi karmaṇoḥ samuccaya uktaḥ kim artham ittham tvam bhrāntaḥ  asi iti na tu punar  prativacanam ananurūpam pṛṣṭāt  anyat  eva dve niṣṭhā mayā purā proktā iti vaktum yuktam na api smārtena eva karmaṇā buddheḥ samuccaye abhiprete vibhāga vacana ādi sarvam upapananam kim ca kṣatriyasya yuddham smārtam karma svadharma iti jānataḥ tad  kim karmaṇi ghoraḥ  mām niyojayasi iti  upālambhaḥ  anupapannaḥ tasmāt  gīta aśāstre īṣat mātreṇa api śrautena smārtena vā karmaṇā ātma jñānasya samuccayaḥ  na kenacid  darśayitum śakyaḥ yasya tu  ajñānāt  rāga ādi doṣa taḥ  vā karmaṇi pravṛttasya yajñena dānena tapasā vā viśuddha sattvasya jñānam utpannam parama artha tattva viṣayam ekam eva idam sarvam brahma akartṛ ca iti tasya karmaṇi karma prayojane ca nivṛtte api loka saṃgraha artham yatna pūrvam yathā pravṛttiḥ tathā eva pravṛttasya yad  pravṛtti rūpam dṛśyate na tad  karma yena buddheḥ samuccayaḥ syāt  yathā bhagavataḥ  vāsudevasya kṣatra dharma ceṣṭitam na jñānena samuccīyate puruṣa artha siddhaye tadvat  tad phala abhisaṃdhi ahaṃkāra abhāvasya tulya tvāt  viduṣaḥ tattvavin na aham karomi iti manyate na ca tad phalam abhisandhatte yathā ca svarga ādi kāma arthinaḥ  agnihotra ādi karma lakṣaṇa dharma anuṣṭhānāya āhitāgneḥ kāmye eva agni hotra ādau pravṛttasya sāmi kṛte vinaṣṭā api kāme tad  eva agni hotra ādi anutiṣṭhataḥ  api na tad kāmyam agni hotra ādi bhavati tathā ca darśayati bhagavān kurvan   api na lipyate na karoti na lipyate iti tatra tatra yad  ca pūrvaiḥ pūrvataram kṛtam karmaṇā eva hi saṃsiddhim āsthitā janaka ādayaḥ iti tad  tu pravibhajya vijñeyam tad  katham yadi tāvat  pūrve janaka ādayaḥ tattva vidaḥ  api pravṛtta karmāṇaḥ syuḥ te loka saṃgraha artham guṇā guṇeṣu vartante iti jñānena eva saṃsiddhim āsthitāḥ karma saṃnyāse prāpte api karmaṇā saha eva saṃsiddhim āsthitāḥ na karma saṃnyāsam kṛtavanta iti  arthaḥ atha na te tattva vidaḥ īśvara samarpitena karmaṇā sādhana bhūtena saṃsiddhim sattva śuddhim jñāna utpatti lakṣaṇām vā saṃsiddhim āsthitā janakādaya iti vyākhyeyam etam eva artham vakṣyati bhagavān sattva śuddhaye karma kurvanti iti sva karmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhim vindati mānavaḥ iti  uktvā siddhim prāptasya punar jñāna niṣṭhām vakṣyati siddhim prāptaḥ  yathā brahma iti  ādinā tasmāt  gīta aśāstre kevalāt  eva tattva jñānān mokṣa prāptiḥ na karma samuccitāt  iti niścitaḥ  arthaḥ yathā ca ayam arthaḥ tathā prakaraṇaśaḥ vibhajya tatra tatra darśayiṣyāmaḥ tatra eva dharma saṃmūḍha cetasaḥ  mithyājñānavataḥ  mahati śoka sāgare nimagnasya arjunasya anyatra ātma jñānāt  uddharaṇam apaśyan bhagavān vāsudevaḥ tatas  kṛpayā arjunam uddidhārayiṣuḥ ātma jñānāya avatārayat    āha na śocyā aśocyāḥ bhīṣma droṇa ādayaḥ sat vṛtta tvāt parama artha svarūpeṇa ca nitya tvāt  tān aśocyān anvaśocaḥ  anuśocitavān asi te mriyante mad nimittam aham taiḥ  vinābhūtaḥ kim kariṣyāmi rājya sukha ādinā iti tvam prajñā vādān prajñāvatām buddhimatām vāda an   ca vacanāni ca bhāṣase tad  etad  mauḍhyam pāṇḍityam ca viruddham ātmani darśayasi unmatta iva iti  abhiprāyaḥ yasmāt  gatāsūn gata prāṇān mṛtān agatāsūn agata prāṇān jīvataś ca na anuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ ātma jñāḥ paṇḍā ātma viṣayā buddhiḥ  yeṣām te hi paṇḍitāḥ pāṇḍityam nirvidya iti śruteḥ paramārtha taḥ  tu tān nityān aśocyān anuśocasi atas  mūḍhaḥ  asi iti  abhiprāyaḥ kutas  te aśocyāḥ yatas  nityāḥ katham na tu  eva jātu kadācid  aham nāsam kintv āsam eva atīteṣu deha utpatti vināśeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu viyat  iva nitya eva aham āsam iti  abhiprāyaḥ tathā na tvam na āsīḥ kintv āsīḥ  eva tathā na ime janādhipā āsan kintv āsann eva tathā na ca eva na bhaviṣyāmaḥ kintu bhaviṣyāma eva sarve vayam atas  asmāt  deha vināśāt  param uttara kāle api triṣu  api kāleṣu nityā ātma svarūpeṇa iti  arthaḥ deha abheda anuvṛttyā bahuvacanam na ātma bheda abhiprāyeṇa tatra katham iva nitya ātmā iti dṛṣṭāntam āha dehaḥ  asya asti iti dehī tasya dehinaḥ  dehavataḥ ātmanaḥ  asmin vartamāne dehā yathā yena prakāreṇa kaumāram kumāra bhāvaḥ  bālya avasthā yauvanam yūnaḥ  bhāvaḥ madhyamā avasthā jarā vayaḥ hāniḥ jīrṇa avasthā iti  etāḥ tisraḥ  avasthāḥ anyonya vilakṣaṇāḥ tāsām prathama avasthā nāśe na nāśaḥ dvitīya avasthā upajane na upajana ātmanaḥ kim tarhi avikriyasya eva dvitīya tṛtīya avasthā prāptiḥ ātmanaḥ  dṛṣṭā tathā tadvat  eva dehāt  anyaḥ  dehaḥ  deha antaram tasya prāptiḥ deha antara prāptiḥ avikriyasya eva ātmana iti  arthaḥ dhīraḥ  dhīmān tatra evam sati na muhyati na moham āpadyate yadi api  ātma vināśa nimittaḥ  mohaḥ  na saṃbhavati nitya ātmā iti vijānataḥ tathā api śīta uṣṇa sukha duḥkha prāpti nimittaḥ  mohaḥ  laukikaḥ  dṛśyate sukha viyoga nimittaḥ  mohaḥ  duḥkha saṃyoga nimitta ca śokaḥ iti  etad  arjunasya vacanam āśaṅkaya bhagavān āha mātrā ābhiḥ mīyante śabda ādaya iti śrotra ādīni indriyāṇi mātrāṇām sparśāḥ śabda ādibhiḥ saṃyogāḥ te śīta uṣṇa sukha duḥkha dāḥ śītam uṣṇam sukham duḥkham ca prayacchanti iti athavā spṛśyanta iti sparśā viṣayāḥ śabda ādayaḥ mātrāś ca sparśāḥ  ca śīta uṣṇa sukha duḥkha dāḥ śītam kadācid  sukham kadācid  duḥkham tathā uṣṇam api aniyata svarūpam sukha duḥkhe punar  niyata rūpe yatas  na vyabhicarataḥ atas tābhyām pṛthak  śīta uṣṇayoḥ grahaṇam yasmāt  te mātrā sparśa ādayaḥ āgama apāyinaḥ āgama apāya śīlāḥ tasmāt  anityāḥ atas  tān śīta uṣṇa ādīn titikṣasva prasahasva teṣu harṣam viṣādam vā mā kārṣīḥ iti  arthaḥ śīta uṣṇa ādīn sahataḥ kim syāt  iti śṛṇu yam hi puruṣam same duḥkha sukhe yasya tam sama duḥkha sukham sukha duḥkha prāptau harṣa viṣāda rahitam dhīram dhīmantam na vyathayanti na cālayanti nitya ātma darśanāt  ete yathā uktāḥ śīta uṣṇa ādayaḥ sa nitya ātma svarūpa darśa niṣṭhaḥ  dvandva sahiṣṇuḥ amṛta tvāya amṛta bhāvāya mokṣāya iti  arthaḥ kalpate samarthaḥ  bhavati itas  ca śoka mohau akṛtvā śīta uṣṇa ādi sahanam yuktam yasmāt  na asataḥ  avidyamānasya śīta uṣṇa ādeḥ sa kāraṇasya na vidyate na asti bhāvaḥ bhavanam astitā na hi śīta uṣṇa ādi sa kāraṇam pramāṇaiḥ  nirūpyamāṇam vastu sambhavati vikāraḥ  hi saḥ vikāraḥ  ca vyabhicarati yathā ghaṭa ādi saṃsthānam cakṣuṣā nirūpyamāṇam mṛd vyatirekeṇa anupalabdheḥ  asat  tathā sarvaḥ  vikāraḥ kāraṇa vyatirekeṇa anupalabdheḥ  asat  janma pradhvaṃsābhyām prāk  ūrdhvam ca anupalabdheḥ kāryasya ghaṭa ādeḥ mṛdādi kāraṇasya ca tad kāraṇa vyatirekeṇa anupalabdheḥ  asattvam tad asattve sarva abhāva prasaṅga iti ced  na sarvatra buddhi dvaya upalabdheḥ sat buddhiḥ  asat buddhiḥ  iti yad viṣayā buddhiḥ  na vyabhicarati tad  sat  yad viṣayā vyabhicarati tad  asat  iti sat asat vibhāge buddhi tantre sthite sarvatra dve buddhī sarvaiḥ  upalabhyete samāna adhikaraṇe na nīlotpalavat  san ghaṭaḥ san paṭaḥ san hastī iti evam sarvatra tayoḥ  buddhyoḥ ghaṭa ādi buddhiḥ  vyabhicarati tathā ca darśitam na tu sat buddhiḥ tasmāt  ghaṭa ādi buddhi viṣayaḥ  asan vyabhicārāt  na tu sat buddhi viṣayaḥ avyabhicārāt  ghaṭe vinaṣṭe ghaṭa buddhau vyabhicarantyām sat buddhiḥ  api vyabhicarati iti ced  na paṭād evapi sat buddhi darśanāt  viśeṣaṇa viṣayā eva sā sat buddhiḥ sat buddhivat  ghaṭa buddhiḥ  api ghaṭa antarā dṛśyata iti ced  na paṭa ādau adarśanāt  sat buddhiḥ  api naṣṭe ghaṭe na dṛśyata iti ced  na viśeṣya abhāvāt sat buddhiḥ  viśeṣaṇa viṣayā satī viśeṣya abhāve viśeṣaṇa anupapattau kiṃviṣayā syāt  na tu punar  sat buddheḥ viṣaya abhāvāt eka adhikaraṇa tvam ghaṭa ādi viśeṣya abhāve na yuktam iti ced  na idam udakam iti marīci ādau anyatara abhāve api sāmānādhikaraṇya darśanāt tasmāt  deha ādeḥ  dvandvasya ca sa kāraṇasya asataḥ  na vidyate bhāva iti tathā sataś ca ātmanaḥ  abhāvaḥ  avidyamāna tā na vidyate sarvatra avyabhicārāt  iti  avocāma evam ātmānātmanoḥ sat asatoḥ ubhayoḥ  api dṛṣṭaḥ upalabdhaḥ  antaḥ nirṇayaḥ sat  sat  eva asat  asad eva iti tu  anayoḥ yathā uktayoḥ tattva darśibhiḥ tad  iti sarvanāma sarvam ca brahma tasya nāma tad  iti tad bhāvaḥ  tattvam brahmaṇaḥ  yāthātmyam tad  draṣṭum śīlam yeṣām te tattva darśinaḥ taiḥ  tattva darśibhiḥ tvam api tattva darśinām dṛṣṭim āśritya śokam moham ca hitvā śīta uṣṇa ādīni niyata aniyata rūpāṇi dvandvāni vikāraḥ  ayam asann eva marīci jalavan mithyā avabhāsate iti manasi niścitya titikṣasva iti  abhiprāyaḥ kim punar  tad  yad  sat  eva sarvadā eva asti iti ucyate avināśi na vinaṣṭum śīlam yasya iti tuśabdaḥ  asataḥ  viśeṣaṇa arthaḥ tad  viddhi vijānīhi kim yena sarvam idam jagat  tatam vyāptam sadākhyena brahmaṇā sa ākāśam ākāśena eva ghaṭa ādayaḥ vināśam adarśanam abhāvam avyayasya na vyeti upacaya apacayau na yāti iti avyayam tasya avyayasya na etad  sadākhyam brahma svena rūpeṇa vyeti vyabhicarati niravayava tvāt  deha ādivat  na api  ātmīyena ātmīya abhāvāt yathā devadattaḥ  dhana hānyā vyeti na tu evam brahma vyeti atas  avyayasya asya brahmaṇaḥ vināśam na kaścid  kartum arhati na kaścid  atmānam vināśayitum śaknoti īśvaraḥ  api ātmā hi brahma sva ātmani ca kriyā virodhāt kim punar  tad  asat  yad  sva ātma sattām vyabhicarati iti ucyate antar  vināśaḥ vidyate yeṣām te antavantaḥ yathā mṛgatṛṣṇikā ādau sat buddhiḥ anuvṛttā pramāṇa nirūpaṇa ante vicchidyate sa tasya antar  tathā ime dehāḥ svapna māyā deha ādi vaca antavantaḥ nityasya śarīriṇaḥ śarīravataḥ  anāśinaḥ aprameyarya ātmanaḥ  antavanta iti uktāḥ vivekibhiḥ iti  arthaḥ nityasya anāśinaḥ iti na punaruktam nitya tvasya dvividha tvāt  lokā nāśasya ca yathā dehaḥ  bhasmībhūtaḥ  adarśanam gataḥ  naṣṭa ucyate vidyamānaḥ  api yathā anyathā pariṇataḥ  vyādhi ādi yuktaḥ  jātaḥ  naṣṭa ucyate tatra nityasya ṭh anāśinaḥ iti dvividhena api nāśena asaṃbandhaḥ  asya iti  arthaḥ anyathā pṛthivī ādivat  api nitya tvam syāt  ātmanaḥ tad  mā bhūt iti nityasya anāśinaḥ iti āha aprameyamya na prameyasya pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇaiḥ aparicchādyasya iti  arthaḥ nanu āgamena ātmā paricchidyate pratyakṣa ādinā ca pūrvam na ātmanaḥ svatas siddha tvāt sirā hi ātmani pramātari pramitsoḥ pramāṇa anveṣaṇā bhavati na hi pūrvam ittham aham iti ātmānam apramāya pa cāt prameya paricchādāya pravartate na hi ātmā nāma kasyacid  aprasiddhaḥ  bhavati śāstram tu antyam pramāṇam atad dharma adhyāropaṇa mātra nivartaka tvena pramāṇa tvam ātmanaḥ pratipadyate na hi  ajñāta artha jñāpaka tvena tathā ca śrutiḥ yad  sākṣāt  aparokṣāt  brahma ya ātmā sarva antaraḥ iti yasmāt  evam nityaḥ  avikriyaḥ  ca ātmā tasmāt  yudhyasva yuddhāt  uparamam mā kārṣīḥ iti  arthaḥ na hi  atra yuddha kartavyatā vidhīyate yuddhe pravṛtta eva hi asau śoka moha pratibaddhaḥ tūṣṇīm āste atas  tasya pratibandha apanayana mātram bhagavatā kriyate tasmāt  yudhyasva iti anuvāda mātram na vidhiḥ śoka moha ādi saṃsāra kāraṇa nivṛtti artham gīta aśāstram na pravartakam iti  etasya arthasya sākṣi bhūte ṛcau ānināya bhagavān yad  tu manyase yuddhā bhīṣma āt ayaḥ  mayā hanyante aham eva teṣām hantā iti eṣā buddhiḥ  mṛṣā eva te katham ya enam prakṛtam dehinam vetti vijānāti hantāram hanana kriyāyāḥ kartāram ya ca enam anyaḥ  manyate hatam deha hananena hataḥ  aham iti hanana kriyāyāḥ karma bhūtam tau ubhau na vijānītaḥ na jñātavantau avivekena ātmānam hantā aham hataḥ  asmi  aham iti deha hananena ātmānam aham pratyaya viṣayam yau vijānītaḥ tau ātma svarūpa anabhijñau iti  arthaḥ yasmāt  na ayam atmā hanti na hanana kriyāyāḥ kartā bhavati na ca hanyate na ca karma bhavati iti  arthaḥ avikriyatvāt  katham avikriya ātmā iti dvitīyaḥ  mantraḥ na jāyate na utpadyate jani lakṣaṇā vastu vikriyā na ātmanaḥ  vidyate iti  arthaḥ tathā na mriyate vā vā śabdaḥ ca arthe na mriyate ca iti antyā vināśa lakṣaṇā vikriyā pratiṣidhyate kadācid  chabdaḥ sarva vikriyā pratiṣedhaiḥ saṃbadhyate na kadācid  jāyate na kadācid  mriyate iti  evam yasmāt  ayam ātmā bhūtvā bhavana kriyām anubhūya paścāt  abhavitā abhāvam gantā na bhūyas  punar  tasmāt  na mriyate yaḥ  hi bhūtvā na bhavitā sa mriyata iti  ucyate lokā vā śabdāt  na śabdāt  ca ayam ātmā abhūtvā vā bhavitā dehavat  na bhūyas  tasmāt  na jāyate yaḥ  hi abhūtvā bhavitā sa jāyata iti  ucyate na evam ātmā atas  na jāyate yasmāt  evam tasmāt  ajaḥ yasmāt  na mriyate tasmāt  nityaś ca yadi api ādi antayoḥ  vikriyayoḥ pratiṣedhe sarvā vikriyāḥ pratiṣiddhā bhavanti tathā api madhya bhāvinīnām vikriyāṇām sva śabdaiḥ  eva pratiṣedhaḥ kartavyaḥ  anuktānām api yauvana ādi samasta vikriyāṇām pratiṣedhaḥ  yathā syāt  iti  āha śāśvata iti  ādinā śāśvata iti apakṣaya lakṣaṇā vikriyā pratiṣidhyate śaśvat bhavaḥ śāśvataḥ na apakṣīyate sva rūpeṇa niravayava tvāt  na api guṇa kṣayeṇa apakṣayaḥ nirguṇa tvāt  apakṣaya viparītā api vṛddhi lakṣaṇā vikriyā pratiṣidhyate purāṇa iti yaḥ  hi avayava āgamena upacīyate sa vardhate abhinava iti ca ucyate ayam tu ātmā niravayava tvāt  purā api nava eva iti purāṇaḥ na vardhate iti  arthaḥ tathā na hanyate hantiḥ atra vipariṇāma arthe draṣṭavyaḥ  apunarukta tāyai na vipariṇamyate iti  arthaḥ hanyamāne vipariṇamyamāne api śarīrāḥ asmin mantre ṣaṣ bhāva vikārā laukika vastu vikriyā ātmani pratiṣidhyante sarva prakāra vikriyā rahita ātmā iti vākya arthaḥ yasmāt  evam tasmāt  ubhau tau na vijānītaḥ iti pūrveṇa mantreṇa asya saṃbandhaḥ ya enam vetti hantāram iti anena mantreṇa hanana kriyāyāḥ kartā karma ca na bhavati iti pratijñāya na jāyate iti  anena avikriya tvam hetum uktvā pratijñāta artham upasaṃharati veda vijānāti avināśinam antyabhāva vikāra rahitam nityam vipariṇāma rahitam yaḥ  veda iti saṃbandhaḥ enam pūrveṇa matreṇa ukta lakṣaṇam ajam janma rahitam avyayam apakṣaya rahitam katham kena prakāreṇa sa vidvān puruṣaḥ  adhikṛtaḥ hanti hanana kriyām karoti katham vā ghātayati hantāram prayojayati na kathaṃcid  kaṃcid  hanti na kathaṃcid  kaṃcid  ghātayati iti ubhayatra ākṣepaḥ eva arthaḥ praśna artha asaṃbhavāt  hetu arthasya ca avikriyatvasya tulya tvāt  viduṣaḥ sarva karma pratiṣedha eva prakaraṇa arthaḥ  abhipretaḥ  bhagavatā hanteḥ  tu ākṣepaḥ udāharaṇa artha tvena kathitaḥ viduṣaḥ kam karma asaṃbhave hetu viśeṣam paśyan karmāṇi  ākṣipati bhagavān katham sa puruṣaḥ iti nanu ukta eva ātmanaḥ  avikriya tvam sarva karma asaṃbhava kāraṇa viśeṣaḥ satyam uktaḥ na tu sa kāraṇa viśeṣaḥ anya tvāt  viduṣaḥ  avikriyād ātmanaḥ na hi avikriyam sthāṇum viditavataḥ karma na saṃbhavati iti ced  na viduṣaḥ ātma tvāt  na deha ādi saṃghātasya vidvattā atas  pāriśeṣyāt  asaṃhata ātmā vidvān avikriyaḥ iti tasya viduṣaḥ karma asaṃbhavāt  ākṣepaḥ  yuktaḥ katham sa puruṣaḥ iti yathā buddhi ādi  āhṛtasya śabda ādi arthasya avikriya eva san buddhi vṛtti aviveka vijñānena avidyayā upalabdhā ātmā kalpyate evam eva ātmānātma viveka jñānena buddhi vṛttyā vidyā asatya rūpayā eva paramārtha taḥ  avikriya eva ātmā vidvān ucyate viduṣaḥ karma asaṃbhava vacanāt  yāni karmāṇi śāstreṇa vidhīyante tāni aviduṣaḥ  vihitāni iti bhagavataḥ  niścayaḥ  avagamyate nanu vidyā api aviduṣa eva vidhīyate vidita vidyasya piṣṭa peṣaṇavat  vidyā vidhāna anarthakyāt tatra aviduṣaḥ karmāṇi vidhīyante na viduṣaḥ iti viśeṣaḥ  na upapadyate iti ced  na anuṣṭheyasya bhāva abhāva viśeṣa upapatteḥ agnihotra ādi vidhi artha jñāna uttara kālam agnihotra ādi karma aneka sādhana upasaṃhāra pūrvakam anuṣṭheyam kartā aham mama kartavyam iti  evam prakāra vijñānavataḥ  aviduṣaḥ yathā anuṣṭheyam bhavati na tu tathā na jāyate iti  ādy ātma svarupa vidhi artha jñāna uttara kāla bhāvi kiṃcid  anuṣṭheyam bhavati kintu na aham kartā na aham bhoktā iti  ādy ātma ekatva ākartṛtva ādi viṣaya jñānāt na anyat  utpadyate iti eṣa viśeṣa upapadyate yaḥ punar  kartā aham iti vetti ātmānam tasya mama idam kartavyam iti avaśyaṃbhāvinī buddhiḥ syāt  tad apekṣayā saḥ  adhikriyate iti tam prati karmāṇi saṃbhavanti sa ca avidvān ubhau tau na vijānītaḥ iti vacanāt  viśeṣitasya ca viduṣaḥ karma ākṣepa vacanāt  katham sa puruṣaḥ iti tasmāt  viśeṣitasya avikriyā ātma darśinaḥ viduṣaḥ mumukṣaḥ  ca sarva karma saṃnyāse eva adhikāraḥ ata eva bhagavān nārāyaṇaḥ sāṃkhyān viduṣaḥ  aviduṣa ca karmiṇaḥ pravibhajya dve niṣṭhe grāha yati jñāna yogena sāṃkhyānām karma yogena yoginām iti tathā ca putrāya āha bhagavān vyāsaḥ dvau   imau   atha panthānau iti  ādi tathā ca kriyā pathaḥ  ca eva purastāt  paścāt  saṃnyāsaḥ  ca iti etam eva vibhāgam punar  punar  darśayiṣyati bhagavān atattva vid  ahaṃkāra vimūḍha ātmā kartā aham iti manyate tattva vid  tu na aham karomi iti tathā ca sarva karmāṇi manasā saṃnyasya āste ityādi tatra kecid  paṇḍitaṃmanyā vadanti janma ādi ṣaṣ bhāva vikriyā rahitaḥ  avikriyaḥ  akartā ekaḥ  aham ātmā iti na kasyacid  jñānam utpadyate yasmin sati sarva karma saṃnyāsaḥ upadiśyate iti tad  na na jāyate ityādi śāstra upadeśa anarthakya prasaṅgāt yathā ca śāstra upadeśa sāmarthyāt  dharma adharma astitva vijñānam kartuḥ  ca deha antara saṃbandha vijñānam utpadyate tathā śāstrāt  tasya eva ātmanaḥ  avikriyatva ākartṛtva ekatva ādi vijñānam kasmāt  na utpadyate iti praṣṭavyāḥ te karaṇa agocara tvāt iti ced  na manasā eva anudraṣṭavyam iti śruteḥ śāstra ācārya upadeśa śama dama ādi saṃskṛtam mana ātma darśane karaṇam tathā ca tad  adhigamāya anumāne āgame ca sati jñānam na utpadyata iti sāhasa mātram etad  jñānam ca utpadyamānam tad viparītam ajñānam avaśyam bādhate iti  abhyupagantavyam tad  ca ajñānam darśitam hantā aham hataḥ  asmi iti ubhau tau na vijānīta iti atra ca ātmanaḥ hanana kriyāyāḥ kartṛ tvam karma tvam hetu kartṛ tvam ca ajñāna kṛtam darśitam tad  ca sarva kriyāsu  api samānam kartṛtva ādeḥ avidyā kṛta tvam avikriyatvāt  ātmanaḥ vikriyāvān hi kartā ātmanaḥ karma bhūtam anyam prayojayati kuru iti tad  etad  aviśeṣeṇa viduṣaḥ sarva kriyāsu kartṛ tvam hetu kartṛ tvam ca pratiṣedhati bhagavān vāsudevaḥ  viduṣaḥ karma adhikāra abhāva pradarśana artham veda avināśinam katham sa puruṣaḥ iti  ādinā kva punar  viduṣaḥ  adhikāra iti etad  uktam pūrvam eva jñāna yogena sāṃkhyānām iti tathā ca sarva karma saṃnyāsam vakṣyati sarva karmāṇi manasā iti  ādinā nanu manasā iti vacanāt  na vācikānām kāyikānā ca saṃnyāsaḥ iti ced  na sarva karmāṇi iti viśeṣita tvāt  mānasānām eva sarva karmaṇām iti ced  na manaḥ vyāpāra pūrvaka tvāt  vāc kāya vyāpārāṇām manaḥ vyāpāra abhāve tad anupapatteḥ śāstrīyāṇām vākkāya karmaṇām kāraṇāni mānasāni karmāṇi varjayitvā anyāni sarva karmāṇi manasā saṃnyasya īt  iti ced  na na eva kurvan na kārayan iti viśeṣaṇāt  sarva karma saṃnyāsaḥ  ayam bhagavatā uktaḥ mariṣyataḥ  na jīvata iti ced  na nava dvāre pure dehī āste iti viśeṇa anupapatteḥ na hi sarva karma saṃnyāsena mṛtasya tad dehe āsanam saṃbhavati akurvataḥ  akārayata ca dehe saṃnyasya iti saṃbandhaḥ  na dehe āste iti ced  na sarvatra ātmanaḥ  avikriyatva avadhāraṇāt āsana kriyāyāḥ  ca adhikaraṇa apekṣa tvāt tad anapekṣa tvāt  ca saṃnyāsasya saṃpūrvas tu nyāsa śabdaḥ  atra tyāga arthaḥ na nikṣepa arthaḥ tasmāt  gīta aśāstre ātma jñānavataḥ saṃnyāsa eva adhikāraḥ  na karmaṇi iti tatra tatra upariṣṭāt  ātma jñāna prakaraṇe darśayiṣyāmaḥ prakṛtam tu vakṣyāmaḥ tatra ātmanaḥ  avināśi tvam pratijñātam tad  kim iva iti ucyate vāsāṃsi vastrāṇi jīrṇāni durbala tām gatāni yathā loke vihāya parityajya navāni abhinavāni gṛhṇāti upādatte naraḥ puruṣaḥ  aparāṇi anyāni tathā tadvat  eva śarīrāṇi vihāya jīrṇāni anyāni saṃyāti saṃgacchati navāni dehī ātmā puruṣavat  avikriya eva iti  arthaḥ kasmāt  avikriya eva iti āha enam prakṛtam dehinam na chindanti śastrāṇi niravayava tvāt  na avayava vibhāgam kurvanti śastrāṇi asya ādīni tathā na enam dahati pāvakaḥ agniḥ  api na bhasmīkaroti tathā na ca enam kledayanti āpaḥ apām hi sāvayavasya vastuna ādrībhāva karaṇena avayava viśleṣa āpādane sāmarthyam tad  na niravayave ātmani saṃbhavati tathā snehavat  dravyam sneha śoṣaṇena nāśayati vāyuḥ enam tu  ātmānam na śoṣayati mārutaḥ  api yata evam tasmāt  yasmāt  anyonya nāśa hetu bhūtāni enam ātmānam nāśayitum na utsahante asya ādīni tasmāt  nityaḥ nitya tvāt  sarva gataḥ sarva gata tvāt sthāṇuḥ  iva sthira iti  etad  sthira tvāt  acalaḥ  ayam ātmā atas  sanātanaḥ  cirantanaḥ na kāraṇāt  kutaścin niṣpannaḥ abhinava iti  arthaḥ na eteṣām lokānām paunaruktyam codanīyam yatas  ekena eva lokān ātmanaḥ nitya tvam avikriya tvam ca uktam na jāyate mriyate vā iti  ādinā tatra yad  eva ātma viṣayam kiṃcid  ucyate tad  etasmāt  loka arthān na atiricyate kiṃcid  chabdataḥ punaruktam kiṃcid  arthataḥ iti durbodha tvāt  ātma vastunaḥ punar  punar  prasaṅgam āpādya śabda antareṇa tad  eva vastu nirūpayati bhagavān vāsudevaḥ katham nu nāma saṃsāriṇām asaṃsāritva buddhi gocara tām āpannam sat  avyaktam tattvam saṃsāra nivṛttaye syāt  iti kim ca avyaktaḥ sarva karaṇa aviṣaya tvāt na vyajyata iti avyaktaḥ  ayam ātmā ataeva acintyaḥ  ayam yad  dhi indriya gocara s tad  cintā viṣaya tvam āpadyate ayam tu  ātmā anindriya gocara tvāt  acintyaḥ ataeva avikāryaḥ yathā kṣīram dadhyā tañcana ādinā vikāri na tathā ayam ātmā niravayavatvāc cāvi kriyaḥ na hi niravayavam kiṃcid  vikriyā ātmakam dṛṣṭām avikriyatvāt  avikāryaḥ  ayam ātmā ucyate tasmāt  evam yathā ukta prakāreṇa enam ātmānam viditvā tvam na anuśocitum arhasi hanta aham eṣām mayā ete hanyanta iti ātmanaḥ  anitya tvam abhyupagamya idam ucyate atha ca iti abhyupagama arthaḥ enam prakṛtam ātmānam nitya jātam loka prasiddhayā praty aneka śarīra utpatti jātaḥ  jāta iti manyase tathā pratitad tad vināśam nityam vā manyase mṛtam mṛtaḥ  mṛta  iti tathā api tathā abhāve api  ātmani tvam mahā bāhaḥ na evam śocitum arhasi janmavataḥ  na āśaḥ nāśavataḥ  janma ca iti  etau   avaśyaṃbhāvinā   iti tathā ca sati jātasya hi labdhajanmanaḥ dhruvaḥ  avyabhicārī mṛtyuḥ  maraṇam dhruva janma mṛtasya ca tasmāt  aparihāryaḥ  ayam janma maraṇa lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ tasmin   aparihārye arthe na tvam śocitum arhasi kārya karaṇa saṃghāta ātmakāni api bhūtāni  uddiśya śokaḥ  na yuktaḥ kartum yatas  avyakta ādīni  avyaktam adarśanam anupalabdhiḥ ādiḥ  yeṣām bhūtānām putra mitra ādi kārya karaṇa saṃghāta ātmakānām tāni avyakta dīni bhūtāni prāk utpatteḥ utpannāni ca prāc maraṇāt  vyakta madhyāni avyakta nidhanāni  eva punar  avyaktam adarśanam nidhanam maraṇam yeṣām tāni avyakta nidhanāni maraṇāt  ūrdhvam api  avyakta tām eva pratipadyante iti  arthaḥ tathā ca uktam adarśanāt  āpatitaḥ punar  ca adarśanam gataḥ na asau tava na tasya tvam vṛthā kā paridevanā iti tatra kā paridevanā kaḥ  vā pralāpaḥ  adṛṣṭa dṛṣṭa pranaṣṭa bhrānti bhūteṣu bhūteṣu  iti  arthaḥ durvijñeyaḥ  atham prakṛta ātmā kim tvām eva ekam upālabhe sādhāraṇe bhrānti nimitte katham durvijñeyaḥ  ayam ātmā iti ata āha āścaryavat  āścaryam adṛṣṭa pūrvam adbhutam akasmāt  dṛśyamānam tena tulyam āścaryavat  āścaryam iva enam ātmānam paśyati kaścid  āścaryavat  enam vadati tathā eva ca anyaḥ āścarya vac ca enam anyaḥ sṛṇoti śrutvā dṛṣṭvā uktvā api enam ātmānam veda na ca eva kaścid  athavā yaḥ  ayam ātmānam paśyati sa āścarya tulyaḥ yaḥ  vadati ya ca sṛṇoti saḥ  aneka sahasreṣu kaścid  eva bhavati atas  durbodha ātmā iti  abhiprāyaḥ atha idānīm prakaraṇa artham upasaṃharan brūte dehī śarīrī nityam sarvadā sarva avasthāsu avadhyaḥ niravayava tvān nitya tvāt  ca tatra avadhyaḥ  ayam dehe śarīre sarvasya sarva gata tvāt sthāvara ādiṣu sthitaḥ  api sarvasya prāṇi jātasya dehe vadhyamāne api  ayam dehī na vadhyaḥ  yasmāt  tasmāt  bhīṣma ādīni sarvāṇi bhūtāni uddiśya na tvam śocitum arhasi iha parama artha tattva apekṣāyām śokaḥ  mohaḥ  vā na saṃbhavati iti  uktam na kevalam parama artha tattva apekṣāyām eva kim tu svadharmam api svar  dharmaḥ kṣatriyasya yuddham tam api avekṣya tvam na vikampitum pracalitum na arhasi kṣatriyasya svābhāvikād dharmāt  ātma svābhāvyāt  iti  abhiprāyaḥ tad  ca yuddham pṛthivī jaya dvāreṇa dharma artham prajā rakṣaṇa artham ca iti dharmāt  anapetam param dharmyam tasmāt  dharmyāt  yuddhāt  chreyaḥ  anyat  kṣatriyasya na vidyate hi yasmāt  kutas  ca tad  yuddham kartavyam iti ucyate yadṛcchayā ca aprārthita tayā upapannam āgatam svarga dvāram apāvṛtam udghāṭitam ya etad  īdṛśam yuddham labhante kṣatriyāḥ he pārtha kim na sukhinas te etam kartavya tā prāptam api atha ced  tvam imam dharmyam dharmāt  anapetam vihitam saṃgrāmam yuddham na kariṣyasi ced  tatas  tad akaraṇāt svadharmam kīrtim ca mahādeva ādi samāgama nimittām hitvā kevalam pāpam avāpsyasi na kevalam svadharma kīrti parityāgaḥ akīrtim ca api yuddhā bhūtāni kathayiṣyanti te tava avyayām dīrgha kālām dharma ātmā śūra iti  evam ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ saṃbhāvitasya ca akīrtiḥ maraṇāt  atiricyate saṃbhāvitasya ca akīrteḥ varam maraṇam iti  arthaḥ kim ca bhayāt  karṇa ādibhyaḥ raṇāt  yuddhāt  uparatam nivṛttam maṃsyante cintayiṣyanti na kṛpayā iti tvām mahā rathāḥ duryodhana prabhṛtayaḥ yeṣām ca tvam duryodhana ādīnām bahu mataḥ  bahubhiḥ  guṇaiḥ  yuktaḥ iti  evam mataḥ bahu mataḥ  bhūtvā punar  yāsyasi lāghavam laghu bhāvam kim ca avācya vādān avaktavyavādān   ca bahūn aneka prakārān vadiṣyanti tava ahitāḥ śatravaḥ nindantaḥ kutsayantaḥ tava tvadīyam sāmarthyam nivāta kavaca ādi yuddha nimittam tatas  tasmāt  nindā prāpteḥ  duḥkhāt  duḥkhataram nu kim tatas  kaṣṭataram duḥkham na asti iti  arthaḥ yurā punar  kriyamāṇe karṇa ādibhiḥ hataḥ  vā prāpsyasi svargam hataḥ san svargam prāpsyasi jitvā vā karṇa ādīn śūrān bhokṣyase mahīm ubhayathā api tava lābha eva iti  abhiprāyaḥ yata evam tasmāt  uttiṣṭha kaunteya yuddhāya kṛtāni ca yaḥ jeṣyāmi śatrūn mariṣyāmi vā iti niścayam kṛtvā iti  arthaḥ tatra yuddham svadharma iti  evam yudhyamānasya upadeśam imam sṛṇu sukha duḥkhe same tulye kṛtvā rāga dveṣau   api  akṛtvā iti  etad  tathā lābha alābhau jaya ajayau ca samau kṛtvā tatas  yuddhāya yujyasva ghaṭāsva na evam yuddham kurvan pāpam avāpsyasi iti  eṣa upadeśaḥ prāsaṅgikaḥ śoka moha apanayanāya laukikaḥ  nyāyaḥ svadharmam api ca avekṣya iti  ādyaiḥ lokaiḥ  uktaḥ na tu tātparyeṇa parama artha darśanam iha prakṛtam tad  ca uktam upasaṃhriyate eṣā te abhihitā iti śāstra viṣaya vibhāga pradarśanāya iha hi pradarśite punar  śāstra viṣaya vibhāge upariṣṭāt  jñāna yogena sāṃkhyānām karma yogena yoginām iti niṣṭhā dvaya viṣayam śāstram sukham pravartiṣyate śrotāraḥ  ca viṣaya vibhāgena sukham grahīṣyanti iti  ata āha eṣā te tubhyam abhihitā uktā sāṃkhye parama artha vastu viveka viṣaye buddhiḥ  jñānam sākṣāt  śoka moha ādi saṃsāra hetu doṣa nivṛtti kāraṇam yoge tu tad prāpti upāye niḥsaṅga tayā dvandva prahāṇa pūrvakam īśvara ārādhana arthe karma yoge karma anuṣṭhāne samādhi yoge ca imām anantaram eva ucyamānām buddhim śṛṇu tām ca buddhim stauti prarocana artham buddhyā yayā yoga viṣayayā yuktaḥ he pārtha karma bandham karma eva dharma adharma ākhyaḥ  bandhaḥ karma bandha s tam prahāsyasi īśvara prasāda nimitta jñāna prāpteḥ  iti  abhiprāyaḥ kim ca anyat  na iha mokṣa mārge karma yoge abhikrama nāśaḥ abhikramaṇam abhikramaḥ prārambhaḥ  tasya na āśaḥ na asti yathā kṛṣi ādeḥ yoga viṣaye prārambhasya na anaikāntika phala tvam iti  arthaḥ kim ca na api cikitsāvat  pratyavāyaḥ  vidyate bhavati kim tu su alpam api asya dharmasya yoga dharmasya anuṣṭhitam trāyate rakṣati mahataḥ bhayāt  saṃsāra bhayāt  janma maraṇa ādi lakṣaṇāt yā iyam sāṃkhye buddhiḥ  uktā yoge ca vakṣyamāṇa lakṣaṇā sā vyavasāya ātmikā niścaya svabhāvā ekā eva buddhiḥ  itara viparīta buddhi śākhā bhedasya vā adhikā samyak pramāṇa janita tvāt  iha śreyaḥ mārge he kuru nandana   yāḥ punar  itarā viparīta buddhayaḥ yāsām śākhā bheda pracāra vaśāt  anantaḥ  apāraḥ  anuparataḥ saṃsāraḥ  nitya pratatas  vistīrṇaḥ  bhavati pramāṇa janita viveka buddhi nimitta vaśāt  ca uparatāsu  ananta bheda buddhiṣu saṃsāraḥ  api  uparamate tā buddhayaḥ  bahu śākhāḥ bahu vayaḥ śākhāḥ yāsām tāḥ bahu śākhāḥ bahu bhedā iti  etad  pratiśākhā bhedena hi  anantā ca buddhayaḥ keṣām avyavasāyinām pramāṇa janita viveka buddhi rahitānām iti  arthaḥ yām imām vakṣyamāṇām puṣpitām puṣpita iva vṛkṣaḥ śobhamānām śrūyamāṇa ramaṇīyām vācam vākya lakṣaṇām pravadanti ke avipaścitaḥ  amedhasaḥ  avivekina iti  arthaḥ veda vāda ratāḥ bahvi artha vāda phala sādhana prakāśakeṣu veda vākyeṣu ratāḥ he pārtha na anyat  svarga prāpti ādi phala sādhanebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ  asti iti  evam vādinaḥ vadana śīlāḥ te ca kāma ātmānaḥ kāma svabhāvāḥ kāma parā iti  arthaḥ svarga parāḥ svargaḥ paraḥ puruṣa arthaḥ yeṣām te svarga parāḥ svarga pradhānāḥ janma karma phala pradām karmaṇaḥ phalam karma phalam janma eva karma phalam janma karma phalam tad  pradadāti iti janma karma phala pradā tām vācam pravadanti iti  anuṣajyate kriyā viśeṣa bahulām kriyāṇām viśeṣāḥ kriyā viśeṣāḥ te bahulā yasyām vāci tām svarga paśu putra ādi arthāḥ yayā vācā bāhulyena prakāśyante bhoga aiśvarya gatim prati bhogaḥ  ca aiśvaryam ca bhoga aiśvarye tayoḥ  gatiḥ prāptiḥ bhoga aiśvarya gatiḥ tām prati sādhana bhūtāḥ ye kriyā viśeṣāḥ tad bahulān tām vācam pravadantaḥ mūḍhāḥ saṃsāre parivartante iti  abhiprāyaḥ teṣām ca bhoga aiśvarya prasaktānām bhogaḥ kartavyaḥ ca aiśvaryam ca iti bhoga aiśvaryayoḥ  eva praṇayavatām tad ātma bhūtānām tayā kriyā viśeṣa bahulayā vācā apahṛta cetasām ācchādita viveka prajñānām vyavasāya ātmikā sāṃkhye yoge vā buddhiḥ samādhau samādhīyate asmin puruṣa upabhogāya sarvam iti samādhiḥ antaḥkaraṇam buddhiḥ tasmin samādhau na vidhīyate na bhavati iti  arthaḥ ya evam viveka buddhi rahitāḥ teṣām kāma ātmanām yad  phalam tad  āha traiguṇya viṣayāḥ traiguṇyam saṃsāraḥ  viṣayaḥ prakāśayitavyaḥ yeṣām te vedāḥ traiguṇya viṣayāḥ tvam tu nistraiguṇyaḥ  bhava arjuna niṣkāmaḥ  bhava iti  arthaḥ nirdvandvaḥ sukha duḥkha hetū sa pratipakṣau padārthau dvandva śabda vācyau tatas  nirgataḥ nirdvandvaḥ  bhava nitya sattva sthaḥ sadā sattva guṇa āśritaḥ  bhava tathā niryogakṣemaḥ  anupāttasya upādānam yogaḥ upāttasya rakṣaṇam kṣemaḥ yogakṣema pradhānasya śreyasi pravṛttiḥ  duṣkarā iti  atas  niryogakṣemaḥ  bhava ātmavān apramatta ś ca bhava eṣa tava upadeśaḥ svadharmam anutiṣṭhataḥ sarveṣu veda ukteṣu karmasu yāni  uktāni  anantāni phalāni tāni na apekṣyante ced  kim artham tāni īśvarāya iti  anuṣṭhīyante iti  ucyate sṛṇu yathā loke kūpa taḍāga ādi anekasmin udapāne paricchinna udake yāvān yāvat parimāṇaḥ snāna pāna ādiḥ  arthaḥ phalam prayojanam sa sarvaḥ  arthaḥ sarvatas  saṃpluta udake api yaḥ  arthaḥ tāvān eva saṃpadyate tatra antarbhavati iti  arthaḥ evam tāvān tāvat parimāṇa  eva saṃpadyate sarveṣu vedeṣu veda ukteṣu karmasu yaḥ  arthaḥ yad  karma phalam saḥ  arthaḥ brāhmaṇasya saṃnyāsinaḥ parama artha tattvam vijānataḥ yaḥ  arthaḥ yad  vijñāna phalam sarvatas  saṃpluta udaka sthānīyam tasmin tāvān eva saṃpadyate tatra eva antarbhavati iti  arthaḥ yathā kṛtāya vijitāya adhareyāḥ saṃyanti  evam enam sarvam tad  abhisameti yad  kiṃcid  prajāḥ sādhu kurvanti yaḥ  tad  veda yad  sa veda iti śruteḥ sarvam karma akhilam iti ca vakṣyati tasmāt  prāk  jñāna niṣṭha adhikāra prāpteḥ karmaṇi  adhikṛtena kūpa taḍāga ādi artha sthānīyam api karma kartavyam tava ca karmaṇi  eva adhikāraḥ  na jñāna niṣṭhāyām te tava tatra ca karma kurvataḥ mā phaleṣu adhikāraḥ  astu karma phala tṛṣṇā mā bhūt  kadācana kasyāṃcid  api  avasthāyām iti  arthaḥ yadā karma phale tṛṣṇā te syāt  tadā karma phala prāpteḥ  hetuḥ syāḥ evam mā karma phala hetuḥ bhūḥ yadā hi karma phala tṛṣṇā prayuktaḥ karmaṇi pravartate tadā karma phalasya eva janmanaḥ  hetuḥ  bhavet  yadi karma phalam na iṣyate kim karmaṇā duḥkha rūpeṇa iti mā te tava saṅgaḥ  astu  akarmaṇi akaraṇe prītiḥ  mā bhūt  yadi karma phala prayuktena na kartavyam karma katham tarhi kartavyam iti ucyate yoga sthaḥ san kuru karmāṇi kevalam īśvara artham tatra api īśvaraḥ  me tuṣyatu iti saṅgam tyaktvā dhanaṃjaya phala tṛṣṇā śūnyena kriyamāṇe karmaṇi sattva śuddhi jā jñāna prāpti lakṣaṇā siddhiḥ tad viparyaya jā asiddhiḥ tayoḥ siddhi asiddhyoḥ  api samaḥ tulyaḥ  bhūtvā kuru karmāṇi kaḥ  asau yogaḥ  yatrasthaḥ kuru iti  uktam idam eva tad  dūreṇa ati vipra karṣeṇa atyantam eva hi  avaram adhamam nikṛṣṭam karma phala arthinā kriyamāṇam buddhi yogāt  samatva buddhi yuktāt  karmaṇaḥ janma maraṇa ādi hetu tvāt he dhanaṃjaya yata evam tatas  yoga viṣayāyām buddhau tad paripāka jāyām vā sāṃkhya buddhau śaraṇam āśrayam abhaya prāpti kāraṇam anviccha prārthayasva parama artha jñāna śaraṇaḥ  bhava iti  arthaḥ yatas  avaram karma kurvāṇāḥ kṛpaṇāḥ dīnāḥ phala hetavaḥ phala tṛṣṇā prayuktāḥ santaḥ yaḥ  vā etad  akṣaram gārgy aviditvā asmāl lokāt  praiti sa kṛpaṇaḥ iti śruteḥ samatva buddhi yuktaḥ san svadharmam anutiṣṭhan yad  phalam prāpnoti tad  śṛṇu buddhi yuktaḥ karma samatva viṣayayā buddhyā yuktaḥ  buddhi yuktaḥ saḥ jahāti parityajati iha asmin loke ubhe sukṛta duṣkṛte puṇya pāpe sattva śuddhi jñāna prāpti dvāreṇa yatas  tasmāt  samatva buddhi yogāya yujyasva ghaṭāsva yogaḥ  hi karmasu kauśalam svadharma ākhyeṣu karmasu vartamānasya yā siddhi asiddhyoḥ samatva buddhiḥ  īśvara arpita cetaḥ tayā tad  kauśalam kuśala bhāvaḥ tad  dhi kauśalam yad  bandhana svabhāvāni  api karmāṇi samatva buddhyā svabhāvān nivartante tasmāt  samatva buddhi yuktaḥ  bhava tvam karma jam phalam tyaktvā iti vyavahitena sambandhaḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa deha prāptiḥ karma jam phalam karmabhyaḥ  jātam buddhi yuktāḥ samatva buddhi yuktāḥ santaḥ hi yasmāt  phalam tyaktvā parityajya manīṣiṇaḥ jñāninaḥ  bhūtvā janma bandha vinirmuktāḥ janma eva bandhaḥ janma bandhaḥ tena vinirmuktāḥ jīvanta eva janma bandhāt  vinirmuktāḥ santaḥ padam paramam viṣṇoḥ mokṣa ākhyam gacchanti anāmayam sarva upadrava rahitam iti  arthaḥ athavā buddhi yogāt  dhanaṃjaya iti  ārabhya parama artha darśana lakṣaṇā eva sarvatas  saṃpluta udaka sthānīyā karma yoga ja sattva śuddha janitā buddhiḥ  darśitā sākṣāt sukṛta duṣkṛta prahāṇa ādi hetutva śravaṇāt yadā yasmin kāle te tava moha kalilam moha ātmakam aviveka rūpam kāluṣyam yena ātmā anātma viveka bodham kaluṣīkṛtya viṣayam pratyantaḥkaraṇam pravartate tad  tava buddhiḥ vyatitariṣyati vyatikramiṣyati ati śuddha bhāvam āpātryate iti  arthaḥ tadā tasmin kāle gantāsi prāpsyasi nirvedam vairāgyam śrotavyasya śrutasya ca tadā śrotavyam śrutam ca te niṣphalam pratibhāti iti  abhiprāyaḥ moha kalila atyaya dvāreṇa labdha ātma viveka ja prajñaḥ kadā karma yoga jam phalam parama artha yogam avāpsyāmi iti ced  tad  sṛṇu śruti vipratinnā aneka sādhya sādhana saṃbandha prakāśana śrutibhiḥ śravaṇaiḥ pravṛtti nivṛtti lakṣaṇaiḥ vipratipannā nānā pratinnā vikṣiptā satī te tava buddhiḥ  yadā yasmin kāle sthāsyati sthirībhūtā bhaviṣyati niścalā vikṣepa calana varjitā satī samādhau samādhīyate cittam asmin   iti samādhiḥ  ātmā tasmin ātmani iti  etad  acalā tatra api vikalpa varjitā iti  etad  buddhiḥ  antaḥkaraṇam tadā tasmin kāle yogam avāpsyasi viveka prajñām samādhim prāpsyasi praśna bījam pratilabhya arjuna uvāca labdha samādhi prajñasya lakṣaṇa bubhutsayā arjuna uvāca arjuna uvāca sthitā pratiṣṭhitā aham asmi param brahma iti prajñā yasya saḥ sthita prajñas tasya sthita prajñasya kā bhāṣā kim bhāṣaṇam vacanam katham asau paraiḥ  bhāṣyate samādhi sthasya samādhau sthitasya he keśava sthita dhīḥ sthita prajñaḥ svayam vā kim prabhāṣeta kim āsīta vrajeta kim āsanam vrajanam vā tasya katham iti  arthaḥ sthita prajñasya lakṣaṇam anena lokena pṛcchayate yaḥ  hi  ādita eva saṃnyasya karmāṇi jñāna yoga niṣṭhāyām pravṛttaḥ yaḥ  ca karma yogena tayoḥ prajahāti iti  ārabhya ā adhyāya parisamāpteḥ sthita prajña lakṣaṇam sādhanam ca upadiśyate sarvatra eva hi adhyātma śāstre kṛtārtha lakṣaṇāni yāni tāni  eva sādhanāni upadiśyante yatna sādhya tvāt  yāni yatna sādhyāni sādhanāni lakṣaṇāni ca bhavanti tāni śrī bhagavān uvāca prajahāti prakarṣeṇa jahāti parityajati yadā yasmin kāle sarvān samastān kāmān icchā bhedān he pārtha manaḥ gatān manasi praviṣṭāan hṛdi praviṣṭān sarva kāma parityāge tuṣṭi kāraṇa abhāvāt śarīra dhāraṇa nimitta śeṣe ca sati unmatta pramattasya iva pravṛttiḥ prāptā iti  ata ucyate ātmani  eva pratyagātma svarūpe eva ātmanā svena eva bāhya lābha nirapekṣas tuṣṭāḥ parama artha darśana amṛta rasa lābhena anyasmāt  alaṃpratyayavān sthita prajñaḥ sthitā pratiṣṭhitā ātmā anātma viveka jā prajñā yasya saḥ sthita prajñaḥ vidvān tadā ucyate tyakta putra vitta loka eṣaṇaḥ saṃnyāsī ātma ārāma ātma krīḍāḥ sthita prajña iti  arthaḥ kim ca duḥkheṣu  ādhyātmika ādiṣu prāpteṣu na udvignam na prakṣubhitam duḥkha prāptau manaḥ  yasya saḥ  ayam anudvigna manāḥ tathā sukheṣu prāpteṣu vigatā spṛhā tṛṣṇā yasya na agniḥ  iva indhana ādi ādhāne sukhāni  anu vivardhate sa vigata spṛhaḥ vīta rāga bhaya krodhaḥ rāga ca bhayam ca krodha ca vītā vigatā yasmāt  sa vīta rāga bhaya krodhaḥ sthita dhīḥ sthita prajñaḥ  muniḥ saṃnyāsī tadā ucyate kim ca yaḥ muniḥ sarvatra deha jīvita ādiṣu  api anabhisnehaḥ  abhisneha varjitaḥ  tad  tad  prāpya śubha aśubham tad  tad  śubham aśubham vā labdhvā na abhinandati na dveṣṭi śubham prāpya na tuṣyati na hṛṣyati aśubham ca prāpya na dveṣṭi iti  arthaḥ tasya evam harṣa viṣāda varjitasya viveka jā prajñā pratiṣṭhitā bhavati kim ca yadā saṃharate samyak  upasaṃharate ca ayam jñāna niṣṭhāyām pravṛttaḥ  yatiḥ kūrmaḥ  aṅgāni iva yathā kūrmaḥ  bhayāt  svāni  aṅgāni upasaṃharati sarvaśas  sarvatas  evam jñāna niṣṭhaḥ indriyāṇi indriya arthebhyaḥ sarva viṣayebhyaḥ  upasaṃharate tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā iti  ukta artham vākyam tatra viṣayān anāharataḥ āturasya api indriyāṇi kūrma aṅgāni iva saṃhriyante na tu tad viṣayaḥ  rāgaḥ sa katham saṃhriyate iti  ucyate yadi api viṣayāḥ viṣaya upalakṣitāni viṣaya śabda vācyāni indriyāṇi nirāhārasya anāhriyamāṇa viṣayasya kaṣṭe tapasi sthitasya mūrkhasya api vinivartante dehinaḥ  dehavataḥ rasa varjam rasaḥ  rāgaḥ  viṣayeṣu yaḥ  tam varjayitvā rasa śabdaḥ  rāge prasiddhaḥ svarasena pravṛttaḥ rasikaḥ rasa jñaḥ iti  ādi darśanāt  saḥ  api rasaḥ  rañjana rūpaḥ sūkṣmaḥ  asya yateḥ param parama artha tattvam brahma dṛṣṭvā upalabhya aham eva tad  iti vartamānasya nivartate nirbījam viṣaya vijñānam saṃpadyate iti  arthaḥ na asati samyak darśane rasasya ucchedaḥ tasmāt  samyak darśana ātmikāyāḥ prajñāyāḥ sthairyam kartavyam iti  abhiprāyaḥ samyak darśana lakṣaṇa prajñā sthairyam cikīrṣatā ādau indriyāṇi sva vaśe sthāpayitavyāni yasmāt  tad anavasthāpane doṣam āha yatatas prayatnam kurvataḥ hi yasmāt  kaunteya puruṣasya vipaścitaḥ medhāvinaḥ  api iti vyavahitena saṃbandhaḥ indriyāṇi pramāthīni pramathana śīlāni viṣaya abhimukham hi puruṣam vikṣobhayanti ākulīkurvanti ākulīkṛtya ca haranti prasabham prasahya prakāśam eva paśyataḥ  viveka vijñāna yuktam manaḥ yatas  tasmāt  tāni sarvāṇi saṃyamya saṃyamanam vaśīkaraṇam kṛtvā yuktaḥ samāhitaḥ san āsīta mad paraḥ  aham vāsudevaḥ sarva pratyagātmā paraḥ  yasya sa mad paraḥ na anyaḥ  aham tasmāt  iti  āsīta iti  arthaḥ evam āsīnasya yateḥ  vaśe hi yasya indriyāṇi vartante abhyāsa balāt  tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā atha idānīm parābhaviṣyataḥ sarva an artha mūlam idam ucyate dhyāyataḥ  cintayataḥ  viṣayāt  śabda ādīn viṣaya viśeṣān ālocayataḥ puṃsaḥ puruṣasya saṅgaḥ āsaktiḥ prīti s teṣu viṣayeṣu upajāyate utpadyate saṅgāt  prīteḥ saṃjāyate samutpadyate kāma s tṛṣṇā kāmāt  kutaścid  pratihatāt  krodhaḥ  abhijāyate krodhāt  bhavati saṃmohaḥ  avivekaḥ kārya akārya viṣayaḥ kruddhaḥ  hi saṃmūḍhaḥ san gurum api  ākrośati saṃmohāt  smṛti vibhramaḥ śāstra ācārya upadeśa āhita saṃskāra janitāyāḥ smṛte syāt  vibhramaḥ  bhraṃśaḥ smṛti utpatti nimitta prāptau anutpattiḥ tatas  smṛti bhraṃśāt  buddhi nāśaḥ buddhi nāśaḥ kārya akārya viṣaya viveka ayogya tā antaḥkaraṇasya buddheḥ  nāśa ucyate buddheḥ  nāśāt praṇaśyati tāvat  eva hi puruṣaḥ yāvat  antaḥkaraṇam tadīyam kārya akārya viṣaya viveka yogyam tad ayogya tve naṣṭa eva puruṣaḥ  bhavati atas  tasya antaḥkaraṇasya buddheḥ  nāśāt praṇaśyati puruṣa artha ayogyaḥ  bhavati iti  arthaḥ sarva anarthasya mūlam uktam viṣaya abhidhyānam atha idānīm mokṣa kāraṇam idam ucyate rāga dveṣa viyuktai rāgaḥ  ca dveṣaḥ  ca rāga dveṣau tad puraḥsarā hi indriyāṇām pravṛttiḥ svābhāvikī tatra yaḥ  mumukṣuḥ bhavati saḥ tābhyām viyuktaiḥ śrotra ādibhiḥ  indriyaiḥ  viṣayān avarjanīyān caran upalabhamānaḥ ātma vaśyaiḥ  ātmanaḥ  vaśyāni vaśībhūtāni indriyāṇi taiḥ  ātma vaśyaiḥ  vidheya ātmā icchātaḥ vidheya ātmā antaḥkaraṇam yasya saḥ  ayam prasādam adhigacchati prasādaḥ prasanna tā svāsthyam prasāde sati kim syāt  iti  ucyate prasāde sarva duḥkhānām ādhyātmika ādīnām hāniḥ  vināśaḥ  asya yateḥ  upajāyate kim ca prasanna cetasaḥ svastha antaḥkaraṇasya hi yasmāt  āśu śīghram buddhiḥ paryavatiṣṭhate ākāśam iva pari samantāt  avatiṣṭhate ātma svarūpeṇa eva niścalībhavati iti  arthaḥ evam prasanna cetasaḥ  avasthita buddhiḥ kṛtakṛtya tā yatas  tasmāt  rāga dveṣa viyuktaiḥ  indriyaiḥ śāstra aviruddheṣu avarjanīyeṣu yuktaḥ samācaret  iti vākya arthaḥ sā iyam prasanna tā stūyate na asti na vidyate na bhavati iti  arthaḥ buddhiḥ ātma svarūpa viṣayā ayuktasya asamāhita antaḥkaraṇasya na ca asti ayuktasya bhāvanā ātma jñāna abhiniveśaḥ tathā na ca asti  abhāvayata ātma jñāna abhiniveśam akurvataḥ śāntiḥ  upaśamaḥ aśāntasya kutas  sukham indriyāṇām hi viṣaya sevā tṛṣṇātaḥ nivṛttiḥ  yā tad sukham na viṣaya viṣayā tṛṣṇā duḥkham eva hi sā na tṛṣṇāyām satyām sukhasya gandha mātram api  upapadyate iti  arthaḥ ayuktasya kasmāt  buddhiḥ  na asti iti  ucyate indriyāṇām hi yasmāt  caratām sva sva viṣayeṣu pravartamānānām yad  manaḥ  anuvidhīyate anupravartate tad  indriya viṣaya vikalpanena pravṛttam manaḥ  asya yateḥ harati prajñām ātmānātma viveka jām nāśayati katham vāyuḥ nāvam iva ambhasi udake jigamiṣatām mārgāt uddhṛtya unmārge yathā vāyuḥ nāvam pravartayati evam ātma viṣayām prajñām hṛtvā manaḥ  viṣaya viṣayām karoti yatatas  hi iti  upanyastasya arthasya anekadhā upapattim uktvā tam ca artham upapādya upasaṃharati indriyāṇām pravṛttau doṣa upapāditaḥ  yasmāt  tasmāt  yasya yateḥ he mahā bāhaḥ nigṛhītāni sarvaśas  sarva prakāraiḥ mānasa ādi bhedaiḥ indriyāṇi indriya arthebhyaḥ śabda ādibhyaḥ  tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā yaḥ  ayam laukikaḥ  vaidika ca vyavahāraḥ sa utpanna viveka jñānasya sthita prajñasya avidyā kārya tvāt avidyā nivṛttau nivartate avidyāyāḥ  ca vidyā virodhāt  nivṛttiḥ iti  etam artham sphuṭīkurvan   āha yā niśā rātriḥ sarva padārthānām aviveka karī tamaḥ svabhāva tvāt sarva bhūtānām sarveṣām bhūtānām kim tad  parama artha tattvam sthita prajñasya viṣayaḥ yathā naktaṃcarāṇām ahar eva sat  anyeṣām niśā bhavati tadvat  naktaṃcara sthānīyānām ajñānām sarva bhūtānām niśā iva niśā parama artha tattvam agocara tvāt  atad buddhīnām tasyām parama artha tattva lakṣaṇāyām ajñāna nidrāyāḥ prabuddhaḥ  jāgarti saṃyamī saṃyamavān jita indriyaḥ  yogī iti  arthaḥ yasyām grāhya grāhaka bheda lakṣaṇāyām avidyā niśāyām prasuptāni  eva bhūtāni jāgrati iti ucyante yasyām niśāyām prasuptā iva svapna dṛśaḥ sā niśā avidyā rūpa tvāt parama artha tattvam paśyataḥ  muneḥ atas  karmāṇi avidyā avasthāyām eva codyante na vidyā avasthāyām vidyāyām hi satyām udite savitari śārvaram iva tamaḥ praṇāśam upagacchati avidyā prāk  vidyā utpatteḥ avidyā pramāṇa buddhyā gṛhyamāṇā kriyā kāraka phala bheda rūpā satī sarva karma hetu tvam pratipadyate na apramāṇa buddhyā gṛhyamāṇāyāḥ karma hetutva upapattiḥ pramāṇa bhūtena vedena mama coditam kartavyam karma iti hi karmaṇi kartā pravartate na avidyā mātram idam sarvam bheda jātam iti jñānam tasya ātma jñasya sarva karma saṃnyāse eva adhikāraḥ  na pravṛttau tathā ca darśayiṣyati tad buddhayaḥ  tad ā ātmānaḥ iti  ādinā jñāna niṣṭhāyām eva tasya adhikāram tatra api pravartaka pramāṇa abhāve pravṛtti anupapattiḥ iti ced  na sva ātma viṣaya tvāt  ātma vijñānasya na hi  ātmanaḥ sva ātmani pravartaka pramāṇa apekṣatā ātma tvāt  eva tad antatvāt  ca sarva pramāṇānām pramāṇa tvasya na hi  ātma svarūpa adhigame sati punar  pramāṇa prameya vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati pramātṛ tvam hi  ātmanaḥ nivartayati antyam pramāṇam nivartayat  eva ca apramāṇībhavati svapna kāla pramāṇam iva prabodhe loke ca vastu adhigame pravṛtti hetutva adarśanāt  pramāṇasya tasmāt  na ātma vidaḥ karmaṇi  adhikāra iti siddham viduṣas tyakta eṣaṇasya sthita prajñasya yateḥ  eva mokṣa prāptiḥ na tu asaṃnyāsinaḥ kāma kāminaḥ iti  etam artham dṛṣṭāntena pratipādayiṣyan āha āpūryamāṇam adbhiḥ  acala pratiṣṭham acala tayā pratiṣṭhā avasthitiḥ yasya tam acala pratiṣṭham samudram āpaḥ sarvatas  gatāḥ praviśanti sva ātma stham avikriyam eva santam yadvat  tadvat  kāmāḥ viṣaya saṃnidhau   api sarvatas  icchā viśeṣāḥ yam puruṣam samudram iva āpaḥ avikurvantaḥ praviśanti sarve ātmani  eva pralīyante na sva ātma vaśam kurvanti sa śāntiḥ  mokṣam āpnoti na itaraḥ kāma kāmī kāmyanta iti kāmāḥ viṣayāḥ tān kāmayitum śīlam yasya saḥ kāma kāmī na eva prāpnoti iti  arthaḥ yasmāt  evam tasmāt  vihāya parityajya kāmān yaḥ saṃnyāsī pumān sarvān aśeṣatas  kārtsnyena carati jīvana mātra ceṣṭā śeṣaḥ paryaṭati iti  arthaḥ niḥspṛhaḥ śarīra jīvana mātre api nirgatā spṛhā yasya saḥ niḥspṛhaḥ san nirmamaḥ śarīra jīvana mātra ākṣipta parigrahe api mama idam iti  abhiniveśa varjitaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ vidyāvattva ādi nimitta ātma saṃbhāvanā rahitaḥ iti  etad  sa evaṃbhūtaḥ sthita prajñaḥ brahma vid  śāntim sarva saṃsāra duḥkha uparama lakṣaṇām nirvāṇa ākhyām adhigacchati prāpnoti brahma bhūtaḥ  bhavati iti  arthaḥ sā eṣā jñāna niṣṭhā stūyate eṣā yathā uktā brāhmī brahmaṇi bhavā iyam sthitiḥ sarvam karma saṃnyasya brahma rūpeṇa eva avasthānam iti  etad  he pārtha na enām sthitim prāpya labdhvā na vimuhyati na moham prāpnoti sthitvā asyām sthitau brāhmyām yathā uktāyām antakāle api antye vayasy api brahma nirvāṇam brahma nirvṛtim mokṣam ṛcchati gacchati kim u vaktavyam brahmacaryāt  eva saṃnyasya yāvat  jīvam yaḥ  brahmaṇi  eva avatiṣṭhate sa brahma nirvāṇam ṛcchati iti śāstrasya pravṛtti nivṛtti viṣaya bhūte dve buddhī bhagavatā nirdiṣṭe sāṅkhye buddhiḥ  yoge buddhiḥ  iti ca tatra prajahāti yadā kāmān iti  ārabhya ā adhyāya parisamāpteḥ sāṅkhya buddhi āśritānām saṃnyāsam kartavyam uktvā teṣām tad niṣṭhatayā eva ca kṛtārtha tā uktā eṣā brāhmī sthitiḥ iti arjunāya ca karmaṇi  eva adhikāra s te mā saṅgaḥ  astu  akarmaṇi iti karma eva kartavyam uktavān yoga buddhim āśritya na tatas  eva śreyaḥ prāptim uktavān tad  etad  ālakṣya paryākulībhūta buddhiḥ  arjuna uvāca katham bhaktāya śreyaḥ  arthine yad  sākṣāt  śreyaḥ sādhanam sāṅkhya buddhi niṣṭhām śrāvayitvā mām karmaṇi dṛṣṭa an ekānartha yukte pāramparyeṇa api anaikāntika śreyaḥ prāpti phale niyuñjyāt  iti yuktaḥ paryākulībhāvaḥ  arjunasya tad anurūpa praśnaḥ jyāyasī ced  iti  ādiḥ praśna apākaraṇa vākyam ca bhagavatā uktam yathā ukta vibhāga viṣaye śāstre kecid  tu arjunasya praśna artham anyathā kalpayitvā tad pratikūlam bhagavataḥ prativacanam varṇayanti yathā ca ātmanā sambandha granthe gīta arthaḥ  nirūpita s tad pratikūlam ca iha punar  praśna prativacanayoḥ  artham nirūpayanti katham tatra sambandha granthe tāvat  sarveṣām āśramiṇām jñāna karmaṇoḥ samuccayaḥ  gīta aśāstre nirūpitaḥ  artha  iti  uktam punar  viśeṣitam ca yāvat jīva śruti coditāni karmāṇi parityajya kevalāt  eva jñānān mokṣaḥ prāpyata iti  etad  ekāntena eva pratiṣiddham iti iha tu  āśrama vikalpam darśayatā yāvat jīva śruti coditānām eva karmaṇām parityāga uktaḥ tad  katham īdṛśam viruddham artham arjunāya brūyāt  bhagavān śrotā vā katham viruddham artham avadhārayet  tatra etad  syāt  gṛhasthānām eva śrauta karma parityāgena kevalāt  eva jñānān mokṣaḥ pratiṣidhyate na tu  āśrama antarāṇām iti etad  api pūrva uttarviruddham eva katham sarva āśramiṇām jñāna karmaṇoḥ samuccayaḥ  gīta aśāstre niścitaḥ  artha  iti pratijñāya iha katham tad viruddham kevalāt  eva jñānān mokṣam brūyāt  āśrama antarāṇām atha matam śrauta karma apekṣayā etad vacanam kevalāt  eva jñānāt  śrauta karma rahitāt  gṛhasthānām mokṣaḥ pratiṣidhyate iti tatra gṛhasthānām vidyamānam api smārtam karma avidyamānavat  upekṣya jñānāt  eva kevalān na mokṣa iti  ucyata iti etad  api viruddham katham gṛhasthasya eva smārta karmaṇā samuccitāt  jñānān mokṣaḥ pratiṣidhyate na tu āśrama antarāṇām iti katham vivekibhiḥ śakyam avadhārayitum kim ca yadi mokṣa sādhana tvena smārtāni karmāṇi ūrdhvaretasām samuccīyante tathā gṛhasthasya api iṣyatām smārtaiḥ  eva samuccayaḥ  na śrautaiḥ atha śrautaiḥ smārtaiḥ  ca gṛhasthasya eva samuccayaḥ  mokṣāya ūrdhvaretasām tu smārta karma mātra samuccitāj jñānān mokṣa iti tatra evam sati gṛhasthasya āyāsa bāhulyam śrautam smārtam ca bahu duḥkha rūpam karma śirasi aropitam syāt  atha gṛhasthasya eva āyāsa bāhulya kāraṇān mokṣaḥ syāt  na āśrama antarāṇām śrauta nitya karma rahita tvāt  iti tad  api  asat  sarva upaniṣatsu itihāsa purāṇa yoga śāstre ca jñāna aṅga tvena mumukṣoḥ sarva karma saṃnyāsa vidhānāt  āśrama vikalpa samuccaya vidhāna āt  ca śruti smṛtyoḥ siddha s tarhi sarva āśramiṇām jñāna karmaṇoḥ samuccayaḥ na mumukṣoḥ sarva karma saṃnyāsa vidhānāt vyutthāya atha bhikṣā caryam caranti tasmāt  saṃnyāsam eṣām tapasām atiriktam āhuḥ nyāsa eva atyarecayet iti na karmaṇā na prajayā dhanena tyāgena eke amṛta tvam ānaśuḥ iti ca brahmacaryāt  eva pravrajet  iti  ādyāḥ śrutayaḥ tyaja dharmam adharmam ca ubhe satya anṛte tyaja ubhe satya anṛte tyaktvā yena tyajasi tad  tyaja saṃsāram eva niḥsāram dṛṣṭvā sāra didṛkṣayā pravrajanti  akṛta udvāhāḥ param vairāgyam āśritāḥ iti bṛhaspatiḥ  api kacam prati karmaṇā badhyate jantuḥ  vidyayā ca vimucyate tasmāt  karma na kurvanti yatayaḥ pāra darśinaḥ iti śuka anuśāsanam iha api sarva karmāṇi manasā saṃnyasya iti  ādi mokṣasya ca akārya tvān mumukṣoḥ karma ānarthakyam nityāni pratyavāya parihāra artham anuṣṭheyāni iti ced  na asaṃnyāsi viṣaya tvāt pratyavāya prāpteḥ na hi agni kārya ādi akaraṇāt  saṃnyāsinaḥ pratyavāyaḥ kalpayitum śakyaḥ  yathā brahmacāriṇām asaṃnyāsinām api karmiṇām na tavan nityānām karmaṇām abhāvāt  eva bhāva rūpasya pratyavāyasya utpattiḥ kalpayitum śakyā katham asataḥ sat jāyate iti asataḥ sat janma asambhava śruteḥ yadi vihita akaraṇāt  asambhāvyam api pratyavāyam brūyāt  vedas tadā anartha karaḥ  vedaḥ apramāṇam iti  uktam syāt  vihitasya karaṇa akaraṇayoḥ duḥkha mātra phala tvāt tathā ca kārakam śāstram na jñāpakam iti anupapanna artham kalpitam syāt  na ca etad  iṣṭam tasmāt  na saṃnyāsinām karmāṇi atas  jñāna karmaṇoḥ samuccaya anupapattiḥ jyāyasī ced  karmaṇas te matā buddhiḥ  iti arjunasya praśna anupapatteḥ  ca yadi hi bhagavatā dvitīye adhyāye jñānam karma ca samuccayena tvayā anuṣṭheyam iti  uktam syāt  tatas  arjunasya praśnaḥ  anupapannaḥ  jyāyasī ced  karmaṇas te matā buddhiḥ  janārdana iti arjunāya ced  buddhi karmaṇī tvayā anuṣṭheye iti ukte yā karmaṇaḥ  jyāyasī buddhiḥ sā api  uktā eva iti tad  kim karmaṇi ghore mām niyojayasi keśava iti praśnaḥ  na kathaṃcana upapadyate na ca arjunasya eva jyāyasī buddhiḥ  na anuṣṭheya iti bhagavatā uktam pūrvam iti kalpayitum yuktam yena jyāyasī ced  iti praśnaḥ syāt  yadi punar  ekasya puruṣasya jñāna karmaṇor virodhāt  yugapad  anuṣṭhānam na sambhavati iti bhinna puruṣa anuṣṭheya tvam bhagavatā pūrvam uktam syāt  tatas  ayam praśna upapannaḥ jyāyasī ced  iti  ādiḥ avivekataḥ praśna kalpanāyām api bhinna puruṣa anuṣṭheya tvena bhagavataḥ prativacanam na upapadyate na ca ajñāna nimittam bhagavat prativacanam kalpyam asmāc ca bhinna puruṣa anuṣṭheya tvena jñāna karma niṣṭhayoḥ  bhagavataḥ prativacana darśanāt  jñāna karmaṇoḥ samuccaya anupapattiḥ tasmāt  kevalāt  eva jñānān mokṣa iti  eṣaḥ  arthaḥ  niścitaḥ  gītāsu sarva upaniṣatsu ca jñāna karmaṇor ekam vada niścitya iti ca eka viṣayā eva prārthanā anupapanna ubhayoḥ samuccaya sambhave kuru karma eva tasmāt  tvam iti ca jñāna niṣṭhāsambhavam arjunasya avadhāraṇena darśayiṣyati jyāyasī śreyasī ced  yadi karmaṇaḥ sakāśāt  te tava matā abhipretā buddhiḥ  jñānam he janārdana   yadi buddhi karmaṇī samuccite iṣṭe tadā ekam śreyaḥ sādhanam iti karmaṇaḥ  jyāyasī buddhiḥ  iti karmaṇaḥ  atirikta karaṇam buddheḥ  anupapannam arjunena kṛtam syāt  na hi tad  eva tasmāt  phalataḥ atiriktam syāt  tathā ca karmaṇaḥ śreyaskarī bhagavatā uktā buddhiḥ aśreyaskaram ca karma kurv iti mām pratipādayati tad  kim nu kāraṇam iti bhagavata upālambham iva kurvan tad  kim kasmāt  karmaṇi ghore krūre hiṃsā lakṣaṇe mām niyojayasi keśava iti ca yad  āha tad  ca na upapadyate atha smārtena eva karmaṇā samuccayaḥ sarveṣām bhagavatā uktaḥ  arjunena ca avadhārita ced  tad  kim karmaṇi ghore mām niyojayasi iti  ādi katham yuktam vacanam kim ca vyāmiśreṇa iva yadi api vivaktā abhidhāyī bhagavān tathā api mama manda buddheḥ  vyāmiśram iva bhagavat vākyam pratibhāti tena mama buddhim mohayasi iva mama buddhi vyāmoha apanayāya hi pravṛttas tvam tu katham mohayasi atas  bravīmi buddhim mohayasi iva me mama iti tvam tu bhinna kartṛkayoḥ jñāna karmaṇor eka puruṣa anuṣṭhāna asaṃbhavam yadi manyase tatra evam sati tad  tayoḥ  ekam buddhim karma vā idam eva arjunasya yogyam buddhi śakti avasthā anurūpam iti niścitya vada brūhi yena jñānena karmaṇā vā anyatareṇa śreyaḥ  aham āpnuyām prāpnuyām yadi hi karma niṣṭhāyām guṇa bhūtam api jñānam bhagavatā uktam syāt  tad  katham tayoḥ  ekam vada iti  eka viṣaya eva arjunasya śuśrūṣā syāt  na hi bhagavatā pūrvam uktam anyatara d eva jñāna karmaṇoḥ vakṣyāmi na eva dvayam iti yena ubhaya prāpti asaṃbhavam ātmanaḥ  manyamāna ekam eva prārthayet  praśna anurūpam eva prativacanam śrī bhagavān uvāca loke asmin śāstra artha anuṣṭhāna adhikṛtānām traivarṇikānām dvividhā dvi prakārā niṣṭhā sthitiḥ anuṣṭheya tātparyam purā pūrvam sarga ādau prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā tāsām abhyudaya niḥśreyasa prāpti sādhanam veda artha saṃpradāyam āviṣkurvatā proktā mayā sarvajñena īśvareṇa he anaghā apāpa tatra kā sā dvividhā niṣṭhā iti  āha tatra jñāna yogena jñānam eva yoga s tena sāṃkhyānām ātmānātma viṣaya viveka vijñānavatām brahmacarya āśramāt  eva kṛta saṃnyāsānām vedānta vijñāna su niścita arthānām paramahaṃsa parivrājakānām brahmaṇi  eva avasthitānām niṣṭhā proktā karma yogena karma eva yogaḥ karma yoga s tena karma yogena yoginām karmiṇām niṣṭhā proktā iti  arthaḥ yadi ca ekena puruṣeṇa ekasmai puruṣa arthāya jñānam karma ca samuccityā anuṣṭheyam bhagavatā iṣṭam uktam vakṣyamāṇam vā gītāsu vedeṣu ca uktam katham iha arjunāya upasannāya priyāya viśiṣṭa abhinna puruṣa kartṛke eva jñāna karma niṣṭhe brūyāt  yadi punar  arjunaḥ  jñānam karma ca dvayam śrutvā svayam eva anuṣṭhāsyati anyeṣām tu bhinna puruṣa anuṣṭheya tām vakṣyāmi iti matam bhagavataḥ kalpyeta tadā rāga dveṣavān apramāṇa bhūtaḥ  bhagavān kalpitaḥ syāt  tad  ca ayuktam tasmāt  kayā api yuktyā na samuccayaḥ  jñāna karmaṇoḥ yad  arjunena uktam karmaṇaḥ  jyāyaḥ tvam buddheḥ  tad  ca sthitam anirākaraṇāt  tasya āś ca jñāna niṣṭhāyāḥ saṃnyāsinām eva anuṣṭheya tvam bhinna puruṣa anuṣṭheyatva vacanāt  bhagavata evam eva anumatam iti gamyate mām ca bandha kāraṇe karmaṇi  eva niyojayasi iti viṣaṇṇa manasam arjunam karma nārabhe iti  evam manvānam ālakṣya āha bhagavān na karmaṇā m an ārambhāt  iti athavā jñāna karma niṣṭhayoḥ paraspara virodhāt  ekena puruṣeṇa yugapad  anuṣṭhātum aśakya tve sati itaretara anapekṣayoḥ  eva puruṣa artha hetu tve prāpte karma niṣṭhāyā jñāna niṣṭhā prāpti hetu tvena puruṣa artha hetu tvam na svātantryeṇa jñāna niṣṭhā tu karma niṣṭha upāya labdha ātmikā satī svātantryeṇa puruṣa artha hetuḥ anya anapekṣā iti  etam artham pradarśayiṣyan āha bhagavān na karmaṇā kriyāṇām yajña ādīnām iha janmani janmāntare vā anuṣṭhitānām upātta durita kṣaya hetutvena sattva śuddhi kāraṇānām tad kāraṇa tvena ca jñāna utpatti dvāreṇa jñāna niṣṭhā hetūnām jñānam utpadyate puṃsām kṣayāt  pāpasya karmaṇaḥ yathā ādarśa tala prakhye paśyati  ātmānam ātmani iti  ādi smaraṇāt  anārambhāt  ananuṣṭhānāt  naiṣkarmyam niṣkarma bhāvam karma śūnyatām jñāna yogena niṣṭhām niṣkriya ātma svarūpeṇa eva avasthānam iti yāvat  puruṣaḥ  na aśnute na prāpnoti iti  arthaḥ karmaṇām anārambhān naiṣkarmyam na aśnuta iti vacanāt  tad viparyayāt teṣām ārambhān naiṣkarmyam aśnuta iti gamyate kasmāt  punar  kāraṇāt  karmaṇām anārambhān naiṣkarmyam na aśnute iti ucyate karma ārambhasya eva naiṣkarmya upāya tvāt na hi  upāyam antareṇa upeya prāptiḥ  asti karma yoga upāya tvam ca naiṣkarmya lakṣaṇasya jñāna yogasya śrutau iha ca pratipādanāt  śrutau tāvat  prakṛtasya ātma lokasya vedyasya vedanā upāya tvena tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇā vividiṣanti yajñena iti  ādinā karma yogasya jñāna yoga upāya tvam pratipāditam iha api ca saṃnyāsas tu mahā bāhaḥ duḥkham āptum ayogataḥ yoginaḥ karma kurvanti saṅgam tyaktvā ātma śuddhaye yajñaḥ  dānam tapaḥ  ca eva pāvanāni manīṣiṇām iti  ādi pratipādayiṣyati nanu ca abhayam sarva bhūtebhyaḥ  dattvā naiṣkarmyam ācaret  iti  ādau kartavya karma saṃnyāsāt  api naiṣkarmya prāptim darśayati loke ca karmaṇām anārambhān naiṣkarmyam iti prasiddhataram atas  ca naiṣkarmya arthinaḥ kim karma ārambheṇa iti prāptam ata āha na ca saṃnyasanāt  eva iti na api saṃnyasanāt  eva kevalāt  karma parityāga mātrāt  eva jñāna rahitāt  siddhim naiṣkarmya lakṣaṇām jñāna yogena niṣṭhām samadhigacchati na prāpnoti kasmāt  punar  kāraṇāt  karma saṃnyāsa mātrāt  eva kevalāt  jñāna rahitāt  siddhim naiṣkarmya lakṣaṇām puruṣaḥ  na adhigacchati iti hetu ākāṅkṣāyām āha na hi yasmāt  kṣaṇam api kālam jātu kadācid  kaścid  tiṣṭhati  akarma kṛt  san kasmāt  kāryate pravartyate hi yasmāt  avaśa eva asvatantra eva karma sarvaḥ prāṇī prakṛti jaiḥ prakṛtitaḥ  jātaiḥ sattva rajaḥ tamobhiḥ guṇaiḥ ajña iti vākya śeṣaḥ yatas  vakṣyati guṇaiḥ  yaḥ  na vicālyate iti sāṃkhyānām pṛthakkaraṇāt  ajñānām eva hi karma yogaḥ na jñāninām jñāninām tu guṇaiḥ  acālyamānānām svatas  calana abhāvāt karma yogaḥ  na upapadyate tathā ca vyākhyātam veda avināśinam iti  atra yad  tu  anātma jñaḥ coditam karma na ārabhate iti tad  asad eva iti  āha karmendriyāṇi hasta ādīni saṃyamya saṃhṛtya ya āste tiṣṭhati manasā smaran cintayan indriya arthān viṣayān vimūḍha ātmā vimūḍha antaḥaraṇaḥ  mithyā ācāraḥ  mṛṣā ācāraḥ pāpa ācāraḥ sa ucyate yaḥ  tu punar  karmaṇi  adhikṛtaḥ  ajñaḥ buddhīndriyāṇi manasā niyamya ārabhate arjuna karmendriyaiḥ vāc pāṇi ādibhiḥ kim ārabhate iti  āha karma yogam asaktaḥ san phala abhisandhi varjitaḥ sa viśiṣyate itarasmāt  mithyā ācārāt  yatas  evam atas  niyatam nityam śāstra upadiṣṭam yaḥ  yasmin karmaṇi  adhikṛtaḥ phalāya ca aśrutam tad  niyatam karma tad  kuru tvam he arjuna   yatas  karma jyāyaḥ adhikataram phalataḥ hi yasmāt  akarmaṇaḥ  akaraṇāt  anārambhāt  katham śarīra yātrā śarīra sthitiḥ  api ca te tava na prasidhyet  prasiddhim na gacchet  akarmaṇaḥ  akaraṇāt  atas  dṛṣṭaḥ karma akarmaṇoḥ  viśeṣaḥ  loke yad  ca manyase bandha artha tvāt karma na kartavyam iti tad  api  asat  katham yajñaḥ  vai viṣṇuḥ iti śruteḥ  yajña īśvaraḥ tad artham yad  kriyate tad  yajña artham karma tasmāt  karmaṇaḥ  anyatra anyena karmaṇā lokaḥ  ayam adhikṛtaḥ karma kṛt  karma bandhanaḥ karma bandhanam yasya saḥ  ayam karma bandhanaḥ  lokaḥ na tu yajña arthāt  atas tad artham yajña artham karma kaunteya mukta saṅgaḥ karma phala saṅga varjitaḥ san samācāra nirvartaya itas  ca adhikṛtena karma kartavyam saha yajñāḥ yajña sahitāḥ prajās trayaḥ  varṇāḥ  tāḥ sṛṣṭvā utpādya purā pūrvam sarga ādau   uvāca uktavān prajāpatiḥ prajānām srāṣṭā anena yajñena prasaviṣya dhvam prasavaḥ  vṛddhiḥ  utpattis tām kurudhvam eṣa yajñaḥ  vaḥ  yuṣmākam astu bhavatu iṣṭakā madhuj  iṣṭān abhipretān kāmān phala viśeṣān dogdhi iti iṣṭakā madhuj  katham devān indra ādīn bhāvayata vardhayata anena yajñena te devāḥ  bhāvayantu āpyāyayantu vṛṣṭi ādinā vaḥ  yuṣmān evam parasparam anyonyam bhāvayantaḥ śreyaḥ param mokṣa lakṣaṇam vijñāna prāpti krameṇa avāpsyatha svargam vā param śreyaḥ  avāpsyatha kim ca iṣṭān abhipretān bhogān hi vaḥ  yuṣmabhyam devāḥ  dāsyante vitariṣyanti strī paśu putra ādīn yajña bhāvitā yajñaiḥ  vardhitāḥ  toṣitā iti  arthaḥ taiḥ  devaiḥ  dattān bhogān apradāya adattvā ānṛṇyam akṛtvā iti  arthaḥ ebhyaḥ  devebhyaḥ yaḥ  bhuṅkte sva deha indriyāṇi  eva tarpayati stena eva taskara eva sa deva ādi svāpa hārī ye punar  deva yajña ādīn nirvartya tad śiṣṭam aśanam amṛta ākhyam aśitum
