pariṇatāt  pratyakṣam bhavanti jāyante bhūtāni parjanyāt  vṛṣṭeḥ  annasya saṃbhavaḥ  anna saṃbhavaḥ yajñād bhavati parjanyaḥ agnau prāsta āhutiḥ samyak  ādityam upatiṣṭhate āditya at  jāyate vṛṣṭiḥ  vṛṣṭeḥ  annam tatas  prajāḥ iti smṛteḥ yajñaḥ  apūrvam sa ca yajñaḥ karma samudbhavaḥ ṛtvij yajamānayoḥ  ca vyāpāraḥ karma tad samudbhavaḥ  yasya yajñasya apūrvasya sa yajñaḥ karma samudbhavaḥ tad  ca evaṃvidham karma kutaḥ jātam iti  āha karma brahma udbhavam brahma vedaḥ sa udbhavaḥ kāraṇam prakāśakaḥ  yasya tad  karma brahma udbhavam viddhi vijānīhi brahma punar  veda ākhyam akṣara samudbhavam akṣaram brahma paramātmā samudbhavaḥ  yasya tad  akṣara samudbhavam brahma veda iti  arthaḥ yasmāt  sākṣāt  paramātma ākhyād akṣarāt  puruṣa niḥśvāsavat  samudbhūtam brahma tasmāt  sarva artha prakāśaka tvāt  sarva gatam sarva gatam api sat  nityam sadā yajña vidhi pradhāna tvāt  yajñe pratiṣṭhitam evam ittham īśvareṇa veda yajña pūrvakam jagat cakram pravartitam na anuvartayati iha loke yaḥ karmaṇi  adhikṛtaḥ san   aghāyuḥ  agham pāpam āyuḥ  jīvanam yasya saḥ  aghāyuḥ pāpa jīvana iti yāvat  indriya ārāmaḥ indriyaiḥ  ārāmaḥ āramaṇam ākrīḍā viṣayeṣu yasya sa indriya ārāmaḥ  mogham vṛthā he pārtha sa jīvati tasmāt  ajñena adhikṛtena kartavyam eva karma iti prakaraṇa arthaḥ prāk  ātma jñāna niṣṭhā yogya tā prāpteḥ  tādarthyena karma yoga anuṣṭhānam adhikṛtena anātma jñena kartavyam eva iti  etad  na karmaṇām anārambhāt  iti  ata ārabhya śarīra yātrā api ca te na prasidhyet  akarmaṇa iti  evam antena pratipādya yajña arthāt  karmaṇaḥ  anyatra iti  ādinā mogham pārtha sa jīvati iti  evam antena api granthena prāsaṅgikam adhikṛtasya anātma vidaḥ karma anuṣṭhāne bahu kāraṇam uktam tad akaraṇe ca doṣa saṃkīrtanam kṛtam evam sthite kim evam pravartitam caktram sarveṇa anuvartanīyam āhaḥ svid  pūrva ukta karma yoga anuṣṭhāna upāya prāpyām anātma vidā jñāna yogena eva niṣṭhām ātma vidbhiḥ sāṃkhyaiḥ  anuṣṭheyām aprāptena eva iti  evam artham arjunasya praśnam āśaṅkaya svayam eva vā śāstra arthasya viveka pratipatti artham etam vai tam ātmānam viditvā nivṛtta mithyā jñānāḥ santaḥ  brāhmaṇā mithyājñānavadbhyaḥ  avaśyam kartavyebhyaḥ putra eṣaṇa ādibhyaḥ  vyutthāya atha bhikṣā caryam śarīra sthiti mātra prayuktam caranti na teṣām ātma jñāna niṣṭhā avi atirekeṇa anyat kāryam asti iti  evam śruti artham iha gīta aśāstre pratipipādayiṣitam āviṣkurvan   āha bhagavān yaḥ  tu sāṃkhya ātma jñāna niṣṭha ātma ratiḥ ātmani  eva ratiḥ  na viṣayeṣu yasya sa ātma ratiḥ  eva syāt  bhavet  ātma tṛptaḥ  ca ātmanā eva tṛptaḥ  na annarasa ādinā sa mānavaḥ  manuṣyaḥ saṃnyāsī ātmani  eva ca santuṣṭaḥ santoṣaḥ  hi bāhya artha lābhe sarvasya bhavati tam anapekṣya ātmani  eva ca santuṣṭaḥ sarvatas  vīta tṛṣṇa iti  etad  ya īdṛśaḥ ātma vid  tasya kāryam karaṇīyam na vidyate na asti iti  arthaḥ kim na eva tasya paramātma rateḥ kṛtena karmaṇā arthaḥ prayojanam asti astu tarhi  akṛtena akaraṇena pratyavāya ākhyaḥ  anarthaḥ na akṛtena iha loke kaścana kaścid  api pratyavāya prāpti rūpaḥ ātma hāni lakṣaṇaḥ  vā na eva asti na ca asya sarva bhūteṣu brahma ādi sthāvara anteṣu bhūteṣu kaścid  artha vyapāśrayaḥ prayojana nimitta kriyā asādhyaḥ  vyapāśrayaḥ vyapāśrayaṇam ālambanam kaṃcid  bhūta viśeṣam āśritya na sādhyaḥ kaścid  arthaḥ  asti yena tad arthā kriyā anuṣṭheyā syāt  na tvam etasmin sarvatas  saṃpluta udaka sthānīye samyak darśane vartase yatas evam tasmāt  asaktaḥ saṅga varjitaḥ satatam sarvadā kāryam kartavyam nityam karma samācara nirvartaya asaktaḥ  hi yasmāt  samācaran īśvara artham karma kurvan param mokṣam āpnoti pūruṣaḥ sattva śuddhi dvāreṇa iti  arthaḥ yasmāt ca karmaṇā eva hi yasmāt  pūrve kṣatriyāḥ vidvāṃsaḥ saṃsiddhim mokṣam gantum āsthitāḥ pravṛttāḥ ke janaka ādayaḥ janakā vapati prabhṛtayaḥ yadi te prāpta samyak darśanāḥ tatas  loka saṃgraha artham prārabdha karma tvāt  karmaṇā saha eva asaṃnyasya eva karma saṃsiddhim āsthitā iti  arthaḥ atha aprāpta samyak adarśanāḥ janaka ādayaḥ tadā karmaṇā sattva śuddhi sādhana bhūtena ktrameṇa saṃsiddhim āsthitā iti vyākhyeyaḥ lokaḥ atha manyase pūrveḥ api janaka ādibhiḥ ajānadbhiḥ eva kartavyam karma kṛtam tāvatā na avaśyam anyena kartavyam samyak darśanavatā kṛtāthena iti tathā api prārabdha karma āyattaḥ tvam loka saṃgraham eva api lokasya unmārga pravṛtti nivāraṇam loka saṃgrahaḥ tam eva api prayojanam saṃpaśyan kartum arhasi loka saṃgrahaḥ kim artham kartavya iti  ucyate yad yad karma ācarati karoti śreṣṭhaḥ pradhānaḥ tad tad eva karma ācarati itaraḥ  anyaḥ janaḥ tad anugataḥ kim ca saḥ śreṣṭhaḥ yad  pramāṇam kurute laukikam vaidikam vā lokaḥ tad  anuvartate tad eva pramāṇīkaroti iti  arthaḥ yadi  atra te loka saṃgraha kartavyatāyām vipratipattiḥ  tarhi mām kim na paśyasi na me mama pārtha na asti na vidyate kartavyam triṣu  api lokeṣu kiṃcana kiṃcid  api kasmāt  na anavāptam aprāptam avāptavyam prāpaṇīyam tathā api varta eva ca karmaṇi  aham yadi hi punar  aham na varteya jātu kadācid  karmaṇi  atandritaḥ  analasaḥ san mama śreṣṭhasya sataḥ  vatrma mārgam anuvartante manuṣyāḥ he pārtha   sarvaśas  sarva prakāraiḥ utsīdeyuḥ  vinaśyeyuḥ  ime sarve lokāḥ loka sthiti nimittasya karmaṇaḥ  abhāvāt  na kuryām karma ced  aham kim ca saṃkarasya ca kartā syām tena kāraṇena upahanyām imāḥ prajāḥ prajānām anugrahāya pravṛtta upahatim upahananam kuryām iti  arthaḥ mama īśvarasya ananurūpam āpadyate yadi punar  aham iva tvam kṛtārtha buddhiḥ ātma vid anyaḥ  vā tasya api ātmanaḥ kartavya abhāve api para anugraha eva kartavya iti  āha saktāḥ karmaṇi  asya karmaṇaḥ phalam mama bhaviṣyati iti kecid  avidvāṃsaḥ  yathā kurvanti bhārata kuryāt  vidvān ātma vid  tathā āsaktaḥ san tadvat  kim artham karoti tad  sṛṇu cikīrṣuḥ kartum icchuḥ loka saṃgraham evam loka saṃgraham cikīrṣeḥ  na mama ātma vidaḥ kartavyam asti anyasya vā loka saṃgraham muktvā tatas  tasya ātma vidaḥ idam upadiśyate buddhi bhedaḥ  buddhi bhedaḥ  mayā idam kartavyam bhoktavyam ca asya karmaṇaḥ phalam iti niścaya rūpāyāḥ  buddheḥ  bhedanam cālanam buddhi bhedas tam na janayet  na utpādayet  ajñānām avivekinām karma saṅginām karmaṇi  āsaktānām āsaṅgavatām kim nu kuryāt  joṣayet  kārayet  sarva karmāṇi vidvān svayam tad  eva aviduṣām karma yuktaḥ  abhiyuktaḥ samācaran avidvān ajñaḥ katham karmasu sajjate iti  āha prakṛteḥ prakṛtiḥ pradhānam sattva rajaḥ tamasām guṇānām sāmya avasthā tasyāḥ prakṛteḥ guṇaiḥ vikāraiḥ kārya karaṇa rūpaiḥ kriyamāṇāni karmāṇi laukikāni śāstrīyāṇi ca sarvaśas  sarva prakāraiḥ  ahaṃkāra vimūḍha ātmā kārya karaṇa saṃghāta ātma pratyayaḥ ahaṃkāra s tena vividham nānāvidham mūḍha ātmā antaḥkaraṇam yasya saḥ  ayam kārya karaṇa dharmā kārya karaṇa abhimānī avidyayā karmāṇi ātmani manyamānaḥ tad tad karmaṇām aham kartā iti manyate yaḥ punar  vidvān tattva vid  tu mahā bāhaḥ kasya tattva vid  guṇa karma vibhāgayoḥ guṇa vibhāgasya karma vibhāgasya ca tattva vid  iti  arthaḥ guṇāḥ karaṇa ātmakāḥ guṇeṣu viṣaya ātmakeṣu vartante na ātmā iti matvā na sajjate saktim na karoti ye punar  prakṛteḥ guṇaiḥ samyak  mūḍhāḥ saṃmohitāḥ santaḥ sajjante guṇānām karmasu guṇa karmasu vayam karma kurmaḥ phalāya iti tān karma saṅginaḥ  akṛtsna vidaḥ karma phala mātra darśinaḥ mandān manda prajñān kṛtsna vid  ātma vid  svayam na vicālayet  buddhi bheda karaṇam eva cālanam tad  na kuryāt  iti  arthaḥ katham punar  karmaṇi  adhikṛtena ajñena mumukṣuṇā karma kartavyam iti ucyate mayi vāsudeve parameśvare sarvajñe sarva ātmani sarvāṇi karmāṇi saṃnyasya nikṣipya adhyātma cetasā viveka buddhyā aham kartā īśvarāya bhṛtyavat  karomi iti  anayā buddhyā kim ca nirāśīḥ  tyakta āśīḥ nirmamaḥ  mama bhāvaḥ  ca nirgataḥ  yasya tava sa tvam nirmamaḥ  bhūtvā yudhyasva vigata jvaraḥ  vigata santāpaḥ  vigata śokaḥ san   iti  arthaḥ yad  etad  mama matam karma kartavyam iti sa pramāṇam uktam tad  tathā ye me madīyam idam matam nityam anutiṣṭhanti anuvartante mānavā manuṣyāḥ śraddhāvantaḥ śraddadhānā anasūyantaḥ  asūyām ca mayi parama gurau vāsudeve akurvantaḥ  mucyante te api  evaṃbhūtāḥ karmabhiḥ  dharma adharma ākhyaiḥ ye tu tad viparītā etad  mama matam abhyasūyantaḥ  nindantaḥ  na anutiṣṭhanti na anuvartante me matam sarveṣu jñāneṣu vividham mūḍhāḥ  te sarva jñāna vimūḍhān   tān viddhi jānīhi naṣṭān nāśam gatān acetasaḥ  avivekinaḥ kasmāt  punar  kāraṇāt  tvadīyam matam na anutiṣṭhantaḥ para dharmān anutiṣṭhanti svadharmam ca na anuvartante tvad pratikūlāḥ katham na bibhyati tvad śāsana atikrama doṣāt tatra āha sadṛśam anurūpam ceṣṭate ceṣṭām karoti kasyāḥ svasyāḥ svakīyāyāḥ prakṛteḥ prakṛtiḥ  nāma pūrva kṛta dharma adharma ādi saṃskārā vartamāna janma ādau   abhivyaktāḥ sā prakṛtiḥ tasyāḥ sadṛśam eva sarvaḥ  jantuḥ  jñānavān api ceṣṭate kim punar  mūrkhaḥ tasmāt  prakṛtim yānti  anugacchanti bhūtāni prāṇinaḥ nigrahaḥ  niṣedha rūpaḥ kim kariṣyati mama vā anyasya vā durnigrahā prakṛtiḥ  iti vākya śeṣaḥ yadi sarvaḥ  jantuḥ  ātmanaḥ prakṛti sadṛśam eva ceṣṭate na ca prakṛti śūnyaḥ kaścid  asti tatas  puruṣakārasya viṣaya anupapatteḥ śāstra anarthakya prāptau   idam ucyate indriyasya indriyasya arthe sarva indriyāṇām arthe śabda ādi viṣaye iṣṭe rāgaḥ  aniṣṭe dveṣa iti  evam pratīndriya artham rāga dveṣau   avaśyaṃbhāvinau tatra ayam puruṣakārasya śāstra arthasya ca viṣaya ucyate śāstra arthe pravṛttaḥ pūrvam eva rāga dveṣayoḥ  vaśam na āgacchet  yā hi puruṣasya prakṛtiḥ sā rāga dveṣa puraḥsara eva sva kārye puruṣam pravartayati tadā svadharma parityāgaḥ para dharma anuṣṭhānam ca bhavati yadā punā rāga dveṣau tad pratipakṣeṇa niyamayati tadā śāstra dṛṣṭiḥ  eva puruṣaḥ  bhavati na prakṛti vaśaḥ tasmāt  tayaḥ rāga dveṣayoḥ  vaśam na āgacchet  yatas  tau hi  asya puruṣasya paripanthinau śreyaḥ mārgasya vighna kartārau taskarau   iva pathi iti  arthaḥ tatra rāga dveṣa prayuktaḥ  manyate śāsra artham api  anyathā para dharmaḥ  api dharma tvāt  anuṣṭheya eva iti tad  asat  śreyān praśasyataraḥ svar  dharmaḥ svadharmaḥ  viguṇaḥ  api vigata guṇa u api anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ para dharmāt  su anuṣṭhitāt  sādguṇyena saṃpāditāt  api svadharme sthitasya nidhanam maraṇam api śreyaḥ para dharme sthitasya jīvitāt  kasmāt  para dharmaḥ bhaya āvahaḥ naraka ādi lakṣaṇam bhayam āvahati iti yatas  yadi api anartha mūlam dhyāyataḥ  viṣayān puṃsa iti rāga dveṣau hi  asya paripanthinau iti ca uktam vikṣiptam anavadhāritam ca tad  uktam tad  saṃkṣiptam niścitam ca idam eva iti jñātum icchan arjuna uvāca jñāte hi tasmin tad ucchedāya yatnam kuryām iti arjuna uvāca atha kena hetu bhūtena prayuktaḥ san rājñā iva bhṛtyaḥ  ayam pāpam karma carati ācarati pūruṣaḥ puruṣaḥ svayam anicchan   api he vārṣṇeya vṛṣṇi kula prasūta   balāt  iva niyojitaḥ  rājñā iva iti  uktaḥ  dṛṣṭāntaḥ śṛṇu tvam tam vairiṇam sarva anartha karam yam tvam pṛcchasi iti bhagavān uvāca aiśvaryasya samagrasya dharmasya yaśasaḥ śriyaḥ vairāgyasya atha mokṣasya ṣaṇṇām bhaga iti iṅganā iti  aiśvarya ādi ṣaṭkam yasmin vāsudeve nityam apratibaddha tvena sāmastyena ca vartate utpattim pralayam ca eva bhūtānām āgatim gatim vetti vidyām avidyām ca sa vācyaḥ  bhagavān iti utpatti ādi viṣayam ca vijñānam yasya sa vāsudevaḥ  vācyaḥ  bhagavān iti kāma iti kāma eṣa sarva loka śatruḥ  yad nimittā sarva anartha prāptiḥ prāṇinām sa eṣa kāmaḥ pratihataḥ kenacid  krodha tvena pariṇamate atas  krodhaḥ  api  eṣa eva rajaḥ guṇa samudbhavaḥ  rajaḥ  ca tad guṇa ś ca rajaḥ guṇaḥ sa samudbhavaḥ  yasya sa kāmaḥ  rajaḥ guṇa samudbhavaḥ rajaḥ guṇasya vā samudbhavaḥ kāmaḥ  hi  udbhūtaḥ  rajaḥ pravartayan puruṣam pravartayati tṛṣṇayā hi  ahaṃkārita iti duḥkhinām rajaḥ kārye sevā ādau pravṛttānām pralāpaḥ śrūyate mahā aśanaḥ  mahat  aśanam asya iti mahā aśanaḥ ataeva mahā pāpmā kāmena hi preritaḥ  jantuḥ pāpam karoti atas  viddhi  enam kāmam iha saṃsāre vairiṇam katham vairī iti dṛṣṭāntaiḥ pratyāyayati dhūmena sahajena āvriyate vahniḥ prakāśa ātmakaḥ  aprakāśa ātmakena yathā vā ādarśaḥ  malena ca yathā ulbena ca jarāyuṇā garbhaveṣṭanena ca āvṛta ācchāditaḥ  garbhas tathā tena idam āvṛtam kim punar  tad  idaṃśabda vācyam yad  kāmena āvṛtam iti  ucyate āvṛtam etena jñānam jñāninaḥ  nitya vairiṇā jñānī hi jānāti  anena aham anarthe prayuktaḥ pūrvam eva iti duḥkhī ca bhavati nityam eva atas  asau jñāninaḥ  nitya vairī na tu mūrkhasya sa hi kāmam tṛṣṇā kāle mitram iva paśyan tad kārye duḥkhe prāpte jānāti tṛṣṇayā aham duḥkhi tvam āpādita iti na pūrvam eva atas  jñānina eva nitya vairī kiṃrūpeṇa kāmarūpeṇa kāma icchā eva rūpam asya iti kāmarūpas tena duṣpūreṇa duḥkhena pūraṇam asya iti duṣpūras tena analena na asya alam paryāptiḥ  vidyata iti  analas tena ca kim adhiṣṭhānaḥ punar  kāmaḥ  jñānasya āvaraṇa tvena vairī sarvasya lokasya iti  apekṣāyām āha jñāte hi śatroḥ  adhiṣṭhāne sukhena nibarhaṇam kartum śakyata iti indriyāṇi manaḥ  buddhiḥ  ca asya kāmasya adhiṣṭhānam āśraya ucyate etaiḥ  indriya ādibhiḥ  āśrayaiḥ  vimohayati vividham mohayati  eṣa kāmaḥ  jñānam āvṛtya ācchādya dehinam śarīriṇam yataevam tasmāt  tvam indriyāṇi  ādau pūrvam eva niyamya vaśīkṛtya bharata ṛṣabha pāpmānam pāpa ācāram kāmam prajahihi parityaja enam prakṛtam vairiṇam jñāna vijñāna nāśanam jñānam śāstrata ācāryatas  ca ātma ādīnām avabodhaḥ vijñānam viśeṣatas tad anubhavas tayoḥ  jñāna vijñānayoḥ śreyaḥ prāpti hetvoḥ  nāśanam nāśa karam prajahihi ātmanaḥ parityaja iti  arthaḥ indriyāṇi  ādau niyamya kāmam śatrum jahihi iti  uktam tatra kim āśrayaḥ kāmam jahyāt  iti  ucyate indriyāṇi śrotra ādīni pañca deham sthūlam bāhyam paricchinnam ca apekṣya saukṣmya antaratva vyāpi tvā ādi apekṣayā parāṇi prakṛṣṭāni  āhuḥ paṇḍitāḥ tathā indriyebhyaḥ param manaḥ saṃkalpa vikalpa ātmakam tathā manasas tu parā buddhiḥ  niścaya ātmikā tathā yaḥ sarva dṛśyebhyaḥ  buddhi antebhyaḥ  abhyantaraḥ  yam dehinam indriya ādibhiḥ  āśrayaiḥ  yuktaḥ kāmaḥ  jñāna āvaraṇa dvāreṇa mohayati iti  uktam buddheḥ paratas  tu sa sa buddheḥ  draṣṭā para ātmā tatas  kim evam buddheḥ param ātmānam buddhvā jñātvā saṃstabhya samyak  stambhanam kṛtvā ātmānam svena eva ātmanā saṃskṛtena manasā samyak  samādhāya iti  arthaḥ jahy enam śatrum he mahā bāhaḥ   kāmarūpam durāsadam duḥkhena asada āsādanam prāptiḥ  yasya tam durāsadam durvijñeya aneka viśeṣam iti yaḥ  ayam yogaḥ  adhyāya dvayena uktaḥ  jñāna niṣṭhā lakṣaṇaḥ sa sannyāsaḥ karma yoga upāyaḥ yasmin veda arthaḥ parisamāptaḥ pravṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ  nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ  ca gītāsu ca sarvāsu  ayam eva yogaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ  bhagavatā ataeva parisamāptaḥ pravṛttim veda artham manvānaḥ  tam vaṃśa kathanena stauti śrī bhagavān imam adhyāya dvayena uktam yogam vivasvate ādityāya sarga ādau proktavān aham jagat paripālayitṝṇām kṣatriyāṇām bala ādhānāya tena yoga balena yuktāḥ samarthā bhavanti brahma parirakṣitum brahma kṣatre paripālite jagat  paripālayitum alam avyayam avyaya phala tvāt  na hi  asya samyak  darśana niṣṭhā lakṣaṇasya mokṣa ākhyam phalam vyeti sa ca vivasvān manave prāha manuḥ  ikṣvākave sva putrāya ādirājāya abravīt evam kṣatriya paramparā prāptam imam rājarṣayaḥ rājānaḥ  ca te ṛṣayaḥ  ca rājarṣayaḥ viduḥ  imam yogam sa yogaḥ kālena iha mahatā dīrgheṇa naṣṭaḥ  vicchinna sampradāyaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ  he parantapa   ātmanaḥ  vipakṣa bhūtāḥ para ucyante tān śaurya tejaḥ gabhastibhiḥ  bhānuḥ  iva tāpayati iti parantapaḥ śatru tāpana iti  arthaḥ durlabhān ajita indriyān prāpya naṣṭam yogam imam upalabhya lokam ca āpuruṣa artha sambandhinam sa eva ayam mayā te tubhyam adya idānīm yogaḥ proktaḥ purātanaḥ bhaktaḥ  asi me sakhā ca asi iti rahasyam hi yasmāt  etad  uttamam yogaḥ  jñānam iti  arthaḥ bhagavatā vipratiṣiddham uktam iti mā bhūt  kasyacid  buddhiḥ  iti parihāra artham codyam iva kurvan   arjuna uvāca aparam arvāk  vasudeva gṛhe bhavataḥ  janma param pūrvam sarga ādau janma utpattiḥ vivasvata ādityasya tad  katham etad  vijānīyām aviruddha artha tayā yaḥ  tvam eva ādau proktavān imam yogam sa eva tvam idānīm mahyam proktavān asi iti yā vāsudeve anīśvarā sarva jña āśaṅkā mūrkhāṇām tām pariharan śrī bhagavān uvāca pad arthaḥ  hi  arjunasya praśnaḥ bahūni me mama vyatītāni atikrāntāni janmāni tava ca he arjuna tāni  aham veda jāne sarvāṇi na tvam vettha jānīṣe dharma adharma ādi pratibaddha jñāna śakti tvāt aham punar  nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāva tvāt  anāvaraṇa jñāna śaktiḥ  iti veda aham he parantapa katham tarhi tava nityeśvarasya dharma adharma abhāve api janma iti  ucyate ajaḥ api janma rahitaḥ  api san tathā avyaya ātmā kṣīṇa jñāna śakti svabhāvaḥ  api san tathā bhūtānām brahma ādi stamba paryantānām īśvara īśana śīlaḥ  api san prakṛtim svām mama vaiṣṇavīm māyām triguṇa ātmikām yasyāḥ  vaśe sarvam idam jagad vartate yayā mohitam jagat  sat  svam ātmānam vāsudevam na jānāti tām prakṛtim svām adhiṣṭhāya vaśīkṛtya saṃbhavāmi dehavān iva bhavāmi jāta iva ātma māyayā ātmanaḥ  māyayā na paramārtha taḥ  lokavat  tad  ca janma kadā kimartham ca iti  ucyate yadā yadā hi dharmasya glāniḥ  hāniḥ  varṇa āśrama ādi lakṣaṇasya prāṇinām abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sādhanasya bhavati bhārata   abhyutthānam udbhavaḥ  adharmasya tadātmānam sṛjāmi  aham māyayā kimartham paritrāṇāya parirakṣaṇāya sādhūnām sat mārga sthānām vināśāya ca duṣkṛtām pāpa kāriṇām kim ca dharma saṃsthāpana arthāya dharmasya samyak sthāpanam tad artham sambhavāmi yuge yuge pratiyugam tad janma māyā rūpam karma ca sādhu paritrāṇa ādi me mama divyam aprākṛtam aiśvaram evam yathā uktam yaḥ  vetti tattvatas tattvena yathāvat  tyaktvā deham imam punar  janma punar  utpattim na eti na prāpnoti mām eti  āgacchati sa mucyate he arjuna na eṣa mokṣa mārga idānīm pravṛttaḥ kim tarhi pūrvam api vīta rāga bhaya krodhāḥ rāgaḥ  ca bhayam ca krodhaḥ  ca rāga bhaya krodhāḥ vītā vigatā rāga bhaya krodhā yebhyas te vīta rāga bhaya krodhāḥ mad mayā brahma vida īśvara abheda darśinaḥ mām eva parameśvaram upāśritāḥ kevala jñāna niṣṭhā iti  arthaḥ bahavaḥ  aneke jñāna tapasā jñānam eva ca paramātma viṣayam tapaḥ tena jñāna tapasā pūtāḥ parām śuddhim gatāḥ santaḥ mad bhāvam īśvara bhāvam mokṣam āgatāḥ samanuprāptāḥ itara tapaḥ nirapekṣā jñāna niṣṭhā iti  asya liṅgam jñāna tapasā iti viśeṣaṇam tava tarhi rāga dveṣau staḥ yena kebhyaḥ cit eva ātma bhāvam prayacchasi na sarvebhyaḥ iti  ucyate ye yathā yena prakāreṇa yena prayojanena yad phala arthi tayā mām prapadyante tān   tathā eva tad phala dānena bhajāmi  anugṛhṇāmi  aham iti  etad  teṣām mokṣam pratyanarthi tvāt  na hi  ekasya mumukṣu tvam phala arthi tvam ca yugapad  sambhavati atas  ye yad phala arthinas tān   tad phala pradānena ye yathā ukta kāriṇas tu  aphala arthinaḥ  mumukṣa vaḥ  ca tān jñāna pradānena ye jñāninaḥ sannyāsinaḥ  mumukṣa vaḥ  ca tān mokṣa pradānena tathā ārtān ārti haraṇena iti  evam yathā prapadyante ye tān   tathā eva bhajāmi iti  arthaḥ na punār rāga dveṣa nimittam moha nimittam vā kaṃcid  bhajāmi sarvathā api sarva avasthasya mama īśvarasya vartma mārgam anuvartante manuṣyāḥ yad phala arthi tayā yasmin karmaṇi  adhikṛtā ye prayatante te manuṣyā atra ucyante he pārtha sarvaśas  sarva prakāraiḥ yadi tava īśvarasya rāga ādi doṣa abhāvāt sarva prāṇiṣu  anujighṛkṣāyām tulyāyām sarva phala pradāna samarthe ca tvayi sati vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti jñānena eva mumukṣavaḥ santaḥ kasmāt  tvām eva sarve na pratipadyante iti śṛṇu tatra kāraṇam kāṅkṣantaḥ  abhīpsantaḥ karmaṇām siddhim phala niṣpattim prārthayantaḥ  yajanta iha asmin loke devatā indrāt gni ādyāḥ atha yaḥ  anyām devatām upāste anyaḥ  asau   anyaḥ  aham asmi iti na sa veda yathā paśuḥ evam sa devānām iti śruteḥ teṣām hi bhinna devatā yājinām phala ākāṅkṣiṇām kṣipram śīghram hi yasmān mānuṣe loke manuṣya loke hi śāstra adhikāraḥ kṣipram hi mānuṣe loke iti viśeṣaṇāt  anyeṣu  api karma phala siddhim darśayati bhagavān mānuṣe loke varṇa āśrama ādi karma adhikāra iti viśeṣaḥ teṣām ca varṇa āśrama adhikāriṇām karmiṇām phala siddhiḥ kṣipram bhavati karma jā karmaṇaḥ  jātā mānuṣa eva loke varṇa āśrama ādi karma adhikāraḥ na anyeṣu lokeṣu  iti niyamaḥ kiṃnimittaḥ iti athavā varṇa āśrama ādi pravibhāga upetā manuṣyā mama vartma anuvartante sarvaśa iti  uktam kasmāt  punar  kāraṇān niyamena tava eva vartma anuvartante na anyasya kim ucyate cāturvarṇyam catvāra eva varṇāḥ  cāturvarṇyam mayā īśvareṇa sṛṣṭam utpāditam brāhmaṇaḥ  asya mukham āsīt  iti  ādi śruteḥ guṇa karma vibhāga śaḥ guṇa vibhāgaśaḥ karma vibhāga śaś ca guṇāḥ sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi tatra sāttvikasya sattva pradhānasya brāhmaṇasya śamaḥ  damas tapaḥ iti  ādīni karmāṇi sattva upasarjana rajaḥ pradhānasya kṣatriyasya śaurya tejaḥ prabhṛtīni karmāṇi tam aupasarjana rajaḥ pradhānasya vaiśyasya kṛṣi ādīni karmāṇi raja aupasarjana tamaḥ pradhānasya śūdrasya śuśrūṣā eva karma iti  evam guṇa karma vibhāga śaś cāturguṇyam mayā sṛṣṭam iti  arthaḥ tad  ca idam cāturvarṇyam na anyeṣu lokeṣu atas  mānuṣe loke iti viśeṣaṇam hanta tarhi cāturvarṇya sarga ādeḥ karmaṇaḥ kartṛ tvāt tad phalena yujyase atas  na tvam nitya muktaḥ  nityeśvaraś ca iti ucyate yadi api māyā saṃvyavahāreṇa tasya karmaṇaḥ kartāram api santam mām paramārtha taḥ  viddhi  akartāram ataeva avyayam asaṃsāriṇam ca mām viddhi yeṣām tu karmaṇām kartāram mām manyase paramārtha taḥ  teṣām akartā eva aham yatas  na mām tāni karmāṇi limpanti deha ādi ārambhaka tvena ahaṅkāra abhāvāt na ca teṣām karmaṇām phale me mama spṛhā tṛṣṇā yeṣām tu saṃsāriṇām aham kartā iti  ābhimānaḥ karmasu spṛhā tad phaleṣu ca tān karmāṇi limpanti iti yuktam tad abhāvān na mām karmāṇi limpanti iti evam yaḥ  anye api mām ātma tvena abhijānāti na aham kartā na me karma phale spṛhā iti na karmabhiḥ  na badhyate tasya api na deha ādi ārambhakāni karmāṇi bhavanti iti  arthaḥ na aham kartā na me karma phale spṛhā iti evam jñātvā kṛtam karma pūrvaiḥ  api  atikrāntaiḥ  mumukṣubhiḥ kuru tena karma eva tvam na tuṣṇīm āsanam na api saṃnyāsaḥ kartavyaḥ tasmāt  tvad pūrvaiḥ  api  anuṣṭhita tvāt  yadi  anātma jñas tvam tad  ātma śuddhi artham tattva vid  ced  loka saṃgraha artham pūrve janaka ādibhiḥ pūrvataram kṛtam na adhunātana kṛtam nivartitam tatra karma ced  kartavyam tvad vacanāt  eva karomi  aham kim viśeṣitena pūrvaiḥ pūrvataram kṛtam iti ucyate kim karma kim ca akarma iti kavayaḥ  medhāvinaḥ  api  atra asmin karma ādi viṣaye mohitā moham gatāḥ atas te tubhyam aham karma akarma ca pravakṣyāmi yaj jñātvā viditvā karma ādi mokṣyase aśubhāt  saṃsārāt  na ca etad  tvayā mantavyam karma nāma deha ādi ceṣṭā loka prasiddham akarma nāma tad akriyā tūṣṇīm āsanam kim tatra boddhavyam iti kasmāt  ucyate karmaṇaḥ śāstra vihitasya hi yasmāt  api  asti boddhavyam boddhavyam ca asti  eva vikarmaṇaḥ pratiṣiddhasya tathā akarmaṇaḥ  ca tūṣṇīmbhā  asya boddhavyam asti iti triṣu  api  adhyāhāraḥ kartavyaḥ yasmāt  gahanā viṣamā durjñānā karmaṇa iti  upalakṣaṇa artham karma ādīnām karma akarma vikarmaṇām gatiḥ  yāthātmyam tattvam iti  arthaḥ kim punar  tattvam karma ādeḥ  yad  boddhavyam vakṣyāmi iti pratijñātam ucyate karmaṇi karma kriyata iti karma vyāpāra mātram tasmin karmaṇi  akarma karma abhāvam yaḥ paśyet  akarmaṇi ca karma abhāve kartṛ tantra tvāt pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ  vastu  aprāpya eva hi sarva eva kriyā kāraka ādi vyavahāraḥ  avidyā bhūmau   eva karma yaḥ paśyet  paśyati sa buddhimān manuṣyeṣu sa yuktaḥ  yogī ca kṛtsna karma kṛt  samasta karma kṛt  ca sa iti stūyate karma akarmaṇoḥ  itaretara darśī nanu kim idam viruddham ucyate karmaṇi  akarma yaḥ paśyet  iti akarmaṇi ca karma iti na hi karma akarma syāt  akarma vā karma tatra viruddham katham paśyet  draṣṭā na akarma eva paramārthataḥ sat karmavat  avabhāsate mūḍha dṛṣṭeḥ  lokasya tathā karma eva akarmavat  tatra yathābhūta darśana artham āha bhagavān karmaṇi  akarma yaḥ paśyet  iti  ādi atas  na viruddham buddhimattva ādi upapatteḥ  ca boddhavyam iti ca yathābhūta darśanam ucyate na ca viparīta jñānāt  aśubhān mokṣaṇam syāt  yaj jñātvā mokṣyase aśubhāt  iti ca uktam tasmāt  karmākarmaṇī viparyayeṇa gṛhīte prāṇibhiḥ  tad viparyaya grahaṇa nivṛtti artham bhagavataḥ  vacanam karmaṇi  akarma yaḥ iti  ādi na ca atra karma adhikaraṇa karma asti kuṇḍe badarāṇi iva na api  akarma adhikaraṇam karma asti karma abhāva tvāt  akarmaṇaḥ atas  viparīta gṛhīte eva karmākarmaṇī laukikaiḥ yathā mṛgatṛṣṇikāyām udakam śuktikāyām vā rajatam nanu karma karma eva sarveṣām na kvacid  vyabhicarati tad  na nausthasya nāvi gacchantyām taṭa sthesv agatiṣu nageṣu pratikūla gati darśanāt  dūreṣu cakṣuṣā āsannikṛṣṭeṣu gacchatsu gati abhāva darśanāt  evam iha api  akarmaṇi  aham karomi iti karma darśanam karmaṇi ca akarma darśanam viparīta darśanam yena tad nirākaraṇa artham ucyate karmaṇi  akarma yaḥ paśyet  iti  ādi tad  etad  ukta prativacanam api  asakṛt  atyanta viparīta darśana bhāvita tayā momuhyamānaḥ  lokaḥ śrutam api  asakṛt  tattvam vismṛtya vismṛtya mithyā prasaṅgam avatārya avatārya codayati iti punar  punar  uttaram āha bhagavān durvijñeya tvam ca ālakṣya vastunaḥ avyaktaḥ  ayam acintyaḥ  ayam na jāyate mriyate iti  ādina ātmani karma abhāvaḥ śruti smṛti nyāya prasiddha  uktaḥ  vakṣyamāṇaḥ  ca tasmin   ātmani karma abhāve akarmaṇi karma viparīta darśanam atyanta nirūḍham yatas  kim karma kim akarma iti kavayaḥ  api  atra mohitāḥ deha ādi āśrayam karma ātmani  adhyāropya aham kartā mama etad  karma mayā asya karmaṇaḥ phalam bhoktavyam iti ca tathā aham tūṣṇīm bhavāmi yena aham nirāyāsaḥ  akarmā sukhī syām iti kārya karaṇa āśraya vyāpāra uparamam tad kṛtam casukhi tvam ātmani  adhyāropya na karomi kiṃcid  tūṣṇīm sukham āsam iti  abhimanyate lokaḥ tatra idam lokasya viparīta darśana apanayanāya āha bhagavān karmaṇi  akarma yaḥ paśyet  iti  ādi atra ca karma karma eva sat  kārya karaṇa āśrayam karma rahitaḥ  avikriya ātmani sarvaiḥ  adhyastam yatas  paṇḍitaḥ  api  aham karomi iti manyate atha ātma samaveta tayā sarva loka prasiddhe karmaṇi nadī kula stheṣu  iva gatiḥ pratilaumyena atas  akarma karma abhāvam yathābhūtam gati abhāvam iva vṛkṣeṣu yaḥ paśyet  akarmaṇi ca kārya karaṇa vyāpāra uparame karmavat  ātmani  adhyāropite tūṣṇīm akurvan sukham āse iti  ahaṅkāra abhisandhi hetu tvāt tasmin   akarmaṇi ca karma yaḥ paśyet  ya evam karma akarma vibhāga jñaḥ sa buddhimān paṇḍitaḥ  manuṣyeṣu sa yuktaḥ  yogī kṛtsna karma kṛt  ca saḥ  aśubhān mokṣitaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ  bhavati iti  arthaḥ ayam ślokaḥ  anyathā vyākhyātaḥ kaiścid  katham nityānām kila karmaṇām īśvara arthe anuṣṭhīyamānānām tad phala abhāvāt  akarmāṇi tāni  ucyante gauṇyā vṛttyā teṣām ca akaraṇam akarma tad  ca pratyavāya phala tvāt  karma ucyate gauṇyā eva vṛttyā tatra nitye karmaṇi  akarma yaḥ paśyet  phala abhāvāt yathā dhenuḥ  api gauḥ  agauḥ  ucyate kṣīra ākhyam phalam na prayacchati iti tadvat  tathā nityākaraṇe tu  akarmaṇi karmaḥ āśyet  naraka ādi pratyavāya phalam prayacchati iti na etad  yuktam vyākhyānam evaṃjñānāt  aśubhān mokṣa anupapatteḥ yaj jñātvā mokṣyase aśubhāt  iti bhagavatā uktam vacanam bodhyeta katham nityānām anuṣṭhānāt  aśubhāt  syāt  nāma mokṣaṇam na tu teṣām phala abhāva jñānāt na hi nityānām phala abhāva jñānam aśubha mukti phala tvena coditam nitya karma jñānam vā na ca bhagavati veha uktam etena akarmaṇi karma darśanam pratyuktam na hi  akarmaṇi karma iti darśanam kartavyatayā iha codyate nityasya tu kartavyatā mātram na ca akaraṇān nityasya pratyavāyaḥ  bhavati iti vijñānāt  kiṃcid  phalam syāt  na api nitya akaraṇam jñeya tvena coditam na api karma akarma iti mithā darśanāt  aśubhān mokṣaṇam buddhimat tvam yukta tā kṛtsna karma kṛttva ādi ca phalam upapadyate stutiḥ  vā mithyājñānam eva hi sākṣāt  aśubha rūpam kutaḥ anyasmāt  aśubhān mokṣaṇam na hi tamas tamasaḥ  nivartakam bhavati nanu karmaṇi yad  akarma darśanam akarmaṇi vā karma darśanam na tad mithyā jñānam kim tarhi gauṇam phala bhāva abhāva nimittam na karma akarma vijñānāt  api gauṇāt  phalasya aśravaṇāt  na api śruta hānya śruta parikalpanayā kaścid  viśeṣaḥ  labhyate sva śabdena api śakyam vaktum nitya karmaṇām phalam na asti  akaraṇāt  ca teṣām naraka pātaḥ syāt  iti tatra vyājena para vyāmoha rūpeṇa karmaṇi  akarma yaḥ paśyet  iti  ādinā kim tatra eva vyācakṣāṇena bhagavatā uktam vākyam loka vyāmoha artham iti vyaktam kalpitam syāt  na ca etad  chadma rūpeṇa vākyena rakṣaṇīyam vastu na api śabda antareṇa punar  punar  ucyamānam su bodham syāt  iti  evam vaktum yuktam karmaṇi  eva adhikāra s te iti  atra hi sphuṭatara uktaḥ  arthaḥ  na punar  vaktavyaḥ  bhavati sarvatra ca praśastam boddhavyam ca kartavyam eva na niṣprayojanam boddhavyam iti  ucyate na ca mithyājñānam boddhavyam bhavati tad pratyupasthāpitam vā vastu ābhāsam na api nityānām akaraṇāt  abhāvāt  prayavāya bhāva utpattiḥ na asataḥ  vidyate bhāvaḥ iti vacanāt  tad katham asataḥ saj jāyate iti ca darśitam asataḥ sat janma pratiṣedhāt  asataḥ sat utpattim bruvatā asat  eva sat  bhavet  sac ca asat  bhavet  iti  uktam syāt  tad  ca ayuktam sarva pramāṇa virodhāt na ca niṣphalam vidadhyāt  karma śāstram duḥkha svarūpa tvāt duḥkhasya ca buddhi pūrvaka tayā kāryatva anupapatteḥ tad akaraṇe ca naraka pāta abhyupagame anarthāya eva ubhayathā api karaṇe akaraṇe ca śāstram niṣphalam kalpitam syāt  sva abhyupagama virodhaḥ  ca nityam niṣphalam karma iti  abhyupagamya mokṣa phalāya iti bruvataḥ tasmāt  yathāśruta eva arthaḥ karmaṇi  akarma ya iti  ādeḥ tathā ca vyākhyātaḥ  asmābhiḥ ślokaḥ tad  etad  karmaṇi  akarma ādi darśanam stūyate yasya yathā ukta darśinaḥ sarve yāvantaḥ samārambhāḥ karmāṇi samārabhyanta iti samārambhāḥ kāma saṃkalpa varjitāḥ kāmaiḥ tad kāraṇaiḥ  ca saṅkalpa varjitā mudhā eva ceṣṭā mātrā anuṣṭhīyante pravṛttena cel loka saṅgraha artham nivṛttena ced  jīvana mātra artham tam jñāna agni dagdha karmāṇam karma ādau   akarma ādi darśanam jñānam tad  eva agni s tena jñāna agninā dagdhāni śubha aśubha lakṣaṇāni karmāṇi yasya tam āhuḥ paramārthataḥ paṇḍitam budhāḥ brahma vidaḥ yaḥ  tu karma ādau   akarma ādi darśī saḥ  akarma ādi darśanāt  eva niṣkarmā sannyāsī jīvana mātra artha ceṣṭaḥ san karmaṇi na pravartate yadi api prāk vivekataḥ pravṛttaḥ yaḥ  tu prārabdha karmā san   uttara kālam utpanna ātma samyak darśanaḥ syāt  sa sarva karmaṇi prayojanam apaśyan sa sādhanam karma pariyajati  eva sa kutaścin nimittāt  karma parityāga asambhave sati karmaṇi tad phale ca saṅga rahita tayā sva prayojana abhāvāl loka saṅgraha artham pūrvavat  karmaṇi pravṛttaḥ  api na eva kiṃcid  karoti jñāna agni dagdha karma tvāt  tadīyam karma akarma eva sampadyata iti  etam artham darśayiṣyan   āha tyaktvā karmasu  abhimānam phala āsaṅgam ca yathā uktena jñānena nitya tṛptaḥ  nirākāṅkṣaḥ  viṣayeṣu  iti  arthaḥ nirāśraya āśraya rahitaḥ āśrayaḥ  nāma yad  āśritya puruṣa artham sisādhayiṣati dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa phala sādhana āśraya rahita iti  arthaḥ viduṣā kriyamāṇam karma paramārtha taḥ  akarma eva tasya niṣkriya ātma darśana sampanna tvāt  tena evambhūtena sva prayojana abhāvāt sa sādhanam karma parityaktavyam eva iti prāpte tatas  nirgama asambhavāl loka saṅgraha cikīrṣayā śiṣṭa vigarhaṇa aparijihīrṣayā vā pūrvavat  karmaṇi abhipravṛttaḥ  api niṣkrya ātma darśana sampanna tvān na eva kiṃcid  karoti saḥ yaḥ punar  pūrva ukta viparītaḥ prāk  eva karma ambhāt  brahmaṇi sarva antare pratyagātmani niṣkriye saṃjāta ātma darśanaḥ sa dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa iṣṭa viṣaya āśīr vivarjita tayā dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa arthe karmaṇi prayojanam api aśyan sa sādhanam karma saṃnyasya śarīra yātrā mātra ceṣṭaḥ  yatiḥ  jñāna niṣṭhaḥ mucyata iti etad  artham darśayitum āha nirāśīḥ  nirgatā āśiṣaḥ yasmāt  sa nirāśīḥ yata citta ātmā cittam antaḥkaraṇam ātmā bāhyaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ tau   ubhau   api yatau saṃyatau yasya sa yata citta ātmā tyakta sarva parigrahaḥ tyaktaḥ sarvaḥ parigrahaḥ  yena sa tyakta sarva parigrahaḥ śārīram śarīra sthiti mātra prayojanam kevalam tatra api abhimāna varjitam karma kurvan na āpnoti na prāpnoti kilbiṣam aniṣṭa rūpam pāpam dharmam ca dharmaḥ  api mumukṣoḥ  aniṣṭa rūpam kilbiṣam eva bandha āpādaka tvāt  tasmāt  tābhyām muktaḥ  bhavati saṃsārān muktaḥ  bhavati iti  arthaḥ kim ca śārīram kevalam karma iti  atra kim śarīra nirvartyam śārīram karma abhipretam āhaḥ svi c charīra sthiti mātra prayojanam śārīram karma iti kim cātas  yadi śarīra nirvartyam śārīram karma yadi vā śarīra sthiti mātra prayojanam śarīram iti ucyate yadā śarīra nirvartyam karma śārīram abhipretam syāt  tadā dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa prayojanam karma pratiṣiddham api śarīreṇa kurvan na āpnoti kilbiṣam iti bruvataḥ  viruddha abhidhānam prasajyeta śāstrī iyam ca karma dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa prayojanam śarīreṇa kurvan na āpnoti kilbiṣam iti  api bruvataḥ  aprāpta pratiṣedha prasaṅgaḥ śārīram karma kurvan iti viśeṣaṇāt  kevala śabda prayoga āt  ca vāc manasa nirvartyam karma vidhi pratiṣedha viṣayam dharma adharma śabda vācyam kurvan prāpnoti kilbiṣam iti  uktam syāt  tatra api vāc manasābhyām vihita anuṣṭhāna pakṣe kilbiṣa prāpti vacanam viruddham āpadyeta pratiṣiddha sevi pakṣe api bhūta artha anuvāda mātram anarthakam syāt  yadā tu śarīra sthiti mātra prayojanam śārīram karma abhipretam bhavet  tadā dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa prayojanam karma vidhi pratiṣedha gamyam śarīra vāc manasa nirvartyam anyat  akruvan   taiḥ  eva śarīra ādibhiḥ śarīra sthiti mātra prayojanam kevala śabda prayogāt  aham karomi iti  abhimāna varjitaḥ śarīra ādi ceṣṭā mātram loka dṛṣṭyā kurvan na āpnoti kilbiṣam evambhūtasya pāpa śabda vācya kilbiṣa prāpti asambhavāt  kilbiṣam saṃsāram na āpnoti jñāna agni dagdha sarva karma tvāt  apratibandhena mucyate eva iti pūrva ukta samyak darśana phala anuvāda eva eṣaḥ evam śarīram kevalam karma iti  asya arthasya parigrahe niravadyam bhavati tyakta sarva parigrahasya yateḥ  anna ādeḥ śarīra sthiti hetorḥ parigrahasya abhāvāt  yācana ādinā śarīra sthitau kartavyatāyām prāptāyām ayācitam asaṃk ptam upapannam yadṛcchayā iti  ādinā vacanena anujñātam yateḥ śarīra sthiti hetoḥ  anna ādeḥ prāpti dvāram āviṣkurvan   āha yadṛcchā lābha santuṣṭaḥ prārthita upanataḥ  lābhaḥ  yadṛcchā lābhaḥ tena santuṣṭaḥ saṃjāta alaṃpratyayaḥ dvandva atītaḥ  dvandvaiḥ śīta uṣṇa ādibhiḥ  hanyamānaḥ  api  aviṣaṇṇa cittaḥ  dvandva atīta ucyate vimatsaraḥ  vigata mat saraḥ  nirvaira buddhiḥ samas tulyaḥ  yadṛcchā lābhasya siddhau   asiddhau ca ya evambhūtaḥ  yatiḥ  anna ādeḥ śarīra sthiti hetoḥ  lābha alābhayoḥ samaḥ  harṣa viṣāda varjitaḥ karma ādau   akarma ādi darśī yathābhūta ātma darśana niṣṭhaḥ san śarīra sthiti mātra prayojane bhikṣāṭana ādi karmaṇi śarīra ādi nirvartye na eva kiṃcid  karomi iti guṇā guṇeṣu vartanta iti  evam sadā samparicakṣāṇa ātmanaḥ kartṛtva abhāvam paśyan   eva kiṃcid  bhikṣāṭana ādikam karma karoti loka vyavahāra sāmānya darśanena tu laukikaiḥ  āropita kartṛ tve bhikṣāṭana ādau karmaṇi kartā bhavati sva anubhavena tu śāstra pramāṇa ādi janitena akartrā eva sa evam parādhi āropita kartṛ tvam śarīra sthiti mātra prayojanam bhikṣāṭana ādikam karma kṛtvā api na nibadhyate bandha hetoḥ karmaṇaḥ sa hetukasya jñāna agninā dagdha tvāt  iti  ukta anuvāda eva eṣaḥ tyaktvā karma phala āsaṅgam iti  anena ślokena yaḥ prārabdha karmā san yadā niṣkriya brahma ātma darśana sampannaḥ syāt  tadā tasya ātmanaḥ kartṛ karma prayojana abhāva darśinaḥ karma parityāge prāpte kutaścin nimittāt  tad asambhave sati pūrvavat  tasmin karmaṇi  abhipravṛttasya api na eva kiṃcid  karoti sa iti karma abhāvaḥ pradarśitaḥ yasya evam karma abhāvaḥ  darśita s tasya eva gata saṅgasya sarvatas  nivṛtta āsakteḥ  muktasya nivṛtta dharma adharma ādi bandhanasya jñāna avasthita cetasaḥ  jñāna eva avasthitam cetaḥ  yasya saḥ  ayam jñāna avasthita cetāḥ tasya yajñāya yajña nirvṛtti artham ācarataḥ  nirvartayataḥ karma samagram saha agreṇa phalena vartata iti samagram karma tad samagram pravilīyate vinaśyati iti  arthaḥ kasmāt  punar  kāraṇāt  kriyamāṇam karma sva kārya ārambham akurvat  samagram pravilīyata iti  ucyate yatas  brahma arpaṇam yena karaṇena brahma vid havir agnau   arpayati tad  brahma eva iti paśyati tasya ātma vyatirekeṇa abhāvam paśyati yathā śuktikāyām rajata abhāvam paśyati tad  ucyate brahma eva arpaṇam iti yathā yad  rajatam tad  chuktikā eva iti brahma arpaṇam iti  asamaḥ te pade yad arpaṇa buddhyā gṛhyate loke tad  asya brahma vidaḥ  brahma eva iti  arthaḥ brahma havis tathā yad  dhaviḥ  buddhyā gṛhyamāṇam tad  brahma eva asay tathā brahma agnau iti samastam padam agniḥ  api brahmā eva yatra hūyate brahmaṇā kartrā brahmā eva kartā iti  arthaḥ yad  tena hutam havana kriyā tad  brahmā eva yad  tena gantavyam phalam tad  api brahmā eva brahma karma samādhinā brahmā eva karma brahma karma tasmin samādhiḥ  yasya sa brahma karma samādhiḥ  tena brahma karma samādhinā brahmā eva gantavyam evam loka saṅgraham cikīrṣuṇā api kriyamāṇam karam paramārtha taḥ  akarma brahma buddhi upamṛditvāt evam sati nivṛtta karmaṇaḥ  api sarva karma san  yāsinaḥ samyak darśanastuti artham yajñatva sampādanam jñānasya sutarām upapadyate yad arpaṇa ādi adhiyajñe prasiddham tad  asya adhyātmam brahmā eva parama artha darśina iti anyathā sarvasya brahma tve arpaṇa ādīnām eva viśeṣataḥ  brahmatva abhidhānam anarthakam syāt  tasmāt  brahma eva idam sarvam iti  abhijānataḥ  viduṣaḥ sarva karma abhāvaḥ kāraka buddhi abhāvāt  ca na hi kāraka buddhi rahitam yajña ākhyam karma dṛṣṭam sarvam eva agnihotra ādikam karma śabda samarpita devatā viśeṣa sampradāna ādi kāraka buddhimat kartṛ abhimāna phala abhisandhim ac ca dṛṣṭam na upamṛdita kriyā kāraka phala bheda buddhimat  kartṛtva abhimāna phala abhisandhirahitam vā idam tu brahma buddhi upamṛdita arpaṇa ādi kāraka kriyā phala bheda buddhi karma atas akarma eva tad  tathā ca darśitam karmaṇi  akarma yaḥ paśyet  karmaṇi  abhipravṛttaḥ  api na eva kiṃcid  karoti saḥ guṇā guṇeṣu vartante na eva kiṃcid  karomi iti yuktaḥ  manyeta tattva vid  iti  ādibhiḥ tathā ca darśayan   tatra tatra kriyā kāraka phala bheda buddhi upamardam karoti dṛṣṭā ca kāmya agni hotra ādau kāma upamardena kāmya agnihotra ādi ha āniḥ tathā mati pūrvakām ati pūrvaka ādīnām karmaṇām kārya viśeṣasya ārambhaka tvam dṛṣṭam tathā iha api brahma buddhi upamṛdita arpaṇa ādi kāraka kriyā phala bheda buddheḥ  bāhya ceṣṭā mātreṇa karma api viduṣaḥ  akarma sampadyate ata uktam samagram pravilīyate iti atra kecid  āhuḥ yad  brahma tad  arpaṇa ādīni brahmā eva kila arpaṇa ādinā pañcavidhena kāraka ātmanā vyavasthitam sat  tad  eva karma karoti tatra na arpaṇa ādi buddhiḥ  nivartyate kintv arpaṇa ādiṣu brahma buddhiḥ  ādhīyate yathā pratimā ādau viṣṇu ādi buddhiḥ yathā vā nāma ādau brahma buddhiḥ  iti satyam evam api syāt  yadi jñāna yajña stuti artham prakaraṇam na syāt  atra tu samyak darśanam jñāna yajña śabditam anekān yajña śabditān kriyā viśeṣān upanyasya śreyān dravya mayād yajñāj jñāna yajñaḥ parantapa iti jñānam stauti atra ca samartham idam vacanam brahma arpaṇam iti  ādi jñānasya yajñatva sampādane anyathā sarvasya brahma tve arpaṇa ādīnām eva viśeṣataḥ  brahmatva abhidhānam anarthakam syāt  ye tu  arpaṇa ādiṣu pratimāyām viṣṇu dṛṣṭivat  brahma dṛṣṭiḥ kṣipyate nāma ādiṣu  iva ca iti bruvate na teṣām brahma vidyā uktā iha vivakṣitā syāt  arpaṇa ādi viṣaya tvāt  jñānasya na ca dṛṣṭi sampādana jñānena mokṣa phalam prāpyate brahmā eva tena gantavyam iti ca ucyate viruddham ca samyak darśanam antareṇa mokṣa phalam prāpyata iti prakṛti virodhaḥ  ca samyak darśanam ca prakṛtam karmaṇi  akarma yaḥ paśyet  iti  atra ante ca samyak darśanam tasya eva upasaṃhārāt  śreyān dravya mayād yajñāj jñāna yajñaḥ parantapa jñānam labdhvā parām śāntim iti  ādinā samyak darśana stutim eva kurvan   upakṣīṇaḥ  adhyāyaḥ tatra akasmāt  arpaṇa ādau brahma dṛṣṭiḥ  aprakaraṇe pratimāyām iva viṣṇu dṛṣṭiḥ  ucyata iti  anupapannam tasmāt  yathāvyākhyāta artha eva ayam ślokaḥ tatra adhunā samyak darśanasya yajña tvam sampādya tad stuti artham anye api yajñā upakṣipyante daivam eva devāḥ  ijyante yena yajñena asau daivaḥ  yajñas tam eva apare yajñam yoginaḥ karmiṇaḥ paryupāsate kurvanti iti  arthaḥ brahma agnau satyam jñānam anantam brahma vijñānam ānandam brahma yad  sākṣāt  aparokṣāt  brahma ya ātmā sarva antaraḥ iti  ādi vacana uktam aśanāyā pipāsā ādi sarva saṃsāra dharma varjitam na iti na iti iti nirasta aśeṣa viśeṣam brahma śabdena ucyate brahma ca tad agniḥ  ca sa homa adhikaraṇatva vivakṣayā brahma agni s tasmin brahma agnau   apare anye brahma vidaḥ  yajñam yajña śabda vācya ātmā ātmanām asu yajña śabdasya pāṭhāt  tam ātmānam yajñam paramārthataḥ param eva brahma santam buddhi ādi upādhi saṃyuktam adhyasta sarva upādhi dharmakam āhuti rūpam yajṇinā eva ātmanā eva ukta lakṣaṇa upajuhvati prakṣipanti sa upādhikasya ātmanaḥ  nirupādhikena para brahma svarūpeṇa eva yad  darśanam sa tasmin homa s tam kurvanti brahma ātmā ekatva darśana niṣṭhāḥ sannyāsina iti  arthaḥ saḥ  ayam samyak darśana lakṣaṇaḥ  yajñaḥ  daiva yajña ādiṣu yajñeṣu upakṣipyante brahma arpaṇam iti  ādślokaiḥ prastutaḥ śreyān dravya mayād yajñāj jñāna yajñaḥ parantapa iti  ādinā stuti artham śrotra ādīni indriyāṇi  anye yoginaḥ saṃyama agniṣu pratīndriyam saṃyamaḥ  bhidyata iti bahuvacanam saṃyamā eva agnayaḥ  teṣu juhvati indriya saṃyamam eva kurvanti iti  arthaḥ śabda ādīn viṣayān anya indriya agniṣu juhvati indriyāṇi  eva agnayaḥ  teṣu  indriya agniṣu juhvati śrotra ādibhiḥ  aviruddha viṣaya grahaṇam homam manyante kiṃca sarvāṇi indriya karmāṇi indriyāṇām karmāṇi indriya karmāṇi tathā prāṇa karmāṇi prāṇaḥ  vāyuḥ  ādhyātmikaḥ  tad karmāṇi  ākuñcana prasāraṇa ādīni tāni ca apara ātma saṃyama yoga agnau ātmani saṃyama ātma saṃyamaḥ sa eva yoga agni s tasmin   ātma saṃyama yoga agnau yajñāḥ tapaḥ yajñās tapaḥ  yajñaḥ  yeṣām tapasvinām te tapaḥ yajñāḥ yoga yajñāḥ prāṇāyāma pratyāhāra ādi lakṣaṇaḥ  yogaḥ  yajñaḥ  yeṣām te yoga yajñāḥ tathā apare svādhyāya jñāna yajñāḥ  ca svādhyāyaḥ  yathāvidhi ṛc ādi abhyāsaḥ  yajñaḥ  yeṣām te svādhyāya yajñāḥ jñāna yajñā jñānam śāstra artha parijñānam yajñaḥ  yeṣām te jñāna yajñāḥ svādhyāya yajñā jñāna yajñāḥ  ca yatayaḥ  yatana śīlāḥ śaṃsita vratāḥ samyak  śitāni tanūkṛtāni tīkṣṇīkṛtāni vratāni yeṣām te saṃśita vratāḥ kiṃca apāne apāna vṛttau juhvati pratikṣipanti prāṇam prāṇa vṛttim pūraka ākhyam prāṇāyāmam kurvanti iti  arthaḥ prāṇe apānam tathā apare juhvati recaka ākhyam ca prāṇāyāmam kurvanti iti  etad  prāṇa apāna gatī mukhya nāsikābhyām vāyoḥ  nirgamanam prāṇasya gati s tad viparyayeṇa adhas gamanam apānasya gati s te prāṇa prāṇān vāyu bhedān prāṇeṣu  eva juhvati yasya yasya vāyoḥ  jayaḥ kriyata itarān vāyu bhedān tasmin tasmin juhvati te tatra praviṣṭā iva bhavanti sarve api  ete yajña vidaḥ  yajña kṣapita kalmaṣā yajñaiḥ  yathā uktaiḥ kṣapitaḥ  nāśitaḥ kalmaṣaḥ  yeṣām te yajña kṣapita kalmaṣāḥ evam yathā uktān yajñān nirvatrya yajña śiṣṭa amṛta bhujaḥ  yajñānām śiṣṭam yajña śiṣṭam yajña śiṣṭam ca tad  amṛtam gacchanti brahma sanātanam cirantanam mumukṣa vaḥ  ced  kāla atikrama apekṣayā iti sāmarthyāt  gamyate na ayam lokaḥ sarva prāṇi sādhāraṇaḥ  api  asti yathā uktānām yajñānām ekaḥ  api yajñaḥ  yasya na asti saḥ  ayajñas tasya kutaḥ anyaḥ  viśiṣṭa sādhana sādhyaḥ kuru sattama evam yathā uktā bahuvidhā bahu prakārā yajñā vitatā vistīrṇā brahmaṇaḥ  vedasya mukhe dvāre vedadvāreṇa avagamyamānā brahmaṇaḥ  mukhe vitatā ucyante tad  yathā vāci hi prāṇam juhumaḥ iti  ādayaḥ karma jān kāyika vācika mānasa karma udbhavān viddhi tān sarvān anātmajān nirvyāpāraḥ  hi  ātmā ata evam jñātvā vimokṣyase aśubhāt bhasmīkartum śaknoti tasmāt  samyak  darśanam sarva karmaṇām nirbīja tve kāraṇam iti  abhiprāyaḥ sāmarthyāt  yena karmaṇā arīram ārabdham tad  pravṛtta phala tvāt  upabhogena eva kṣīyate tasya tāvat darśanāt  kṣipram eva mokṣaḥ  bhavati iti sarva śāstra nyāya prasiddhaḥ su niścitaḥ  arthaḥ atra saṃśayaḥ  na kartavyaḥ pāpiṣṭhaḥ  hi saṃśayaḥ katham iti  ucyate ajñaś ca anātma jñaḥ  ca aśraddadhānaḥ  ca guru vākya śāstreṣu  aviśvāsavānś ca saṃśaya ātmā ca saṃśaya citta ś ca vinaśyati ajña aśraddadhānau yadi api vinaśyataḥ na tathā yathā saṃśaya ātmā saṃśaya ātmā tu pāpiṣṭhaḥ sarveṣām katham na ayam sādhāraṇaḥ  api lokaḥ  asti tathā na paraḥ  lokaḥ na sukham tatra api saṃśaya utpatteḥ saṃśaya ātmanaḥ saṃśaya cittasya tasmāt  saṃśayaḥ  na kartavyaḥ kasmāt  yoga saṃnyasta karmāṇam parama artha darśana lakṣaṇena yogena saṃnyastāni karmāṇi yena parama artha darśinā dharma adharma ākhyāni tam yoga saṃnyasta karmāṇam katham yoga saṃnyasta karmā iti  āha jñāna saṃchinna saṃśayam jñānena ātma īśvara ekatva darśana lakṣaṇena saṃchinnaḥ saṃśayaḥ  yasya yaḥ  jñāna saṃchinna saṃśayaḥ ya evam yoga saṃnyasta karmā tam ātmavantam apramattam guṇa ceṣṭā rūpeṇa dṛṣṭāni karmāṇi na nibadhnanti  aniṣṭa ādi rūpam phalam na ārabhante he dhanaṃjaya yasmāt  karma yoga anuṣṭhānāt  aśuddhi kṣaya hetuka jñāna saṃchinna saṃśayaḥ  na nibadhyate karmabhiḥ  jñāna agni dagdha karma tvāt  eva yasmāt  ca jñāna karma anuṣṭhāna viṣaye saṃśayavān vinaśyati tasmāt  pāpiṣṭham ajñāna saṃbhūtam ajñānāt  avivekāj jātam hṛd stham hṛdi buddhau sthitam jñāna asinā śoka moha ādi doṣa haram samyak  darśanam jñānam tad  eva asiḥ khaḍga s tena jñāna asinā ātmanaḥ svasya ātma viṣaya tvāt  saṃśayasya na hi parasya saṃśayaḥ pareṇa cchettavyatām prāptaḥ yena svasya iti viśeṣyeta ata ātma viṣayaḥ  api svasya eva bhavati chittvā enam saṃśayam sva vināśa hetu bhūtam yogam samyak darśana upāyam karma anuṣṭhānam ātiṣṭha kurv iti  arthaḥ uttiṣṭha ca idānīm yuddhāya bhārata iti saṃnyāsam parityāgam karmaṇām āstrīyāṇām anuṣṭheya viśeṣāṇām śaṃsasi praśaṃsasi kathayasi iti  etad  punar  yogam ca teṣām eva anuṣṭhānam avaśya kartavyam śaṃsasi atas  me katarat  śreyaḥ iti saṃśayaḥ kim karma anuṣṭhānam śreyaḥ kim vā tad hānam iti praśasyataram ca anuṣṭheyam atas  ca yad  śreyaḥ praśasyataram etayoḥ karma saṃnyāsa karma yogayoḥ  yad anuṣṭhānāt śreyaḥ  avāptiḥ  mama syāt  iti manyase tad  ekam anyatarat  saha eka puruṣa anuṣṭheyatva asaṃbhavāt me brūhi su niścitam abhipretam tava iti sva abhiprāyam ācakṣāṇaḥ  nirṇayāya śrī bhagavān uvāca saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇām parityāgaḥ karma yogaḥ  ca teṣām anuṣṭhānam tau   ubhau   api niḥśreyasa karau mokṣam kurvāte jñāna utpatti hetu tvena ubhau yadi api niḥśreyasa karau tathā api tayoḥ  tu niḥśreyasa hetvoḥ karma saṃnyāsāt  kevalāt  karma yogaḥ  viśiṣyata iti karma yogam stauti kasmāt  iti āha jñeyaḥ  jñātavyaḥ sa karma yogī nitya saṃnyāsī iti yaḥ  na dveṣṭi kiṃcid  na kāṅkṣati duḥkha sukhe tad sādhane ca evaṃvidhaḥ  yaḥ karmaṇi vartamānaḥ  api sa nitya saṃnyāsī iti jñātavya iti  arthaḥ nirdvandvaḥ  dvandva varjitaḥ  hi yasmāt  mahā bāhaḥ sukham bandhāt  anāyāsena pramucyate saṃnyāsa karma yogayoḥ  bhinna puruṣa anuṣṭheyayoḥ  viruddhayoḥ phale api virodhaḥ  yuktaḥ na tu ubhayoḥ  niḥśreyasa kara tvam eva iti prāpta idam ucyate sāṃkhya yogau pṛthak  viruddha bhinna phalau bālāḥ pravadanti na paṇḍitāḥ paṇḍitā aḥ  tu jñānina ekam phalam aviruddham icchanti katham ekam api sāṃkhya yogayoḥ samyak  āsthitaḥ samyak  anuṣṭhitavān iti  arthaḥ ubhayoḥ  vindate phalam ubhayoḥ  tad  eva hi niḥśreyasam phalam atas  na phale virodhaḥ  asti nanu saṃnyāsa karma yoga śabdena prastutya sāṃkhya yogayoḥ phala eka tvam katham iha aprakṛtam bravīti na eṣa doṣaḥ yadi api  arjunena saṃnyāsam karma yogam ca kevalam abhipretya praśnaḥ kṛtaḥ bhagavān   tu tad aparityāgena eva sva abhipretam ca viśeṣam saṃyojya śabda antara vācya tayā prativacanam dadau sāṃkhya yogau   iti tau   eva saṃnyāsa karma yogau jñāna tad upāya sama buddhitva ādi saṃyuktau sāṃkhya yoga śabda vācyauv iti bhagavataḥ  matam atas  na aprakṛta prakriyā iti ekasya api samyak  anuṣṭhānāt  katham ubhayoḥ phalam vindate iti  ucyate yad  sāṃkhyaiḥ  jñāna niṣṭhaiḥ saṃnyāsibhiḥ prāpyate sthānam mokṣa ākhyam tad  yogaiḥ  api jñāna prāpti upāyatvena īśvare samarpya karmāṇi  ātmanaḥ phalam anabhisaṃdhāya anutiṣṭhanti ye te yogā yoginaḥ taiḥ  api parama artha jñāna saṃnyāsa prāpti dvāreṇa gamyata iti  abhiprāyaḥ ata ekam sāṅkhyam ca yogam ca yaḥ paśyati phala eka tvāt  sa paśyati samyak  paśyati iti  arthaḥ evam tarhi yogāt  saṃnyāsa eva viśiṣyate katham tarhi idam uktam tayoḥ  tu karma saṃnyāsāt  karma yogaḥ  viśiṣyate iti sṛṇu tatra kāraṇam tvayā pṛṣṭām kevalam karma saṃnyāsam karma yogam ca abhipretya tayoḥ  anyataraḥ kaḥ śreyān iti tad anurūpam prativacanam mayā uktam karma saṃnyāsāt  karma yogaḥ  viśiṣyate iti jñānam anapekṣya jñāna apekṣas tu saṃnyāsaḥ sāṃkhyam iti mayā abhipretaḥ parama artha yogaḥ  ca sa eva yaḥ  tu karma yogaḥ  vaidikaḥ sa ca tādarthyāt  yogaḥ saṃnyāsa iti ca upacaryate katham tādarthyam iti  ucyate saṃnyāsas tu pāramārthikaḥ  duḥkham āptum prāptum ayogataḥ  yogena vinā yoga yuktaḥ  vaidikena karma yogena vaidikena karma yogena īśvara samarpita rūpeṇa phala nirapekṣeṇa yuktaḥ  muniḥ mananād īśvara svarūpasya muniḥ brahma parama ātma jñāna niṣṭhā lakṣaṇa tvāt prakṛtaḥ saṃnyāsaḥ  brahmā ucyate nyāsa iti brahmā brahmā hi paraḥ iti śruteḥ brahma parama artha saṃnyāsam parama artha jñāna niṣṭhā lakṣaṇam na cireṇa kṣipram eva adhigacchati prāpnoti atas  mayā uktam karma yogaḥ  viśiṣyata iti yadā punar  ayam samyak darśana prāpti upāya tvena yogena yuktaḥ  yoga yuktaḥ  viśuddha ātmā viśuddha sattvaḥ  vijita ātmā vijita dehaḥ  jita indriyaḥ  ca sarva bhūta ātma bhūta ātmā sarveṣām brahma ādīnām stamba paryantānām bhūtānām ātma bhūta ātmā pratyak cetanaḥ  yasya sa sarva bhūta ātma bhūta ātmā samyak darśī iti  arthaḥ sa tatra evam vartamānaḥ  loka saṃgrahāya karma kurvan   api na lipyate na karmabhiḥ  badhyate iti  arthaḥ na ca asau paramārthataḥ karoti iti  atas  yuktaḥ samāhitaḥ san manyeta cintayet  tattva vid ātmanaḥ  yāthātmyam tattvam vetti iti tattva vid  parama artha darśī iti  arthaḥ kadā katham vā tattvam avadhārayan manyeta iti  ucyate manyeta iti pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ yasya evam tattva vidaḥ sarva kārya karaṇa ceṣṭāsu karmasu  akarma eva paśyataḥ samyak darśinaḥ  tasya sarva karma saṃnyāsa eva adhikāraḥ karmaṇaḥ  abhāva darśanāt  na hi mṛgatṛṣṇikāyām udaka buddhyā pānāya pravṛtta udaka abhāva jñāne api tatra eva pāna prayojanāya pravartate yaḥ  tu punar  atattva vid  pravṛttaś ca karma yoge brahmaṇi īśvara ādhāya nikṣipya tad artham karma karomi iti bhṛtya iva svāmi artham sarvāṇi karmāṇi mokṣe api phale saṅgam tyaktvā karoti yaḥ sarva karmāṇi lipyate na sa pāpena na saṃbadhyate padma patram iva ambha sodakena kevalam sattva śuddhi mātram eva phalam tasya karmaṇaḥ syāt  yasmāt  kāyena dehena manasā buddhyā ca kevalaiḥ  mamatva varjitaiḥ īśvarāya eva karma karomi na mama phalāya iti mamatva buddhi śūnyaiḥ  indriyaiḥ  api kevala śabdaḥ kāya ādibhiḥ  api pratyekam saṃbadhyate sarva vyāpāreṣu mamatā varjanāya yoginaḥ karmiṇaḥ karma kurvanti saṅgam tyaktvā phala viṣayam ātma śuddhaye sattva śuddhaya iti  arthaḥ tasmāt  tatra eva tava adhikāra iti kuru karma eva yasmāt ca yukta īśvarāya karmaṇi karomi na mama phalāya iti  evam samāhitaḥ san karma phalam tyaktvā parityajya śāntim mokṣa ākhyām āpnoti naiṣṭhikīm niṣṭhāyām bhavān sattva śuddhi jñāna prāpti sarva karma saṃnyāsa jñāna niṣṭhā krameṇa iti vākya śeṣaḥ yaḥ  tu punar  ayuktaḥ  asamāhitaḥ kāmakāreṇa karaṇam kāraḥ kāmasya kāraḥ kāmakāraḥ tena kāmakāreṇa kāma prerita tayā iti  arthaḥ mama phalāya idam karomi karma iti  evam phale saktaḥ  nibadhyate atas tvam yuktaḥ  bhava iti  arthaḥ yaḥ  tu parama artha darśī saḥ sarvāṇi karmāṇi sarva karmāṇi saṃnyasya parityajya nityam naimittikam kāmyam pratiṣiddham ca tāni sarvāṇi karmāṇi manasā viveka buddhyā karma ādau   akarma sandarśanena saṃtyajya iti  arthaḥ āste tiṣṭhati sukham tyakta vāc manaḥ kāya ceṣṭaḥ  nirāyāsaḥ prasanna citta ātmanaḥ  anyatra nivṛtta sarva bāhya prayojana iti sukham āste iti  ucyate vaśī jita indriya iti  arthaḥ kva katham āste iti  āha nava dvāre pure sapta śīrṣāṇyāni  ātmana upalabdhi dvārāṇi arvāk  dve mūtra purīṣa visarga arthe taiḥ  dvāraiḥ  nava dvāram puram ucyate śarīram puram iva puram ātmā eka svāmikam tad artha prayojana aiḥ  ca indriya manaḥ buddhi viṣayaiḥ  aneka phala vijñānasya utpādakaiḥ pauraiḥ  iva adhiṣṭhitam tasmin nava dvāre pure dehī sarvam karma saṃnyasya āste kim viśeṣaṇena sarvaḥ  hi dehī saṃnyāsy asaṃnyāsī vā dehe eva āste tatra anarthakam viśeṣaṇam iti ucyate yaḥ  tu  ajñaḥ dehī deha indriya saṃghāta mātra ātmadarśī sa sarvaḥ  api gehe bhūmau   āsane vā asa iti manyate na hi deha mātra ātma darśinaḥ geha iva dehe āsa iti pratyayaḥ saṃbhavati deha ādi saṃghāta vyatirikta ātma darśinaḥ  tu dehe āse iti pratyaya upapadyate para karmaṇām ca parasmin   ātmani  avidyayayā adhyāropitānām vidyayā viveka jñānena manasā saṃnyāsa upapadyate utpanna viveka jñānasya sarva karma saṃnyāsinaḥ  api geha iva deha eva nava dvāre pura āsanam prārabdha phala karma saṃskāra śeṣa anuvṛttyā deha eva viśeṣa vijñāna utpatteḥ dehe eva asta iti  asti  eva viśeṣaṇa phalam vidvada vidvat pratyaya bheda apekṣa tvāt yadi api kārya karaṇa karmāṇi  avidyayā ātmani  adhyāropitāni saṃnyasya āste iti  uktam tathā api ātma samavāyi tu kartṛ tvam kārayitṛ tvam ca syāt  iti  āśaṅkya āha na eva kurvan svayam na kārya karaṇāni kārayan kriyāsu pravartayan kim yad  tad  kartṛ tvam kārayitṛ tvam ca dehinaḥ sva ātma samavāyi sat  saṃnyāsān na saṃbhavati yathā gacchataḥ  gatiḥ  gamana vyāpāra parityāge na syāt  tadvat  kim vā svata eva ātmanaḥ  na asti iti atra ucyate na asti  ātmanaḥ svatas  kartṛ tvam kārayitṛ tvam ca uktam hi avikāryaḥ  ayam ucyate śarīra sthaḥ  api kaunteya na karoti na lipyate iti dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti ca śruteḥ kiṃca na kartṛ tvam svatas  kurv iti na api karmāṇi ratha ghaṭa prāsāda ādīn īpsitatamāni lokasya sṛjati  utpādayati prabhuḥ  ātmā na api ratha ādi kṛtavata s tad phalena saṃyogam na karma phala saṃyogam yadi kiṃcid  api svatas  na karoti na kārayati ca dehī kas tarhi kurvan kārayan ca pravartata iti ucyate svabhāvaḥ  tu svar  bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ  avidyā lakṣaṇā prakṛtiḥ  māyā pravartate daivī hi iti  ādinā vakṣyamāṇā paramārtha taḥ  tu na ādatte na ca gṛhṇāti bhaktasya api kasyacid  pāpam na ca eva ādatte sukṛtam bhaktaiḥ prayuktam vibhuḥ kimartham tarhi bhaktaiḥ pūjā ādi lakṣaṇam yāga dāna homa ādikam ca sukṛtam prayujyate iti  āha ajñānena āvṛtam jñānam viveka vijñānam tena muhyanti karomi kārayāmi bhokṣye bhojayāmi iti  evam moham gacchanti  avivekinaḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ  jantavaḥ jñānena tu yena ajñānena āvṛtāḥ muhyanti jantavaḥ  tad  ajñānam yeṣām jantūnām viveka jñānena ātma viṣayeṇa nāśitam ātmanaḥ  bhavati teṣām jantūnām ādityavat  yathā ādityaḥ samastam rūpa jātam avabhāsayati tadvat  jñānam jñeyam vastu sarvam prakāśayati tad  param parama artha tattvam yad  param jñānam prakāśitam tasmin brahmaṇi gatā buddhiḥ  yeṣām te tad buddhayaḥ tad ātmānaḥ  tad  eva param brahma ātmā yeṣām te tad ātmanāḥ tad niṣṭhāḥ niṣṭhā abhiniveśas tātparyam sarvāṇi karmāṇi saṃnyasya tasmin brahmaṇi  eva avasthānam yeṣām te tad niṣṭhāḥ tad parāyaṇā ca tad  eva param ayanam parā gatiḥ  yeṣām bhavati te tad parāyaṇāḥ kevala ātmarataya iti  arthaḥ yeṣām jñānena nāśitam ātmanaḥ  ajñānam te gacchanti evaṃvidyāḥ apunarāvṛttim apunar deha saṃbandham jñāna nirdhūta kalmaṣā yathā uktena jñānena nirdhūtaḥ  nāśitaḥ kalmaṣaḥ pāpa ādi saṃsāra kāraṇa doṣaḥ  yeṣām te jñāna nirdhūta kalmaṣā yatayaḥ iti  arthaḥ yeṣām jñānena nāśitam ātmanaḥ  ajñānam te paṇḍitāḥ katham tattvam payanti iti  ucyate vidyā vinaya saṃpanne vidyā ca vinayaḥ  ca vidyā vinayau vinaya upāmaḥ tābhyām vidyā vinayābhyām saṃpannaḥ  vidyā vinaya saṃpannaḥ  vidvān vinīta ś ca yaḥ  brāhmaṇas tasmin brāhmaṇe gavi hastini śuni ca eva śvapāke ca paṇḍitāḥ sama darśinaḥ vidyā vinaya saṃpanne uttama saṃskāravati brāhmaṇe sāttvike madhyamāyām ca rājasyām gavi saṃskāra hīnāyām atyantam eva kevala tāmase hasti ādau ca sattva ādi guṇaiḥ  tad jaiḥ  ca saṃskāraiḥ  tathā rājasaiḥ  tathā tāmasaiḥ  ca saṃskāraiḥ  atyantam eva aspṛṣṭām samam ekam avikriyam tad  brahma draṣṭum śīlam yeṣām te paṇḍitāḥ sama darśinaḥ nanu  abhojyāt na as te doṣavantaḥ samā samābhyām viṣama same pūjātaḥ iti smṛteḥ na te doṣavantaḥ katham iha eva jīvadbhiḥ eva taiḥ sama darśibhiḥ paṇḍitaiḥ  jitaḥ  vaīkṛtaḥ sargaḥ  janma yeṣām sāmye sarva bhūteṣu brahmaṇi sama bhāve sthitam ni calībhūtam manaḥ  antaḥkaraṇam nirdoṣam yadi api doṣavatsu vapākā ādiṣu mūḍhaiḥ  tad doṣaiḥ  doṣavat  iva vibhāvyate tathā api tad doṣaiḥ  aspṛṣṭām iti nirdoṣam doṣa varjitam hi yasmāt  na api sva guṇa bheda bhinnam nirguṇa tvāt  caitanyasya vakṣyati ca bhagavān icchā ādīnām kṣetra dharma tvam anādi tvāt nirguṇa tvāt iti ca na api  antyā viśeṣāḥ ātmanaḥ  bhedakāḥ santi pratiśarīram teṣām sattve pramāṇa anupapatteḥ atas  samam brahma ekam ca tasmāt  brahmaṇi eva te sthitāḥ tasmāt  na doṣa gandha mātram api tān spṛati deha ādi saṃghāta ātma darśana abhimāna abhāvāt teṣām deha ādi saṃghāta ātma darśana abhimānavat viṣayam tu tad  sūtram samā samābhyām viṣama same pūjātaḥ iti pūjā viṣaya tvena viśeṣaṇāt  dṛśyate hi brahma vid  ṣaḍāṅga vid  catur veda vid  iti pūjā dānādau guṇa viśeṣa saṃbandhaḥ kāraṇam brahma tu sarva guṇa doṣa saṃbandha varjitam iti atar brahmaṇi te sthitāḥ iti yuktam karma viṣayam ca sama asamābhyām iti  ādi idam tu sarva karma saṃnyāsa viṣayam prastutam sarva karmāṇi manasā iti ārabhya ādhyāya parisamāpteḥ yasmāt  nirdoṣam samam brahma ātmā tasmāt  na prahṛṣeyet  praharṣam na kuryāt  priyam iṣṭām prāpya labdhvā na udvijet  prāpya ca apriyam aniṣṭām labdhvā deha mātra ātma darśinām hi priya apriya prāptī harṣa viṣa ādau kurvāte na kevala ātma darśinaḥ tasya priya apriya prāpti asaṃbhavāt kim ca sarva bhūteṣu  ekaḥ samaḥ  nirdoṣa ātmā iti sthirā nirvicikitsā buddhiḥ  yasya sa sthira buddhiḥ  asaṃmūḍhaḥ saṃmoha varjitaś ca syāt  yathā ukta brahma vid brahmaṇi sthitaḥ  akarma kṛt  sarva karma saṃnyāsi iti  arthaḥ kim ca brahmaṇi sthitaḥ bāhya sparśeṣu bāhyā ca te sparśāḥ  ca bāhya sparśāḥ spṛśyante iti sparśāḥ śabda ādayaḥ  viṣayāḥ  teṣu bāhya sparśeṣu asakta ātmā antaḥkaraṇam yasya saḥ  ayam asakta ātmā viṣayeṣu prīti varjitaḥ san vindati labhate ātmani yad  sukham tad  vindati iti  etad  sa brahma yoga yukta ātmā brahmaṇi yogaḥ samādhiḥ  brahma yoga s tena brahma yogena yuktaḥ samāhita s tasmin vyāpṛta ātmā antaḥkaraṇam yasya sa brahma yoga yukta ātmā sukham akṣayam aśnute vyāpnoti tasmāt  bāhya viṣaya prīteḥ kṣaṇikāyāḥ  indriyāṇi nivartayet  ātmani  akṣaya sukha arthī iti  arthaḥ itas  ca nivartayet  ye hi yasmāt  saṃssparśa jā viṣaya indriya saṃsparśebhyaḥ  jātā bhogā bhuktayaḥ  duḥkha yonaya eva te avidyā kṛta tvāt  dṛśyante hi  ādhyātmika ādīni duḥkhāni tad nimittāni  eva yathā ihaloke tathā para loke api iti gamyate eva śabdāt  na saṃsāre sukhasya gandha mātram api  asti iti buddhvā viṣaya mṛgatṛṣṇikāyāḥ  indriyāṇi nivartayet  na kevalam duḥkha yonaya eva ādi antavanta ś ca ādiḥ  viṣaya indriya saṃyogaḥ  bhogānām antar  ca tad viyoga eva atas  ādi antavantaḥ  anityāḥ madhya kṣaṇa bhāvi tvāt  iti  arthaḥ kaunteya na teṣu bhogeṣu ramate budhaḥ viveki  avagata parama artha tattvaḥ atyanta mūḍhānām eva hi viṣayeṣu ratiḥ  dṛśyate yathā paśu prabhṛtīnām ayam ca śreyaḥ mārga pratipakṣī kaṣṭatamaḥ  doṣaḥ sarva anartha prāpti hetuḥ  durnivāraḥ  ca iti tad parihāre yatna ādhikyam kartavyam iti  āha bhagavān śaknoti  utsahata iha eva jīvan   eva yaḥ soḍhum prasahitum prāk  pūrvam śarīravimokṣaṇāt  ā maraṇāt  iti  arthaḥ maraṇa sīmākaraṇam jīvataḥ  avayaṃbhāvi hi kāma krodha udbhavaḥ  vegaḥ ananta nimittavān hi saḥ iti yāvat  maraṇam tāvat  na visrāmbhaṇīya iti  arthaḥ kāmaḥ indriya gocara prāpte iṣṭaḥ  viṣaye śrūyamāṇe smaryamāṇe vā anubhūte sukha hetau yā gaṄdha s tṛṣṇā sa kāmaḥ krodhaḥ  ca ātmanaḥ pratikūleṣu duḥkha hetuṣu dṛyamāneṣu śrūyamāṇeṣu smaryamāṇeṣu vā yaḥ  dveṣaḥ sa krodhaḥ tau kāma krodhau   udbhavaḥ  yasya vegasya sa kāma krodha udbhavaḥ  vegaḥ romāñcana prahṛṣṭa netra vadana ādi liṅgaḥ  antaḥkaraṇa prakṣobha rūpaḥ kāma udbhavaḥ  vegaḥ gātra prakampa prasveda saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭha puṭa rakta netra ādi liṅgaḥ krodha udbhavaḥ  vegaḥ tam kāma krodha udbhavam vegam ya utsahate prasahate soḍhum prasahitum saḥ  yuktaḥ  yogī sukhī ca iha loke naraḥ kathaṃbhūta ś ca brahmaṇi sthitaḥ  brahma prāpnoti iti  āha bhagavān yaḥ  antar sukhaḥ  antar ātmani sukham yasya saḥ  antar sukhaḥ tathā antar eva ātmani  ārāma āramaṇam ākrīḍā yasya saḥ  antara ārāmaḥ tathā eva antar eva ātmani  eva jyotiḥ prakāśaḥ  yasya saḥ  antar jyotiḥ  eva ya īdṛśaḥ saḥ  yogī brahma nirvāṇam brahmaṇi nirvṛtim mokṣam iha jīvan   eva brahma bhūtaḥ san   adhigacchati prāpnoti kiṃca labhante brahma nirvāṇam mokṣam ṛṣayaḥ samyak darśinaḥ saṃnyāsinaḥ kṣīṇa kalmaṣāḥ kṣīṇa pāpā nirdoṣa āḥ  chinna dvaidhāḥ chinna saṃśayā yata ātmānaḥ saṃyata indriyāḥ sarva bhūta hite ratāḥ sarveṣām bhūtānām hite ānukūlye ratā ahiṃsakā iti  arthaḥ kiṃca kāma krodha viyuktānām kāmaḥ  ca krodhaḥ  ca kāma krodhau tābhyām viyuktānām yatīnām saṃnyāsinām yata cetasām saṃyata antaḥkaraṇānām abhita ubhayatas  jīvatām mṛtānām ca brahma nirvāṇam mokṣaḥ  vartate vidita ātmanām viditaḥ  jñāta ātmā yeṣām te vidita ātmanām teṣām vidita ātmanām samyak darśinām iti  arthaḥ samyak  darśana niṣṭhānām saṃnyāsinām sadyas muktiḥ  uktā karma yogaḥ  ca īśvara arpita sarva bhāvena īśvare brahmaṇi  ādhāya kriyamāṇaḥ sattva śuddhi jñāna prāpti sarva karma saṃnyāsa krameṇa mokṣāya iti bhagavān pade pade abravīt  vakṣyati ca atha idānīm dhyāna yogam samyak darśanasya antaraṅgam vistareṇa vakṣyāmi iti tasya sūtra sthānīyān ślokān upadiśati sma sparśān śabda ādīn kṛtvā bahis  bāhyān śrotra ādi dvāreṇa antar buddhau praveśitāḥ śabda ādayaḥ  viṣayāḥ  tān acintayataḥ  śabda ādayaḥ  bāhyā bahis  eva kṛtā bhavanti tān evam bahis  kṛtvā cakṣuḥ  ca eva antare bhruvoḥ kṛtvā iti  anuṣajyate tathā prāṇa apānau nāsā abhyantara cāriṇau samau kṛtvā yata indriya manaḥ buddhiḥ  yatāni saṃyatāni indriyāṇi manaḥ  buddhiḥ  ca yasya sa yata indriya manaḥ buddhiḥ mananāt  muniḥ saṃnyāsī mokṣa parāyaṇa evam deha saṃsthānān mokṣa parāyaṇaḥ  mokṣa eva param ayanam parā gatiḥ  yasya saḥ  ayam mokṣa parāyaṇaḥ  muniḥ  bhavet  vigata icchā bhaya krodha icchā ca bhayam ca krodhaḥ  ca icchā bhaya krodhāḥ  te vigatāḥ yasmāt  sa vigata icchā bhaya krodhaḥ ya evam vartate sadā saṃnyāsī mukta eva saḥ na tasya mokṣaḥ  anyaḥ kartavyaḥ  asti evam samāhita cittena kim vijñeyam iti  ucyate bhoktāram yajña tapasām yajñānām tapasām ca kartṛ rūpeṇa devatā rūpeṇa ca sarva loka maheśvaram sarveṣām lokānām mahāntam īśvaram suhṛdam sarva bhūtānām sarva prāṇinām pratyupakāra nirapekṣa tayā upakāriṇam sarva bhūtānām hṛdayeśayam sarva karma phala adhyakṣam sarva pratyaya sākṣiṇam mām nārāyaṇam jñātvā śāntim sarva saṃsāra uparatim ṛcchati prāpnoti atīta anantara adhyāya ante dhyāna yogasya samyak  darśanam praty antaraṅgasya sūtra bhūtāḥ ślokāḥ sparśān kṛtvā bahis  iti  ādaya upadiṣṭaḥ teṣām vṛtti sthānīyaḥ  ayam ṣaṣṭhaḥ  adhyāya ārabhyate tatra dhyāna yogasya bahis aṅgam karma iti yāvat  dhyāna yoga ārohaṇa samartha s tāvat  gṛhasthena adhikṛtena kartavyam karma iti  atas tad  stauti nanu kimartham dhyāna yoga ārohaṇa sīmākaraṇam yāvatā anuṣṭheyam eva vihitam karma yāvajjīvam na ārurukṣoḥ  muneḥ  yogam karma kāraṇam ucyate iti viśeṣaṇāt  ārūḍhasya ca śamena eva saṃbandha karaṇāt  ārurukṣoḥ  ārūḍhasya ca śamaḥ karmaḥ  ca ubhayam kartavya tvena abhipretam ced  syāt  tadārurukṣoḥ  ārūḍhasya ca iti śama karma viṣaya bhedena viśeṣaṇam vibhāga karaṇam ca anarthakam syāt  tatra āśramiṇām kaścid  yogam ārurukṣuḥ  bhavati ārūḍhaḥ  ca kaścid  anye nārurukṣavaḥ na ca ārūḍhāḥ tān apekṣya ārurukṣoḥ  ārūḍhasya ca iti viśeṣaṇam vibhāga karaṇam ca upapadyata eva iti ced  na tasya eva iti vacanāt  punar  yoga grahaṇāt  ca yoga ārūḍhasya iti ya āsīt  pūrvam yogam ārurukṣuḥ  tasya eva ārūḍhasya śama eva kartavyaḥ kāraṇam yoga phalam pratyucyata iti atas  na yāvat jīvam kartavyatva prāptiḥ kasyacid  api karmaṇaḥ yoga vibhraṣṭa vacanāt  ca gṛhasthasya ced  karmiṇaḥ  yogaḥ  vihitaḥ ṣaṣṭhe adhyāye sa yoga vibhraṣṭaḥ  api karma gatim karma phalam prāpnoti iti tasya na āśa āśaṅkā anupapannā syāt  avaśyam hi kṛtam karma kāmyam nityam vā mokṣasya nitya tvāt  anārabhya tve svam phalam ārabhata eva nityasya ca karmaṇaḥ  veda pramāṇau  abuddha tvāt phalena bhavitavyam iti  avocāma anyathā vedasya anartha arthatva prasaṅgāt  iti na ca karmaṇi sati  ubhaya vibhraṣṭa vacanam arthavat  karmaṇaḥ  vibhraṃśa kāraṇa anupapatteḥ karma kṛtam īśvare saṃnyasya iti  atas  kartari karma phalam na ārabhata iti ced  na īśvare saṃnyāsasya adhikatara phala hetutva upapatteḥ mokṣāya eva iti ced  sva karmaṇām kṛtānām īśvare nyāsaḥ  mokṣāya eva na phala antarāya yoga sahitaḥ yogāt  ca vibhraṣṭa iti  atas tam prati nāśa śaṅkā yuktā eva iti ced  na ekākī yata citta ātmā nirāśīḥ  aparigrahaḥ brahmacāri vrate sthitaḥ iti karma saṃnyāsa vidhānāt na ca atra gṛhasthasya nirāśīḥ  aparigrahaḥ iti  ādi vacanam anukūlam ubhaya vibhraṣṭa praśna anupapatteḥ  ca anāśrita iti  anena karmiṇa eva saṃnyāsi tvam yogi tvam ca uktam pratiṣiddham ca niragneḥ akriyasya ca saṃnyāsi tvam yogi tvam ca iti ced  na dhyāna yogam prati bahis aṅgasya sataḥ karmaṇaḥ phala ākāṅkṣā saṃnyāsa stuti paratvāt na kevalam niragniḥ  akriya eva saṃnyāsī yogī ca kim tarhi karmi  api karma phala āsaṅgam saṃnyasya karma yogam anutiṣṭhan sattva śuddhi artham sa saṃnyāsī ca yogī ca bhavati iti stūyate na ca ekena vākyena karma phala āsaṅga saṃnyāsa stutiḥ  caturtha āśrama pratiṣedhaḥ  ca upapadyate na ca prasiddham niragneḥ  akriyasya parama artha saṃnyāsinaḥ śruti smṛti purāṇa itihāsa yoga śāstreṣu vihitam saṃnyāsi tvam yogi tvam ca pratiṣedhati bhagavān sva vacana virodha āt  ca sarva karmāṇi manasā saṃnyasya na eva kurvan na kārayan āste maunī saṃtuṣṭaḥ  yena kenacid  aniketaḥ sthira matiḥ vihāya kāmān yaḥ sarvān pumānś carati niḥspṛhaḥ sarva ārambha parityāgī iti ca tatra tatra bhagavatā sva vacanāni darśitāni taiḥ  virudhyetas  caturtha āśrama pratiṣedhaḥ tasmāt  muneḥ  yogam ārurukṣoḥ pratipanna ga arhasthyasya agnihotra ādi karma phala nirapekṣam anuṣṭhīyamānam dhyāna yoga ārohaṇa sādhana tvam sattva śuddhi dvāreṇa pratipadyata iti sa saṃnyāsī ca yogī ca iti stūyate anāśritaḥ  na āśritaḥ  anāśritaḥ kim karma phalam karmaṇām phalam karma phalam yad  tad anāśritaḥ karma phala tṛṣṇā rahita iti  arthaḥ yaḥ  hi karma phale tṛṣṇāvān sa karma phalam āśritaḥ  bhavati ayam tu tad viparītaḥ atas  anāśritaḥ karma phalam evaṃbhūtaḥ san kāryam kartavyam nityam kāmya viparītam agnihotra ādikam karma karoti nirvartayati yaḥ kaścid  īdṛśaḥ karmī sa karmi  antarebhyaḥ  viśiṣyate iti  evam artham āha sa saṃnyāsī ca yogī ca iti saṃnyāsaḥ parityāgaḥ sa yasya asti sa saṃnyāsī ca yogī ca yogaḥ  citta samādhānam sa yasya asti sa yogī ca iti evaṃguṇa saṃpannaḥ  ayam mantavyaḥ na kevalam niragniḥ  akriya eva saṃnyāsī yogī ca iti mantavyaḥ nirgatāḥ agnayaḥ karma aṅga bhūtā yasmāt  sa niragniḥ akriyaḥ  ca anagni sādhana api  avidyamānāḥ kriyās tapaḥ dāna ādikā yasya asau   akriyaḥ nanu ca niragneḥ akriyasya eva śruti smṛti yoga śāstreṣu saṃnyāsi tvam yogi tvam ca prasiddham katham iha sa agneḥ sa kriyasya ca saṃnyāsi tvam yogi tvam ca aprasiddham ucyata iti na eṣa doṣaḥ kayācid  guṇa vṛttyā ubhayasya saṃpipādayiṣita tvāt  tad  katham karma phala saṃkalpa saṃnyāsāt  saṃnyāsi tvam yoga aṅga tvena ca karma anuṣṭhānāt karma phala saṃkalpasya ca citta vikṣepa hetoḥ parityāgāt  yogi tvam ca iti gauṇam ubhayam na punar  mukhyam saṃnyāsi tvam yogi tvam ca abhipretam iti  etam artham darśayitum āha yam sarva karma tad phala parityāga lakṣaṇam parama artha saṃnyāsam saṃnyāsam iti prāhuḥ śruti smṛti vidaḥ yogam karma anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇam tam parama artha saṃnyāsam viddhi jānīhi he pāṇḍāva karma yogasya pravṛtti lakṣaṇasya tad viparītena nivṛtti lakṣaṇena parama artha saṃnyāsena kīdṛśam sāmānyam aṅgīkṛtya tad bhāva ucyate iti  apekṣāyām idam ucyate asti hi parama artha saṃnyāsena sādṛśyam kartṛ dvārakam karma yogasya yaḥ  hi parama artha saṃnyāsī sa tyakta sarva karma sādhana tayā sarva karma tad phala viṣayam saṃkalpam pravṛtti hetu kāma kāraṇam saṃnyasyati ayam api karma yogī karma kurvāṇa eva phala viṣayam saṃkalpam saṃnyasyati iti etam artham darśayiṣyan   āha na hi yasmāt  asaṃnyasta saṃkalpaḥ  asaṃnyastaḥ  aparityaktaḥ saṅkalpaḥ  abhisandhiḥ  yena saḥ  asaṃnyasta saṅkalpaḥ kaścana kaścid  api karmī yogī samādhānavān bhavati na saṃbhavati iti  arthaḥ phala saṃkalpasya citta vikṣepa hetu tvāt tasmāt  yaḥ kaścana karmī saṃnyasta phala saṃkalpaḥ  bhavet  sa yogī samādhānavān avikṣipta cittaḥ  bhavet  citta vikṣepa hetoḥ phala saṃkalpasya saṃnyasta tvāt  iti  abhiprāyaḥ yoga aṅga tvena karma anuṣṭhānāt karma phala saṅkalpasya vā citta vikṣepa hetoḥ parityāgāt  yogi tvam ca iti saṃnyāsi tvam ca iti  abhipretam ucyate evam parama artha saṃnyāsa karma yogayoḥ kartṛ dvārakam saṃnyāsa sāmānyam apekṣya yam saṃnyāsam iti prāhuḥ  yogam tam viddhi pāṇḍāva iti karma yogasya stuti artham saṃnyāsa tvam uktam dhyāna yogasya phala nirapekṣaḥ karma yogaḥ  bahis aṅgam sādhanam iti tam saṃnyāsa tvena stutvā adhunā karma yogasya dhyāna yoga sādhana tvam darśayati ārurukṣoḥ  āroḍhum icchataḥ anārūḍhasya dhyāna yoge avasthātum aśaktasya eva iti  arthaḥ kasya tasya ārurukṣoḥ muneḥ karma phala saṃnyāsina iti  arthaḥ kim ārurukṣoḥ yogam karma kāraṇam sādhanam ucyate yoga ārūḍhasya punar  tasya eva śamar upaśamaḥ sarva karmabhyaḥ  nivṛttiḥ kāraṇam yoga ārūḍhasya sādhanam ucyate iti  arthaḥ yāvat  yāvat  karmabhya uparamate tāvat  tāvat  nirāyāsasya jita indriyasya cittam samādhīyate tathā sati sa jhaṭiti yoga ārūḍhaḥ  bhavati tathā ca uktam vyāsena na etādṛśam brāhmaṇasya asti vittam yathā ekatā sama tā satyatā ca śīlam sthitiḥ  daṇḍa nidhānam ārjavam tatas  tatas  ca uparamaḥ kriyābhyaḥ iti atha idānīm kadā yoga ārūḍhaḥ  bhavati iti  ucyate yadā samādhīyamāna cittaḥ  yogī hi indriyārtheṣu  indriyāṇām arthāḥ śabda ādayaḥ  teṣu  indriya artheṣu karmasu ca nitya naimittika kāmya pratiṣiddheṣu prayojana abhāva buddhyā na anuṣajjate anuṣaṅgam kartavyatā buddhim na karoti iti  arthaḥ sarva saṃkalpa saṃnyāsī sarvān saṃkalpān iha amutra artha kāma hetūna saṃnyasitum śīlam asya iti sarva saṃkalpa saṃnyāsī yoga ārūḍhaḥ prāpta yoga iti  etad  tadā tasmin kāla ucyate sarva saṃkalpa saṃnyāsi iti vacanāt  sarvān   ca kāmān sarvāṇi ca karmāṇi saṃnyasya īt  iti  arthaḥ saṃkalpamūlā hi sarve kāmāḥ saṃkalpamūlaḥ kāmaḥ  vai yajñāḥ saṃkalpa saṃbhavāḥ kāma jānāmi te mūlam saṃkalpāt  tvam hi jāyase na tvām saṃkalpayiṣyāmi tena me na bhaviṣyasi iti  ādi smṛteḥ sarva kāma parityāge ca sarva karma saṃnyāsaḥ siddhaḥ  bhavati sa yathākāmaḥ  bhavati tad kratuḥ  bhavati yad  kratuḥ  bhavati tad  karma kurute iti  ādi śrutibhyaḥ yad  yad  dhi kurute jantuḥ  tad  tad  kāmasya ceṣṭitam iti  ādi smṛtibhyaḥ  ca nyāyāt  ca na hi sarva saṃkalpa saṃnyāse kaścid  spanditum api śaktaḥ tasmāt  sarva saṃkalpa saṃnyāsi iti vacanāt  sarvān kāmān sarvāṇi karmāṇi ca tyājayati bhagavān yadā evam yoga ārūḍhaḥ tadā tena ātmā udbhṛtaḥ  bhavati saṃsārāt  anartha jātāt  atas  uddharet  saṃsāra sāgare nimagnam ātmanā ātmānam tatas  ut ūrdhvam haret  uddharet  yoga ārūḍha tām āpādayet  iti  arthaḥ na ātmānam avasādayet  na adhas  nayeta na adhas  gamayet  ātmā eva hi yasmāt  ātmanaḥ  bandhuḥ na hi  anyaḥ kaścid  bandhuḥ yaḥ saṃsāra muktaye bhavati bandhuḥ  api tāvat  mokṣam prati pratikūla eva sneha ādi bandhana āyatana tvāt  tasmāt  yuktam avadhāraṇam ātmā eva hi  ātmanaḥ  bandhuḥ  iti ātmā eva ripuḥ śatruḥ yaḥ  anyaḥ  apakārī bāhyaḥ śatruḥ saḥ  api ātma prayukta eva iti yuktam eva avadhāraṇam ātmā eva ripuḥ  ātmana iti ātmā eva bandhuḥ  ātmā eva ripuḥ  ātmana iti  uktam tatra kiṃlakṣaṇa ātmā ātmanaḥ  bandhuḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ  vā ātma ātmanaḥ  ripuḥ  iti  ucyate bandhuḥ  ātma ātmanaḥ  tasya tasya ātmanaḥ sa ātmā bandhuḥ  yena ātmanā ātmā eva jitaḥ ātmā kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ  yena vaśīkṛtaḥ jita indriya iti  arthaḥ anātmanas tu  ajita ātmanas tu śatru tve śatru bhāve varteta ātmā eva śatruvat  yathā anātmā śatruḥ  ātmanaḥ  apakārī tathā ātmā ātmanaḥ  apakāre varteta iti  arthaḥ jita ātmanaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta ātmā jitaḥ  yena sa jita ātmā tasya jita ātmanaḥ praśāntasya prasanna antaḥkaraṇasya sataḥ saṃnyāsinaḥ paramātmā samāhitaḥ sākṣāt ātma bhāvena vartate iti  arthaḥ kim ca śīta uṣṇa sukha duḥkheṣu tathā māne apamāne ca māna apamānayoḥ pūjā paribhavayoḥ samaḥ syāt  jñāna vijñāna tṛpta ātmā jñānam śāstra ukta padārthānām parijñānam vijñānam tu śāstrataḥ  jñātānām tathā eva sva anubhava karaṇam tābhyām jñāna vijñānābhyām tṛptaḥ saṃjāta alaṃpratyayaḥ ātma antaḥkaraṇam yasya sa jñāna vijñāna tṛpta ātmā kūṭāsthaḥ  aprakampyaḥ bhavati iti  arthaḥ vijita indriyaḥ  ca ya īdṛśaḥ yuktaḥ samāhita iti sa ucyate kathyate sa yogī sama loṣṭa aśma kāñcanaḥ loṣṭa aśma kāñcanāni samāni yasya saḥ sama loṣṭa aśma kāñcanaḥ kiṃca suhṛd iti  ādi loka ardham ekam padam suhṛd  iti pratyupakāram anapekṣya upakartā mitram snehavān ariḥ śatruḥ udāsīnaḥ  na kasyacid  pakṣam bhajate madhyasthaḥ  yaḥ  viruddhayoḥ  ubhayoḥ hita eṣī dveṣya ātmanaḥ  apriyaḥ bandhuḥ saṃbandhī iti  eteṣu sādhuṣu śāstra anuvartiṣu api ca pāpeṣu pratiṣiddha kāriṣu sarveṣu  eteṣu sama buddhiḥ kaḥ kiṃkarmā iti  avyāpṛta buddhiḥ  iti  arthaḥ viśiṣyate vimucyate iti vā pāṭha antaram yoga ārūḍhānām sarveṣām ayam uttama iti  arthaḥ ata evam uttama phala prāptaye yogī dhyāyī yuñjīta samādadhyāt  satatam sarvadā ātmānam antaḥkaraṇam rahasi ekānte giri guhā ādau sthitaḥ san ekākī asahāyaḥ rahasi sthitaḥ ekākī ca iti viśeṣaṇāt  saṃnyāsam kṛtvā iti  arthaḥ yata citta ātmā cittam antaḥkaraṇam ātmā dehaḥ  ca saṃyatau yasya sa yata citta ātmā nirāśīḥ  vīta tṛṣṇaḥ  aparigrahaḥ parigraha rahita ś ca iti  arthaḥ saṃnyāsi tve api tyakta sarva parigrahaḥ san yuñjīta iti  arthaḥ atha idānīm yogam yuñjataḥ āsana āhāra vihāra ādīnām yoga sādhana tvena niyamaḥ  vaktavyaḥ prāpta yogasya lakṣaṇam tad phala ādi ca iti  ata ārabhyate tatra āsanam eva tāvat  prathamam ucyate śucau śuddhe vivikte svabhāvataḥ saṃskārataḥ  vā deśe sthāne pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram acalam ātmana āsanam na ati ucchritam na atīva ucchritam na api  ati nīcam tad  ca caila ajina kuśa uttaram cailam ajinam kuśāś ca uttare yasmin   āsane tad  āsanam caila ajina kuśa uttaram pāṭha kramāt  viparītaḥ  atra kramaś caila ādīnām pratiṣṭhāpya kim tatra tasmin   āsana upaviśya yogam yuñjyāt  katham sarva viṣayebhyaḥ  upasaṃhṛtya ekāgram manaḥ kṛtvā yata citta indriya kriyaḥ  cittam ca indriyāṇi ca citta indriyāṇi teṣām kriyāḥ saṃyatā yasya sa yata citta indriya kriyaḥ sa kimartham yogam yuñjyāt  iti  āha ātma viśuddhaye antaḥkaraṇasya viśuddhi artham iti  etad  bāhyam āsanam uktam adhunā śarīra dhāraṇam katham iti  ucyate samam kāya śiraḥ grīvam kāyaś ca śiraś ca grīvā ca kāya śiraḥ grīvam tad  samam dhārayan acalam ca samam dhārayataś calanam saṃbhavati atas  viśinaṣṭi acalam iti sthiraḥ sthiraḥ  bhūtvā iti  arthaḥ svam nāsikā agram saṃprekṣya samyak  prekṣaṇam darśanam kṛtvā eva iti iva śabdaḥ  luptaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ na hi sva nāsikā agra saṃprekṣaṇam iha vidhitsitam kim tarhi cakṣuṣaḥ  dṛṣṭi saṃnipātaḥ sa ca antaḥkaraṇa samādhāna apekṣaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ sva nāsikā agra saṃprekṣaṇam eva ced  vivakṣitam manas tatra eva samādhīyeta na ātmani ātmani hi manasaḥ samādhānam vakṣyati ātma saṃstham manaḥ kṛtvā iti tasmāt  iva śabda lopena akṣṇoḥ  dṛṣṭi saṃnipāta eva saṃprekṣya iti  ucyate diśaḥ  ca anavalokayan diśām ca avalokanam antarā kurvan iti  etad  kiṃca praśānta ātmā prakarṣeṇa śāntaḥ ātma antaḥkaraṇam yasya saḥ  ayam praśānta ātmā vigata bhīḥ vigata bhayaḥ brahmacāri vrate sthitaḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ  vratam brahmacaryam guru śuśrūṣā bhikṣā anna bhukti ādi tasmin sthitaḥ tad anuṣṭhātā bhavet  iti  arthaḥ kim ca manaḥ saṃyamya manasaḥ  vṛttīḥ  upasaṃhṛtya iti  etad  mad cittaḥ  mayi parameśvare cittam yasya saḥ  ayam mad cittaḥ yuktaḥ samāhitaḥ san   āsīta upaviśet  mad paraḥ  aham paraḥ  yasya saḥ  ayam mad paraḥ  bhavati kaścid  rāgī strī cittaḥ na tu striyam eva paratvena gṛhṇāti kim tarhi rājānam mahādevam vā ayam tu mad cittaḥ  mad paraś ca atha idānīm yoga phalam ucyate yujan samādhānām kurvan   evam yathā uktena vidhānena sadā ātmanām sarvadā yogī niyata mānasaḥ  niyatam saṃyatam mānasam manaḥ  yasya saḥ  ayam niyata mānasaḥ śāntim uparatim nirvāṇa paramām nirvāṇam mokṣas tad  paramā niṣṭhā yasyāḥ śānteḥ sā nirvāṇa paramā tām nirvāṇa paramām mad saṃsthām mad adhīnām adhigacchati prāpnoti idānīm yoginaḥ āhāra ādi niyama ucyate na atyaśnata ātma saṃmitam anna parimāṇam atītya aśnataḥ  atyaśnataḥ na yogaḥ  asti na ca ekāntam anaśnataḥ  yogaḥ  asti yad  u ha vā ātma saṃmitam annam tad  avati tad  na hinasti yad  bhūyaḥ hinasti tad  yad  kanīyaḥ  annam na tad  avati iti śruteḥ tasmāt  yogī na ātma saṃmitāt  anna ād adhikam nyūnam vā aśnīyāt  athavā yoginaḥ  yoga śāstre paripaṭhitāt  anna parimāṇāt  atimātram aśnataḥ yogaḥ  na asti uktam hi ardham sa vyañjana annasya tṛtīyam udakasya ca vāyoḥ saṃcaraṇa artham tu caturtham avaśeṣayet  iti  ādi parimāṇam tathā na ca ati svapna śīlasya yogaḥ  bhavati na eva ca atimātram jāgrataḥ  bhavati ca arjuna katham punar  yogaḥ  bhavati iti  ucyate yukta āhāra vihārasya āhriyata iti  āhāraḥ  annam viharaṇam vihāraḥ pāda kramaḥ tau yuktau niyata parimāṇau yasya sa yukta āhāra vihāra s tasya tathā yukta ceṣṭasya yuktā niyatā ceṣṭā yasya karmasu tasya tathā yukta svapna avabodhasya yuktau svapnaḥ  ca avabodhaḥ  ca tau niyata kālau yasya tasya yukta āhāra vihārasya yukta ceṣṭasya karmasu yukta svapna avabodhasya yoginaḥ  yogaḥ  bhavati duḥkha hā duḥkhāni sarvāṇi hanti iti duḥkha hā sarva saṃsāra duḥkha kṣaya kṛt  yogaḥ  bhavati iti  arthaḥ atha adhunā kadā yuktaḥ  bhavati iti  ucyate yadā viniyatam viśeṣeṇa niyatam saṃyatam ekāgra tām āpannam cittam hitvā bāhya artha cintām ātmani  eva kevale avatiṣṭhate sva ātmani sthitim labhate iti  arthaḥ niḥspṛhaḥ sarva kāmebhyaḥ  nirgatā dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa viṣayebhyaḥ spṛhā tṛṣṇā yasya yoginaḥ sa yuktaḥ samāhita iti  ucyate tadā tasmin kāle tasya yoginaḥ samāhitam yad  cittam tasya upamā ucyate yathā dīpaḥ pradīpaḥ  nivāta sthaḥ  nivāte vāta varjite deśe sthitaḥ  na iṅgate na calati sopamā upamīyate anayā iti  upamā yoga jñaiḥ  citta pracāra darśibhiḥ smṛtā cintitā yoginaḥ  yata cittasya saṃyata antaḥkaraṇasya yuñjataḥ  yogam anutiṣṭhata ātmanaḥ samādhim anutiṣṭhata iti  arthaḥ evam yoga abhyāsa balāt  ekāgrībhūtam nivāta pradīpa kalpam sat  yatra yasmin kāle uparamate cittam uparatim gacchati niruddham sarvatas  nivārita pracāram yoga sevayā yoga anuṣṭhānena yatra ca eva yasmin   ca kāla ātmanā samādhi pariśuddhena antaḥkaraṇena ātmānam param caitanyam jyotiḥ svarūpam paśyan   upalabhamānaḥ sva  eva ātmani tuṣyati tuṣṭim bhajate kiṃca sukham ātyantikam atyantam eva bhavati iti  ātyantikam anantam iti  arthaḥ yad  tad  buddhi grāhyam buddhyā eva indriya nirapekṣayā gṛhyate iti buddhi grāhyam atīndriyam indriya gocara atītam aviṣaya janitam iti  arthaḥ vetti tad  īdṛśam sukham anubhavati yatra yasmin kāle na ca eva ayam vidvān ātma svarūpe sthitas tasmāt  na eva calati tattvatas tattva svarūpān na pracyavata iti  arthaḥ kiṃca yam labdhvā yam ātma lābham labdhvā prāpyaś ca aparam anyal lābham lābha antaram tatas  adhikam asti iti na manyate na cintayati kim ca yasmin ātma tattve sthitaḥ  duḥkhena śastra nipāta ādi lakṣaṇena guruṇā mahatā api na vicālyate yatra uparamate iti  ādya ārabhya yāvadbhiḥ  viśeṣaṇaiḥ  viśiṣṭa ātma avasthā viśeṣaḥ  yoga uktaḥ tam vidyāt  vijānīyāt  duḥkha saṃyoga viyogam duḥkhaiḥ saṃyogaḥ  duḥkha saṃyogaḥ tena viyogaḥ  duḥkha saṃyoga viyogaḥ tam duḥkha saṃyoga viyogam yoga iti  eva saṃjñitam viparīta lakṣaṇena vidyāt  vijānīyāt  iti  arthaḥ yoga phalam upasaṃhṛtya punar  anvārambheṇa yogasya kartavyatā ucyate niścaya anirvedayoḥ  yoga sādhanatva vidhāna artham sa yathā ukta phalaḥ  yogaḥ  niścayena adhyavasāyena yoktavyaḥ  anirviṇṇa cetasā na nirviṇṇam anirviṇṇam kim tad  cetas tena nirveda rahitena cetasā cittena iti  arthaḥ kiṃca saṃkalpa prabhavān saṃkalpaḥ prabhavaḥ  yeṣām kāmānām te saṃkalpa prabhavāḥ kāmāḥ  tān tyaktvā parityajya sarvān aśeṣatas  nirlepena kim ca manasā eva viveka yuktena indriya grāmam indriya samudāyam viniyamya niyamanam kṛtvā samantatas samantāt  śanais  śanais  na sahasā uparamet  uparatim kuryāt  kayā buddhyā kiṃviśiṣṭayā dhṛti gṛhītayā dhṛtyā dhairyeṇa gṛhītayā dhṛti gṛhītayā dhairyeṇa yuktayā iti  arthaḥ ātma saṃstham ātmani saṃsthitam ātmā eva sarvam na tatas  anyat  kiṃcid  asti iti  evam ātma saṃstham manaḥ kṛtvā na kiṃcid  api cintayet  eṣa yogasya paramaḥ  vidhiḥ tatra evam ātma saṃstham manaḥ kartum pravṛttaḥ  yogī yatas  yatas  yasmāt  yasmān nimittāt  śabda ādeḥ  niścarati nirgacchati svabhāva doṣān manaḥ  cañcalam atyartham calam ata eva asthiram tatas  tatas  tasmāt  tasmāt  śabda ādeḥ  nimittān niyamya tad tad nimittam yāthātmya nirūpaṇena śabda ādeḥ nimittān niyamya tad tannam ittam yāthātmya nirūpaṇena ābhāsīkṛtya vairāgya bhāvanayā ca etad  mana ātmani  eva vaśam nayet  ātma vaśya tām āpādayet  evam yoga abhyāsa balāt yogina ātmani  eva praśāmyati manaḥ praśānta manasam prakarṣeṇa śāntam manaḥ  yasya saḥ praśānta manās tam praśānta manasam hi enam yoginam sukham uttamam nitiśayam upaiti upagacchati śānta rajasam prakṣīṇa moha ādi kleśa rajasam iti  arthaḥ brahma bhūtam jīvanmuktam brahmā eva sarvam iti  evam niścayavantam brahma bhūtam akalmaṣam dharma adharma ādi varjitam yuñjan   evam yathā uktena krameṇa yogī yoga antarāya varjitaḥ sadā sarvadā ātmānam vigata kalmaṣaḥ  vigata pāpaḥ sukhena anāyāsena brahma saṃsparśam brahmaṇā pareṇa saṃsparśaḥ  yasya tad  brahma saṃsparrśam sukham atyantam antam atītya vartata iti  atyantam utkṛṣṭam niratiśayam aśnute vyāpnoti idānīm yogasya yad  phalam brahma ekatva darśanam sarva saṃsāra viccheda kāraṇam tad  pradarśayate sarva bhūta stham sarveṣu bhūteṣu sthitam svam ātmānam
