sarva bhūtāni ca ātmani brahma ādīni stamba paryantāni ca sarva bhūtāni ātmani  ekatām gatāni īkṣate paśyati yoga yukta ātmā samāhita antaḥkaraṇaḥ sarvatra sama darśanaḥ sarveṣu brahma ādi sthāvara anteṣu viṣameṣu sarva bhūteṣu samam nirviśeṣam brahma ātmā ekatva viṣayam darśanam jñānam yasya sa sarvatra sama darśanaḥ etasya ātmā ekatva darśanasya phalam ucyate yaḥ  mām paśyati vāsudevam sarvasya ātmānam sarvatra sarveṣu bhūteṣu sarvam ca brahma ādi bhūta jātam mayi sarva ātmani paśyati tasya evam ātmā ekatva darśinaḥ aham īśvaraḥ  na praṇaśyāmi na parokṣatām gamiṣyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati sa ca vidvān me mama vāsudevasya na praṇaśyati na parokṣaḥ  bhavati tasya ca mama ca eka ātmaka tvāt  sva ātmā hi nāma ātmanaḥ priya eva bhavati yasmāt  ca aham eva sarva ātmā ekatvadarśī iti  etad  pūrva loka artham samyak  darśanam anūdya tad phalam mokṣaḥ  abhidhīyate sarvathā sarva prakāraiḥ vartamānaḥ  api samyak darśī yogī mayi vaiṣṇave parame pade vartate nityam ukta eva saḥ na mokṣam prati kenacid  pratibadhyate iti  arthaḥ kim ca anyat  ātma aupamyena ātmā svayam eva upamīyate anayā iti  upamā tasyāḥ  upamāyā bhāva aupamyam tena ātma aupamyena sarvatra sarva bhūteṣu samam tulyam paśyati yaḥ  arjuna sa ca kim samam paśyati iti  ucyate yathā mama sukham iṣṭam tathā sarva prāṇinām sukham anukūlam vā śabdaḥ  ca arthe yadi vā yad  ca duḥkham mama pratikūlam aniṣṭam yathā tathā sarva prāṇinām duḥkham aniṣṭam pratikūlam iti  evam ātma aupamyena sukha duḥkhe anukūla pratikūle tulya tayā sarva bhūteṣu samam paśyati na kasyacid  pratikūlam ācarati ahiṃsaka iti  arthaḥ yaḥ evam ahiṃsakaḥ samyak  darśana niṣṭhaḥ sa yogī parama  utkṛṣṭaḥ  mataḥ  abhipretaḥ sarva yoginām madhye etasya yathā uktasya samyak darśana lakṣaṇasya yogasya duḥkha saṃpādyatām ālakṣya śuśruṣuḥ  dhruvam tad prāpti upāyam arjuna uvāca yaḥ  ayam yoga s tvayā proktaḥ sāmyena samatvena he madhusūdana etasya yogasya aham na paśyāmi na upalabhe cañcala tvāt  manasaḥ kim sthirām acalām sthitim asiddham tad  cañcalam hi manaḥ kṛṣṇa iti kṛṣateḥ  vilekhana arthasya rūpam bhakta jana pāpa ādi doṣa ākarṣāṇāt kṛṣṇaḥ tasya saṃbuddhiḥ he kṛṣṇa hi yasmāt  manaḥ  cañcalam na kevalam atyartham cañcalam pramāthi ca pramathana śīlam pramathnāti śarīram indriyāṇi ca vikṣipat  sat  para vaśīkaroti kim ca balavat  prabalam na kenacid  niyantum śakyam durnivāra tvāt  kim ca dṛḍham tantu nāgavat  acchedyam tasya evaṃbhūtasya manasaḥ  aham nigraham nirodham manye vāyoḥ  iva yathā vāyoḥ  duṣkaraḥ  nigrahas tatas  api duṣkaram manye iti  abhiprāyaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca evam etad  yathā bravīṣi asaṃśayam na asti saṃśayaḥ  manaḥ  durnigraham calam iti  atra he mahā bāhaḥ kiṃtu  abhyāsena tu  abhyāsaḥ  nāmaḥ  citta bhūmau kasyāṃcid  samāna pratyaya āvṛttiḥ  cittasya vairāgyeṇa vairāgyam nāma dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa iṣṭa bhogeṣu doṣa darśana abhyāsāt  vaitṛṣṇyam tena ca vairāgyeṇa gṛhyate vikṣepa rūpaḥ pracāraḥ  cittasya evam tad  manaḥ  gṛhyate nigṛhyate nirudhyata iti  arthaḥ yaḥ punar  asaṃyata ātmā tena asaṃyata ātmanā abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām asaṃyataḥ ātma antaḥkaraṇam yasya saḥ  ayam asaṃyata ātmā tena asaṃyata ātmanā yogaḥ  duṣprāpaḥ  duḥkhena prāpyata iti me matiḥ yaḥ  tu punar  vaśya ātma abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām vaśya tvam āpāditaḥ ātmā manaḥ  yasya saḥ  ayam vaśya ātmā tena vaśya ātmanā tu yatatā bhūyaḥ api prayatnam kurvatā śakyaḥ  avāptum yogar upāyataḥ yathā uktāt  upāyāt  tatra yoga abhyāsa aṅgīkaraṇena ihaloka para loka prāpti nimittāni karmāṇi saṃnyastāni yoga siddhi phalam ca mokṣa sādhanam samyak  darśanam na prāptam iti yogī yoga mārgāt  maraṇa kāle calita citta iti tasya nāśam āśaṅkayā arjuna uvāca ayatiḥ  aprayatnavān yoga mārge śraddhayā astikya buddhyā ca upetaḥ  yogāt  antakāle ca calitam mānasam manaḥ  yasya sa calita mānasaḥ  bhraṣṭa smṛtiḥ saḥ  aprāpya yoga saṃsiddhim yoga phalam samyak darśanam kām gatim he kṛṣṇa gacchati kaścid  kim na ubhaya vibhraṣṭaḥ karma mārgāt  yoga mārgāt  ca vibhraṣṭaḥ san chinna abhram iva naśyati kim vā na naśyati  apratiṣṭhaḥ  nirāśrayaḥ  he mahā bāhaḥ vimūḍhaḥ san brahmaṇaḥ pathi brahma prāpti mārge etad  me mama saṃśayam kṛṣṇaḥ  chettum apanetum arhasy aśeṣatas  tvad anya s tvad taḥ  anyaḥ ṛṣiḥ  devaḥ  vā cchettā nāśayitā saṃśayasya asya na hi yasmāt  upapadyate na saṃbhavati atas tvam eva cchettum arhasi iti  arthaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca he pārtha na eva iha loke na amutra parasmin vā loke vināśa s tasya vidyate na asti na āśaḥ nāma pūrvasmāt  hīna janma prāptiḥ sa yoga bhraṣṭasya na asti na hi yasmāt  kalyāṇa kṛt  śubha kṛt  kaścid  durgatim kutsitām gatim he tāta tanoti ātmānam putra rūpeṇa iti pitā tāta ucyate pitā eva putra iti putraḥ  api tāta ucyate śiṣyaḥ  api putra ucyate yatas  na gacchati kim tu  asya bhavati yoga mārge pravṛttaḥ saṃnyāsī sāmarthyāt  prāpya gatvā puṇya kṛtām aśvamedha ādi yājinām lokān tatra ca uṣitvā vāsam anubhūya śāśvatīḥ  nityāḥ samāḥ saṃvatsarān tad bhoga kṣaye śucīnām yathā ukta kāriṇām śrīmatām vibhūtimatām gehe gṛhe yoga bhraṣṭaḥ abhijāyate athavā śrīmatām kulāt  anyasmin yoginām eva daridrāṇām kule bhavati jāyate dhīmatām buddhimatām etad  hi janma yad  daridrāṇām yoginām kule durlabha taram duḥkhalabhyataram pūrvam apekṣya loke janma yad  īdṛśam yathā ukta viśeṣaṇe kule yasmāt  tatra yoginām kule tam buddhi saṃyogam buddhyā saṃyogam buddhi saṃyogam labhate paurvadehikam pūrvasmin dehe bhavam paurvadehikam yatate ca prayatnam ca karoti tatas  tasmāt  pūrva kṛtāt  saṃskārāt  bhūyaḥ bahutaram saṃsiddhau saṃsiddhi nimittam he kuru nandana katham pūrva deha buddhi saṃyoga iti tad  ucyate yaḥ pūrva janmani kṛtaḥ  abhyāsaḥ sa pūrva abhyāsaḥ tena eva balavatā hriyate saṃsiddhau hi yasmāt  avaśaḥ api sa yoga bhraṣṭaḥ na kṛtam ced  yoga abhyāsa jāt saṃskārāt  balavattaram adharma ādi lakṣaṇam karma tadā yoga abhyāsa janitena saṃskāreṇa hriyate adharmaḥ  ced  balavattaraḥ kṛtaḥ tena yoga jaḥ  api saṃskāraḥ  abhibhūyata eva tad kṣaye tu yoga jaḥ saṃskāraḥ svayam eva kāryam ārabhate na dīrgha kāla sthasya api vināśa s tasya asti iti  arthaḥ atas  jijñāsuḥ  api yogasya svarūpam jñātum icchan   api yoga mārge pravṛttaḥ saṃnyāsī yoga bhraṣṭaḥ sāmarthyāt  saḥ  api śabdabrahma veda ukta karma anuṣṭhāna phalam ativartate atikrāmati  apākariṣyati kim uta buddhvā yaḥ  yogam tad niṣṭhaḥ  abhyāsam kuryāt  kutas  ca yogi tvam śreya iti prayatnāt  yatamānaḥ adhikam yatamāna iti  arthaḥ tatra yogī vidvān saṃśuddha kilbiṣaḥ  viśuddha kilbiṣaḥ saṃśuddha pāpaḥ  aneka janma saṃsiddhiḥ  anekeṣu janmasu kiṃcid  kiṃcid  saṃskāra jātam upacitya tena upacitena aneka janma kṛtena saṃsiddhaḥ  aneka janma saṃsiddha s tatas  labdha samyak darśanaḥ san yāti parām prakṛṣṭam gatim yasmāt  evam tasmāt  tapasvibhyaḥ  adhikaḥ  yogī jñānibhyaḥ  api jñānam atra śāstra artha pāṇḍityam tadvadbhyaḥ  api mataḥ  jñātaḥ  adhikaḥ śreṣṭha iti karmibhyaḥ agni hotra ādi karma tadvadbhyaḥ  adhikaḥ  yogī viśiṣṭaḥ  yasmāt  tasmāt  yogī bhava arjuna yoginām api sarveṣām rūdrāt ityādi dhyāna parāṇām madhye mad gatena mayi vāsudeve samāhitena antarātmanā antaḥkaraṇena śraddhāvān śraddadhānaḥ san bhajate sevate yaḥ  mām sa me mama yuktatamaḥ  atiśayena yuktaḥ  mataḥ  abhipreta iti atha jñāna vijñāna yoga ākhyaḥ saptamaḥ  adhyāyaḥ yoginām api sarveṣām mad gatena antarātmanā śraddhāvān bhajate yaḥ  mām sa me yuktatamaḥ  mataḥ iti praśna bījam upanyasya svayam eva īdṛśam madīyam tattvam evam mad gata antarātmā syāt  iti  etad  vivakṣuḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca mayi vakṣyamāṇa viśeṣaṇe parameśvare āsaktam manaḥ  yasya saḥ mayi  āsakta manāḥ he pārtha   yogam yuñjan manaḥ samādhānam kurvan mad āśrayaḥ  aham eva parameśvaraḥ āśrayaḥ  yasya saḥ mad āśrayaḥ yaḥ  hi kaścid  puruṣa arthena kenacid  arthī bhavati sa tad sādhanam karma agni hotra ādi tapaḥ  dānam vā kiṃcid  āśrayam pratipadyate ayam tu yogī mām eva āśrayam pratipadyate hitvā anyat sādhana antaram mayi  eva āsakta manā bhavati yaḥ  tvam evaṃbhūtaḥ san asaṃśayam samagram samastam vibhūti bala śakti aiśvarya ādi guṇa saṃpannam mām yathā yena prakāreṇa jñāsyasi saṃśayam antareṇa evam eva bhagavān iti tad  sṛṇu ucyamānam mayā tad  ca mad viṣayam jñānam te tubhyam aham sa vijñānam vijñāna sahitam sva anubhava yuktam idam vakṣyāmi kathayiṣyāmi  aśeṣatas  kārtsnyena tad  jñānam vivakṣitam stauti śrotuḥ abhimukhīkaraṇāya yaj jñātvā yaj jñānam jñātvā na iha bhūyas  punar  anyat  jñātavyam puruṣa artha sādhanam avaśiṣyate na avaśiṣṭam bhavati iti mad tattva jñaḥ  yaḥ sa sarvajñaḥ  bhavati iti  arthaḥ atas  viśiṣṭa phala tvāt  durlabham jñānam katham iti  ucyate manuṣyāṇām madhye sahasreṣu anekeṣu kaścid  yatati prayatnam karoti siddhaye siddhi artham teṣām yatatām api siddhānām siddhā eva hi te ye mokṣāya yatante teṣām kaścid  eva hi mām vetti tattvataḥ  yathāvat  śrotāram prarocanena abhimukhīkṛtya āha bhūmiḥ pṛthivī tanmātram ucyate na sthūlā bhinnā prakṛtiḥ  aṣṭadhā iti vacanāt  tathā ābādayaḥ api tanmātrāṇi  eva ucyante āpaḥ  analaḥ  vāyuḥ kham mana iti manasaḥ kāraṇam ahaṃkāraḥ  gṛhyate buddhiḥ  iti  ahaṃkāra kāraṇam mahat tattvam ahaṃkāra iti  avidyā saṃyuktam avyaktam yathā viṣa saṃyuktam annam viṣam iti  ucyate evam ahaṃkāra vāsanāvat  avyaktam mūla kāraṇam ahaṃkāra iti  ucyate pravartaka tvāt  ahaṃkārasya ahaṃkāra eva hi sarvasya pravṛtti bījam dṛṣṭam loke iti iyam yathā uktā prakṛtiḥ  me mama aiśvarī māyā śaktiḥ  aṣṭadhā bhinnā bhedam āgatā aparā na parā nikṛṣṭa aśuddha anartha karī saṃsāra bandhana ātmikā iyam itas  asyāḥ yathā uktāya as tu  anyām viśuddhām prakṛtim mama ātma bhūtām viddhi me parām prakṛṣṭam jīva bhūtām kṣetrajña lakṣaṇām prāṇa dhāraṇa nimitta bhūtām he mahā bāhaḥ yayā prakṛtyā idam dhāryate jagad antar praviṣṭayā etad yonīni ete parāpare kṣetra kṣetrajña lakṣaṇe prakṛtī yoniḥ  yeṣām bhūtānām tāni etad yonīni bhūtāni sarvāṇi iti evam upadhāraya jānīhi yasmāt  mama prakṛti yoniḥ kāraṇam sarva bhūtānām atas  aham kṛtsnasya samastasya jagataḥ prabhava utpattiḥ pralayaḥ  vināśa s tathā prakṛti dvaya dvāreṇa aham sarvajña īśvaraḥ  jagataḥ kāraṇam iti  arthaḥ yatas  tasmāt  mattaḥ parameśvarāt  parataram anyat  kāraṇa antaram kiṃcid  na asti na vidyate aham eva jagat kāraṇam iti  arthaḥ he dhanaṃjaya yasmāt  evam tasmāt  mayi parameśvare sarvāṇi bhūtāni sarvam idam jagat  protam anusyūtam anugatam anuviddham grathitam iti  arthaḥ dīrgha tantuṣu paṭavat  sūtre ca maṇi gaṇā iva kena kena dharmeṇa viśiṣṭaḥ  tvayi sarvam idam protam iti  ucyate rasaḥ  aham apām yaḥ sāram sa rasaḥ tasmin rasa bhūte mayi āpaḥ protā iti  arthaḥ evam sarvatra yathā aham apsu rasaḥ evam prabhā asmi śaśi sūryayoḥ praṇava oṃkāraḥ sarva vedeṣu tasmin praṇava bhūte mayi sarve vedāḥ protāḥ tathā khe ākāśe śabdaḥ sāra bhūtaḥ tasmin mayi kham protam tathā pauruṣam puruṣasya bhāvaḥ pauruṣam yatas  puṃbuddhiḥ  nṛṣu tasmin mayi puruṣāḥ protāḥ puṇyaḥ surabhiḥ  gandhaḥ pṛthivyām ca aham tasmin mayi gandha bhūte pṛthivī protā puṇya tvam gandhasya svabhāvata eva pṛthivyām darśitam ap ādiṣu rasa ādeḥ puṇyatva upalakṣaṇa artham apuṇya tvam tu gandha ādīnām avidyā dharma ādi apekṣam saṃsāriṇām bhūta viśeṣa saṃsarga nimittam bhavati tejaḥ  ca dīptiḥ  ca asmi vibhāvasau agnau tathā jīvanam sarva bhūteṣu yena jīvanti sarvāṇi bhūtāni tad  jīvanam tapaḥ  ca asmi tapasviṣu tasmin tapasi mayi tapasvinaḥ protāḥ bījam praroha kāraṇam mām viddhi sarva bhūtānām he pārtha sanātanam cirantanam kim ca buddhiḥ  viveka śaktiḥ  antaḥkaraṇasya buddhimatām viveka śaktimatām asmi tejaḥ prāgalbhyam tadvatām tejasvinām aham balam sāmarthyam ojaḥ  balavatām aham tad  ca balam kāma rāga vivarjitam kāmaḥ  ca rāgaḥ  ca kāma rāgau kāma s tṛṣṇā saṃnikṛṣṭeṣu viṣayeṣu rāgaḥ  rañjanā prāpteṣu viṣayeṣu tābhyām kāma rāgābhyām vivarjitam deha ādi dhāraṇa mātra artham balam sattvam aham asmi na tu yad  saṃsāriṇām tṛṣṇā rāga kāraṇam kim ca dharma aviruddhaḥ dharmeṇa śāstra arthena aviruddhaḥ  yaḥ prāṇiṣu bhūteṣu kāmaḥ yathā deha dhāraṇa mātra ādi arthaḥ  aśana pāna ādi viṣayaḥ sa kāmaḥ  asmi he bharata ṛṣabha kiṃca ye ca eva sāttvikāḥ sattva nirvṛttā bhāvāḥ padārthāḥ rājasāḥ rajaḥ nirvṛttāḥ  tāmasa aḥ  tamaḥ niḥ vṛttāḥ  ca ye kecid  prāṇinām sva karma vaśāt jāyante bhāvāḥ tān matta eva jāyamānān iti evam viddhi sarvān samastān eva evam yadi  api te mattaḥ  jāyante tathā api na tu  aham teṣu tad adhīna s tad vaśaḥ yathā saṃsāriṇaḥ te punar  mayi mad vaśāḥ mad adhīnāḥ evaṃbhūtam api parameśvaram nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvam sarva bhūta ātmānam nirguṇam saṃsāra doṣa bīja pradāha kāraṇam mām na abhijānāti jagad iti  anukrośam darśayati bhagavān tad  ca kiṃnimittam jagataḥ  ajñānam iti  ucyate tribhiḥ  guṇa mayaiḥ guṇa vikāraiḥ rāga dveṣa moha ādi prakāraiḥ  bhāvaiḥ padārthaiḥ  ebhiḥ  yathā uktaiḥ sarvam idam prāṇi jātam jagan mohitam aviveki tām āpāditam san na abhijānāni mām ebhyaḥ  yathā uktebhyaḥ  guṇebhyaḥ param vyatiriktam vilakṣaṇam ca avyayam vyaya rahitam janma ādi sarva bhāva vikāra varjitam iti  arthaḥ katham punar  daivīm etām triguṇa ātmikām vaiṣṇavīm māyām atikrāmati iti  ucyate daivī devasya mama īśvarasya viṣṇoḥ svabhāva bhūtāḥ  hi yasmāt  eṣā yathā uktā guṇa mayī mama māyā duratyayā duḥkhena atyayaḥ  atikramaṇam yasyāḥ sā duratyayā tatra evam sati sarva dharmān parityajya mām eva māyāvinam sva ātma bhūtam sarva ātmanā ye prapadyante te māyām etām sarva bhūta mohinīm taranti  atikrāmanti te saṃsāra bandhanān mucyanta iti  arthaḥ yadi tvām prapannāḥ māyām etām taranti kasmāt  tvām eva sarve na prapadyante iti  ucyate na mām parameśvaram nārāyaṇam duṣkṛtinaḥ pāpa kāriṇaḥ mūḍhāḥ prapadyante nara adhamā narāṇām madhye adhamāḥ nikṛṣṭaḥ te ca māyayā apahṛta jñānāḥ saṃmuṣita jñānā āsuram bhāvam hiṃsā anṛta ādi lakṣaṇam āśritāḥ ye punar  nara uttamāḥ puṇya karmāṇaḥ caturvidhāḥ  catur prakārā bhajante sevante mām janāḥ sukṛtinaḥ puṇya karmāṇaḥ  he arjuna ārta ārti parigṛhīta s taskara vyāghra roga ādinā abhibhūta āpannaḥ jijñāsuḥ  bhagavat tattvam jñātum icchati yaḥ artha arthī dhana kāmaḥ jñānī viṣṇoḥ  tattva vid  ca he bharata ṛṣabha teṣām caturṇām madhye jñānī tattva vid  tattva vid tvān nitya yuktaḥ  bhavati eka bhaktiḥ  ca anyasya bhajanīyasya adarśanāt  atas  sa eka bhaktiḥ  viśiṣyate viśeṣam ādhikyam āpadyate atiricyata iti  arthaḥ priyaḥ  hi yasmāt  aham ātmā jñāninaḥ  atas tasya aham atyartham priyaḥ prasiddham hi loke ātmā priyaḥ  bhavati iti tasmāt  jñānina ātma tvāt  vāsudevaḥ priyaḥ  bhavati iti  arthaḥ sa ca jñānī mama vāsudevasya ātmā eva iti mama atyartham priyaḥ na tarhi  ārta ādayaḥ  trayaḥ  vāsudevasya priyāḥ na kim tarhi udārā utkṛṣṭāḥ sarva eva ete trayaḥ  api mama priyā eva iti  arthaḥ na hi kaścid  mad bhaktaḥ  vāsudevasya apriyaḥ  bhavati jñānī tu  atyartham priyaḥ  bhavati iti viśeṣaḥ tad  kasmāt  iti  ata āha jñānī tu  ātmā eva na anyaḥ  matta iti me mama matam niścayaḥ āsthita āroḍhum pravṛttaḥ sa jñānī hi yasmāt  aham eva bhagavān vāsudevaḥ  na anyaḥ  asmi iti  evam yukta ātmā samāhita cittaḥ san mām eva param brahma gantavyam anuttamām gatim gantum pravṛtta iti  arthaḥ jñānī punar  api stūyate bahūnām janmanām jñāna artha saṃskāra āśrayāṇām ante samāptau jñānavān prāpta paripāka jñānaḥ  mām vāsudevam pratyak ātmānam pratyakṣataḥ prapadyate katham vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti ya evam sarva ātmānam mām nārāyaṇam pratipadyate sa mahātmā na tad samaḥ  anyaḥ  asti adhikaḥ  vā atas  su durlabhaḥ manuṣyāṇām sahasreṣu  iti hi  uktam ātmā eva sarvm vāsudeva iti  evam apratipattau kāraṇam ucyate kāmaiḥ  taiḥ  taiḥ putra paśu svarga ādi viṣayaiḥ  hṛta jñānāḥ apahṛta viveka vijñānāḥ prapadyante anya devatāḥ prāpnuvanti vāsudevāt  ātmanaḥ  anyā devatāḥ tam tam niyamam devatā ārādhane prasiddhaḥ  yaḥ  yaḥ  niyamas tam tam āsthāya āśritya prakṛtyā svabhāvena janma antara arjita saṃskāra viśeṣeṇa niyatāḥ niyamitāḥ svayātmīyayā teṣām ca kāminām yaḥ  yaḥ kāmī yām yām devatā tanum śraddhayā saṃyuktaḥ  bhakta ś ca san   arcitum pūjayitum icchati tasya tasya kāminaḥ  acalām sthirām śraddhām tām eva vidadhāmi sthirīkaromi yayā eva pūrvam pravṛttaḥ svabhāvataḥ  yaḥ  yām devatā tanum śraddhayā arcitum icchati sa tayā mad vihitayā śraddhayā yuktaḥ san tasyāḥ  devatā tanvā rādhanam ārādhanam īhate ceṣṭate labhate ca tatas  tasyāḥ  ārādhitāyāḥ  devatā tanvāḥ kāmān īpsitān mayā eva parameśvareṇa sarvajñena karma phala vibhāga jñatayā vihitān nirmitān tān hi yasmāt  te bhagavatā vihitāḥ kāmāḥ  tasmāt  tān avaśyam labhate iti  arthaḥ hitān iti pada  chede hita tvam kāmānām upacaritam kalpyam na hi kāmā hitāḥ kasyacid  yasmāt  antavat  sādhana vyāpārauvivekinaḥ kāminaḥ  ca te atas  antavat  vināśi tu phalam teṣām tad  bhavati  alpa medhasām alpa prajñānām devān devayajaḥ  yānti devān yajanti iti devayajaḥ te devān yānti mad bhaktā yānti mām api evam samāne api  āyāse mām eva na prapadyante ananta phalāya ahaḥ khalu kaṣṭam vartata iti  anukrośam darśayati bhagavān kiṃnimittam mām eva na prapadyanta iti  ucyate avyaktam aprakāśam vyaktim āpannam prakāśam gatam idānīm manyante mām nitya prasiddham īśvaram api santam abuddhayaḥ  avivekinaḥ param bhāvam param ātma svarūpam ajānantaḥ  avivekinaḥ mama avyayam vyaya rahitam anuttamam niratiśayam madīyam bhāvam ajānantaḥ  manyanta iti  arthaḥ tad ajñānam kiṃnimittam iti  ucyate na aham prakāśaḥ sarvasya lokasya keṣāṃcid  eva mad bhaktānām prakāśaḥ  aham iti  abhiprāyaḥ yoga māyā samāvṛtaḥ  yogaḥ  guṇānām yuktiḥ  ghaṭanam sā eva māyā yoga māyā tayā yoga māyayā samāvṛtaḥ saṃchanna iti  arthaḥ ata eva mūḍhaḥ  lokaḥ  ayam na abhijānāti mām ajam avyayam yayā yoga māyayā samāvṛtam mām lokaḥ  na abhijānāti na asau yoga māyā madīyā satī mama īśvarasya māyāvinaḥ jñānam pratibadhnāti yathā anyasya api māyāvinaḥ māyā jñānam tadvat  yatas  evam atas  aham tu veda jāne samatītāni samatikrāntāni bhūtāni vartamānāni ca arjuna bhaviṣyāṇi ca bhūtāni veda aham mām tu veda na kaścana mad bhaktam mad śaraṇam ekam muktvā mad tattva vedanā bhāvāt  eva na mām bhajate kena punar  mad tattva vedana pratibandhena pratibaddhāni santi jāyamānāni sarva bhūtāni mām na vidanti iti  apekṣāyām idam āha icchā dveṣa samutthena icchā ca dveṣaḥ  ca icchā dveṣau tābhyām samuttiṣṭhati iti icchā dveṣa samuttha s tena icchā dveṣa samutthena kena iti viśeṣa apekṣāyām idam āha dvandva mohena dvandva nimittaḥ  mohaḥ  dvandva mohas tena tau   eva icchā dveṣau śīta uṣṇavat  paraspara viruddhau sukha duḥkha tad hetu viṣayau yathākālam sarva bhūtaiḥ saṃbadhyamānau dvandva śabdena abhidhīyete tatra yadā icchā dveṣau sukha duḥkha tad hetu saṃprāptyā labdha ātmakau bhavataḥ tadā tau sarva bhūtānām prajñāyāḥ sva vaśa āpādana dvāreṇa parama artha ātma tattva viṣaya jñāna utpatti pratibandha kāraṇam moham janayataḥ na hi icchā dveṣa doṣa vaśīkṛta cittasya yathābhūta artha viṣaya jñānam utpadyate bahis  api kim u vaktavyam tābhyām āviṣṭa buddheḥ saṃmūḍhasya pratyagātmani bahu pratibandhe jñānam na utpadyata iti atas tena icchā dveṣa samutthena dvandva mohena bhārata bharata anvayaja sarva bhūtāni saṃmohitāni santi saṃmoham saṃmūḍha tām sarge janmani utpatti kāle iti  etad  yānti gacchanti he paraṃtapa moha vaśāni  eva sarva bhūtāni jāyamānāni jāyanta iti  abhiprāyaḥ yata evam atas tena dvandva mohena pratibaddha prajñānāni sarva bhūtāni saṃmohitāni mām ātma bhūtam na jānanti ata eva ātma bhāvena mām na bhajante ke punar  anena dvandva mohena nirmuktāḥ santas tvām viditvā yathāśāstram ātma bhāve bhajanta iti  apekṣitam artham darśayitum ucyate yeṣām tu punar  anta gatam samāpta prāyam kṣīṇam pāpam janānām puṇya karmaṇām puṇyam karma yeṣām sattva śuddhi kāraṇam vidyate te puṇya karmāṇas teṣām puṇya karmaṇām te dvandva moha nirmuktā yathā uktena dvandva mohena nirmuktā bhajante mām paramātmanām dṛḍha vratāḥ evam eva parama artha tattvam na anyathā iti  evam sarva parityāga vratena niścita vijñānā dṛḍha vratā ucyante te kimartham bhajante iti  ucyate jarā maraṇa mokṣāya jarā maraṇayoḥ  mokṣa artham mām parameśvaram āśritya mad samāhita cittāḥ santaḥ  yatanti prayatante ye te yad  brahma param tad  viduḥ kṛtsnam samastam adhyātmam pratyagātma viṣayam vastu tad  viduḥ karma ca akhilam samastam viduḥ sa adhibhūta adhidaivam adhibhūtam ca adhidaivam ca adhibhūta adhidaivam saha adhibhūta adhidaivena vartata iti sa adhibhūta adhidaivam ca mām ye viduḥ sa adhiyajñam ca saha adhiyajñena sa adhiyajñam ye viduḥ prayāṇa kāle maraṇa kāle api ca mām te viduḥ yukta cetasaḥ samāhita cittā iti iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śrīmat bhagavat gīta ābhāṣye saptamaḥ  adhyāyaḥ te brahma tad  viduḥ kṛtsnam iti  ādinā bhagavatā arjunasya praśna bījāni upadiṣṭani atas tad praśna artham arjuna uvāca eṣām praśnānām yathākramam nirṇayāya śrī bhagavān uvāca akṣaram na kṣarati iti  akṣaram para ātmā etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi iti śruteḥ oṃkārasya ca om iti  eka akṣaram brahma iti pareṇa viśeṣaṇāt  agrahaṇam paramam iti ca niratiśaye brahmaṇi  akṣare upapannataram viśeṣaṇam tasya eva parasya brahmaṇaḥ prati deham pratyak ātma bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ svar  bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ  adhyātmam ucyate ātmānam deham adhikṛtya pratyagātma tayā pravṛttam parama artha brahma avasānam vastu svabhāvaḥ  adhyātmam ucyate adhyātma śabdena abhidhīyate bhūta bhāva udbhava karaḥ  bhūtānām bhāvaḥ bhūta bhāvaḥ  tasya udbhavaḥ  bhūta bhāva udbhavas tam karoti iti bhūta bhāva udbhava karaḥ bhūta vastu utpatti kara iti  arthaḥ visargaḥ  visarjanam devatā uddeśena caru puroḍāśa ādeḥ  dravyasya parityāgaḥ sa eṣa visarga lakṣaṇaḥ  yajñaḥ karma saṃjñitaḥ karma śabdita iti  etad  etasmāt  hi bīja bhūtāt  vṛṣṭi aḍa ādi krameṇa sthāvara jaṅgamāni bhūtāni  udbhavanti adhibhūtam prāṇi jātam adhikṛtya bhavati iti kaḥ  asau kṣaraḥ kṣarati iti kṣaraḥ vināśī bhāvaḥ yad  kiṃcid  janimat  vastu  iti  arthaḥ puruṣaḥ pūrṇam anena sarvam iti puri śayanāt  vā puruṣaḥ āditya antargataḥ  hiraṇyagarbhaḥ sarva prāṇi karaṇānām anugrāhakaḥ saḥ  adhidaivatam adhiyajñaḥ sarva yajña abhimāninī viṣṇu ākhyā devatā yajñaḥ  vai viṣṇuḥ iti śruteḥ sa hi viṣṇuḥ  aham eva atra asmin dehe yaḥ  yajñas tasya aham adhiyajñaḥ yajñaḥ  hi deha nirvartya tvena deha samavāyi iti deha adhikaraṇaḥ  bhavati dehabhṛtām vara   antakāle maraṇa kāle ca mām eva parameśvaram viṣṇum smaran muktvā parityajya kalevaram śarīram yaḥ prayāti gacchati sa mad bhāvam vaiṣṇavam tattvam yāti na asti na vidyate atra asmin   arthe saṃśayaḥ yāti vā na vā iti na mad viṣaya eva ayam niyamaḥ kim tarhi yam yam vā api yam yam bhāvam devatā viśeṣam smaran cintayan tyajati parityajati  ante anta kāle prāṇa viyoga kāle kalevaram śarīram tam tam eva smṛtam bhāvam eva eti na anyam kaunteya sadā sarvadā tad bhāva bhāvitas tasmin bhāvaḥ  tad bhāvaḥ sa bhāvitaḥ smaryamāṇa tayā abhyastaḥ  yena sa tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ san yasmāt  evam antyā bhāvanā deha antara prāptau kāraṇam tasmāt  sarveṣu kāleṣu mām anusmara yathāśāstram yudhyaḥ  ca yuddham svadharmam kuru mayi vāsudeve arpite manaḥ buddhī yasya tava sa tvam mayi  arpita manaḥ buddhiḥ san mām eva yathāsmṛtam eṣyasy āgamiṣyasi asaṃśayaḥ  na saṃśayaḥ  atra vidyate kiṃca abhyāsa yoga yuktena mayi citta samarpaṇa viṣaya bhūta  ekasmin   tulya pratyaya avṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ  vilakṣaṇa pratyaya anantaritaḥ  abhyāsaḥ sa ca abhyāsaḥ  yoga s tena yuktam tatra eva vyāpṛtam yoginaḥ  cetas tena cetasā na anya gāminā na anyatra viṣaya antare gantum śīlam asya iti na anya gāmi tena na anya gāminā paramam niratiśayam puruṣam divyam divi sūrya maṇḍāle bhavam yāti gacchati he pārtha anucintayan śāstra ācārya upadeśam anudhyāyan iti  etad  kiṃviśiṣṭam ca puraṣam yāti iti  ucyate kavim krānta darśinam sarvajñam purāṇam cirantanam anuśāsitāram sarvasya jagataḥ praśāsitāram aṇoḥ sūkṣmāt  api  aṇīyāṃsam sūkṣmataram anusmaret  anucintayet  yaḥ kaścid  sarvasya karma phala jātasya dhātāram vidhātāram vicitra tayā prāṇibhyaḥ  vibhaktāram acintya rūpam na asya rūpam niyatam vidyamānam api kenacid  cintayitum śakyata iti  acintya rūpas tam āditya varṇam ādityasya iva nitya caitanya prakāśaḥ  varṇaḥ  yasya tam āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt  ajñāna lakṣaṇān moha andhakārāt param tam anucintayat  yāti iti pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ kiṃca prayāṇa kāle maraṇa kāle manasā acalena calana varjitena bhaktyā yuktaḥ  bhajanam bhaktis tayā yuktaḥ  yoga balena ca eva yogasya balam yoga balam samādhi ja saṃskāra pracaya janita citta sthairya lakṣaṇam yoga balam tena ca yukta iti  arthaḥ pūrvam hṛdaya puṇḍārīke vaśīkṛtya cittam tatas  ūrdhva gāminyā nāḍyā bhūmi jaya krameṇa bhruvoḥ  madhye prāṇam āveśya sthāpayitvā samyak āpramattaḥ san sa evam buddhimān yogī kavim purāṇam iti  ādi lakṣaṇam tam param parataram puruṣam upaiti pratipadyate divyam dyotana ātmakam punar  api vakṣyamāṇena upāyena pratipitsitasya brahmaṇaḥ  veda vid vadana ādi viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyasya abhidhānam karoti bhagavān yad  akṣaram na kṣarati iti  akṣaram avināśi veda vidaḥ  veda artha jñāḥ vadanti tad  vā etad  akṣaram gārgi brāhmaṇā abhivadanti iti śruteḥ sarva viśeṣa nivartaka tvena abhivadanti  asthūlam aṇu  iti  ādi kim ca viśanti praviśanti samyak darśana prāptau satyām yad  yatayaḥ  yatana śīlāḥ saṃnyāsinaḥ  vīta rāgāḥ vītaḥ  vigataḥ rāgaḥ  yebhyas te vīta rāgāḥ yad  ca akṣaram icchantaḥ  jñātum iti vākya śeṣaḥ brahmacaryam gurau caranti ācaranti tad  te padam tad  akṣara ākhyam padam padanīyam te tava saṃgraheṇa saṃgrahaḥ saṃkṣepaḥ  tena saṃkṣepeṇa pravakṣye kathayiṣyāmi sa yaḥ  ha vai tad  bhagavan manuṣyeṣu prāyaṇa antam oṃkāram abhidhyāyīta katamam vāva sa tena lokam jayati iti tasmai sa ha uvāca etad  vai satyakāma param ca aparam ca brahma yad  oṃkāraḥ iti  upakramya yaḥ punar  etam tri mātreṇa om iti  etena eva akṣareṇa param puruṣam abhidhyāyīta sa sāmabhiḥ  unnīyate brahma lokam iti  ādinā vacanena anyatra dharmāt  anyatra adharmāt  iti ca upakramya sarve vedā yad  padam āmananti tapāṃsi sarvāṇi ca yad  vadanti yad  icchantaḥ  brahmacaryam caranti tad  te padam saṃgraheṇa bravīmi  om iti  etad  iti  ādibhiḥ  ca vacanaiḥ parasya brahmaṇaḥ  vācaka rūpeṇa pratimāvat  pratīka rūpeṇa vā para brahma pratipatti sādhana tvena manda madhyama buddhīnām vivakṣitasya oṃkārasya upāsanam kāla antare mukti phalam uktam yad  tad  eva iha api kavim purāṇam anuśāsitāram yad  akṣaram veda vidaḥ  vadanti iti ca upanyastasya parasya brahmaṇaḥ pūrva ukta rūpeṇa pratipatti upāya bhūtasya oṃkārasya kāla antara mukti phalam upāsanam yoga dhāraṇā sahitam vaktavyam prasakta anuprasaktam ca yad  kiṃcid  iti  evam artha uttare grantha ārabhyate sarva dvārāṇi sarvāṇi ca tāni dvārāṇi ca sarva dvārāṇi  upalabdhau tāni sarvāṇi saṃyasya saṃyamanam kṛtvā manaḥ  hṛdi hṛdaya puṇḍārīke nirūdhya nirodham kṛtvā niṣpracāram āpādya tatra vaśīkṛtena manasā hṛdayāt  ūrdhva gāminyā nāḍyā ūrdhvam ārūhya mūrdhni  ādhāya ātmanaḥ prāṇam āsthitaḥ pṛvṛttaḥ  yoga dhāraṇām dhārayitum tatra eva ca dhārayan om iti eka akṣaram brahma brahmaṇaḥ  abhidhāna bhūtam oṃkāram vyāharan ucārayan tad artha bhūtam mām īśvaram anusmaran anucintayan yaḥ prayāti mriyate sa tyajan parityajan deham śarīram tyajan deham iti prayāṇa viśeṣaṇa artham dehatyāgena prayāṇam ātmanaḥ na svarūpa nāśena iti  arthaḥ sa evam yāti gacchati paramām prakṛṣṭām gatim kiṃca ananya cetāḥ  na anya viṣaye cetaḥ  yasya saḥ  ayam ananya cetāḥ yogī satatam sarvadā yaḥ  mām parameśvaram smarati nityaśas  satatam iti nairantaryam ucyate nityaśas  iti dīrgha kāla tvam ucyate na ṣaṣ māsam saṃvatsaram vā kim tarhi yāvat jīvam nairantaryeṇa yaḥ  mām smarati iti  arthaḥ tasya yoginaḥ  aham sulabhaḥ sukhena labhyaḥ  he pārtha nitya yuktasya sadā samāhita cittasya yoginaḥ yata evam atas  ananya cetāḥ san mayi sadā samāhitaḥ  bhavet  tava saulabhyena kim syāt  iti  ucyate sṛṇu tad  mama saulabhyena yad  bhavati mām upetya mām īśvaram upetya mad bhāvam āpadya punar  janma punar  utpattim na āpnuvanti na prāpnuvanti kiṃviśiṣṭam punarjanma na prāpnuvanti iti tad viśeṣaṇam āha duḥkha ālayam duḥkhānām ādhyātmika ādīnām ālayam āśrayam ālīyante yasmin duḥkhāni iti duḥkha ālayam janma na kevalam duḥkha ālayam aśāśvatam anavasthita svarūpam ca na āpnuvanti īdṛśam punarjanma mahātmānaḥ  yatayaḥ saṃsiddhim mokṣa ākhyām paramām prakṛṣṭām gatāḥ prāptāḥ ye punar  mām na prāpnuvanti te punar  āvartante kim punar  tvad taḥ  anyat  prāptāḥ punar  āvartante iti  ucyate ā brahma bhuvanāt  bhavanti  asmin bhūtāni iti bhuvanam brahmaṇaḥ  bhuvanam brahma bhuvanam brahma loke  iti  arthaḥ ā brahma bhuvanāt  saha brahma bhuvanena lokāḥ sarve punarāvartinaḥ punar āvartana svabhāvāḥ he arjuna mām ekam upetya tu kaunteya punarjanma punar utpattiḥ na vidyate brahma loka sahitā lokāḥ kasmāt  punarāvartinaḥ kāla paricchinna tvāt  katham sahasra yuga paryantam sahasrāṇi yugāni paryantaḥ paryavasānam yasya ahna s tad  ahar  sahasra yuga paryantam brahmaṇaḥ prajāpateḥ  virājaḥ  viduḥ rātrim api yuga sahasra antām ahar parimāṇām eva ke viduḥ  iti  āha te ahorātra vidaḥ kāla saṃkhyā vidaḥ  janā iti  arthaḥ yata evam kāla paricchinnā aḥ  te atas  punarāvartinaḥ lokāḥ prajāpateḥ  ahani yad  bhavati rātrau ca tad  ucyate avyaktāt  avyaktam prajāpateḥ svāpa avasthā tasmāt  avyaktāt  vyaktayaḥ vyajyanta iti vyaktayaḥ sthāvara jaṅgama lakṣaṇāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ prabhavanti  abhivyajyante ahna āgamaḥ  aharāgamas tasmin ahar āgame kāle brahmaṇaḥ prabodha kāle tathā rātri āgame brahmaṇaḥ svāpa kāle pralīyante sarvā vyaktayaḥ  tatra eva pūrva ukte avyakta saṃjñake akṛta abhyāgama kṛta vipraṇāśa doṣa parihāra artham bandha mokṣa śāstra pravṛtti sāphalya pradarśana artham avidyā ādi kleśa mūla karma āśaya vaśāt  ca avaśaḥ bhūta grāmaḥ  bhūtvā bhūtvā pralīyata iti  atas  saṃsāre vairāgya pradarśana artham ca idam āha bhūta grāmaḥ  bhūta samudāyaḥ sthāvara jaṅgama lakṣaṇaḥ  yaḥ pūrvasmin kalpa āsīt  sa eva ayam na anyaḥ bhūtvā bhūtvā ahara āgame pralīyate punar  punar  rātri āgame ahnaḥ kṣaye avaśaḥ asvatantra eva he pārtha prabhavati jāyate avaśa eva aharāgame yad  upanyastam akṣaram tasya prāpti upāyaḥ  nirdiṣṭa om iti  eka akṣaram brahma iti  ādinā atha idānīm akṣarasya eva svarūpa nirdidikṣayedam ucyate anena yoga mārgeṇa idam gantavyam iti paraḥ  vyatiriktaḥ  bhinnaḥ kutas  tasmāt  pūrva uktāt  tuśabdaḥ  akṣarasya vivakṣitasya avyaktād vailakṣaṇya viśeṣaṇa arthaḥ bhāvaḥ akṣara ākhyam param brahma vyatirikta tve sati  api sā lakṣaṇya prasaṅgaḥ  asti iti tad vinivṛtti artham āha anya iti anyaḥ  vilakṣaṇaḥ sa ca avyaktaḥ  anindriya gocaraḥ para s tasmāt  iti  uktam kasmāt  punar  paraḥ pūrva uktāt  bhūta grāma bīja bhūtāt  avidyā lakṣaṇāt  avyaktāt  anyaḥ  vilakṣaṇaḥ  bhāva iti  abhiprāyaḥ sanātanaḥ  cirantanaḥ yaḥ sa bhāvaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu brahma ādiṣu naśyatsu na vinaśyati yaḥ  asau   avyaktaḥ  akṣara iti  ukta s tam eva akṣara saṃjñakam avyaktam bhāvam āhuḥ paramām prakṛṣṭām gatim yam param bhāvam prāpya gatvā na nivartante saṃsārāya tad  dhāma sthānam paramam prakṛṣṭam mama viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti  arthaḥ tad labdheḥ  upāya ucyate puruṣaḥ puri śayanāt  pūrṇa tvāt  vā sa paraḥ pārtha paraḥ  niratiśayaḥ yasmāt  puruṣān na param kiṃcid  sa bhaktyā labhya s tu jñāna lakṣaṇayā ananyayā ātma viṣayayā yasya puruṣasya antar sthāni madhya sthāni bhūtāni kārya bhūtāni kāryam hi kāraṇasya antar varti bhavati yena puruṣeṇa sarvam idam jagat  tatam vyāptam ākāśena iva ghaṭa ādi prakṛtānām yoginām praṇava āveśita brahma buddhīnām kāla antara mukti bhājām brahma pratipattaya uttaraḥ  mārgaḥ  vaktavya iti yatra kāle iti  ādi vivakṣita artha samarpaṇa artham ucyate āvṛtti mārga upanyāsaḥ itara mārga stuti artham ucyate yatra kāle prayātā iti vyavahitena saṃbandhaḥ yatra yasmin kāle tu  anāvṛttim apunarjanma āvṛttim tad viparītām ca eva yogina iti yoginaḥ karmiṇaḥ  cocyante karmiṇas tu guṇataḥ karma yogena yoginām iti viśeṣaṇāt  yoginaḥ yatra kāle prayātā mṛtā yoginaḥ  anāvṛttim yānti yatra kāle ca prayātāḥ āvṛttim yānti tam kālam vakṣyāmi bharata ṛṣabha tam kālam āha agniḥ kāla abhimāninī devatā tathā jyotiḥ  api devatā eva kāla abhimāninī athavā agni jyotiṣī yathā śrute eva devate bhūyasā tu nirdeśaḥ  yatra kāle tam kālam iti āmra vanavat  tathā ahar devatā harabhimāninī śuklaḥ śukla pakṣa devatā ṣaṣ māsā uttarāyaṇam tatra api devatā eva mārga bhūtā iti sthitaḥ  anyatra ayam nyāyaḥ tatra tasmin mārge prayātā mṛtā gacchanti brahma brahma vidaḥ  brahma upāsakā brahma upāsana parā janāḥ krameṇa iti vākya śeṣaḥ na hi sadyas mukti bhājām samyak  darśana niṣṭhānām gatiḥ  āgatiḥ  vā kvacid  asti na tasya prāṇā utkrāmanti iti śruteḥ brahma saṃlīna prāṇa eva te brahma mayā brahma bhūtā eva te dhūmaḥ  rātriḥ  dhūma abhimāninī rātrī abhimāninī ca devatā tathā kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇa pakṣa devatā ṣaṣ māsā dakṣiṇāyanam iti ca pūrvavat  devatā eva tatra candramasi bhavam cāndramasam jyotiḥ phalam iṣṭa ādi kārī yogī karmī prāpya bhuktvā tad kṣayāt  iha punar  nivartate śukla kṛṣṇe śuklā ca kṛṣṇā ca śukla kṛṣṇe jñāna prakāśaka tvāt  śuklā tad abhāvāt kṛṣṇā ete śukla kṛṣṇe hi gatī jagataḥ iti  adhikṛtānām jñāna karmaṇoḥ na jagataḥ sarvasya eva ete gatī saṃbhavataḥ śāśvate nitye saṃsārasya nitya tvāt  mate abhiprete tatra ekayā śuklayā yāti  anāvṛttim anyayā itarayā āvartate punar  bhūyas  na ete yathā ukte sṛtī mārgau pārtha jānan saṃsārāya ekā anyā mokṣāya iti yogī na muhyati kaścana kaścid  api tasmāt  sarveṣu kāleṣu yoga yuktaḥ samāhitaḥ  bhava arjuna śṛṇu tasya yogasya māhātmyam vedeṣu samyak adhīteṣu yajñeṣu ca sādguṇyena anutiṣṭhiteṣu tapaḥsu ca su tapteṣu dāneṣu ca samyak datteṣu yad  eteṣu puṇya phalam puṇyasya phalam puṇya phalam pradiṣṭam śāstreṇa atyeti  atītya gacchati sat  sarvam phala jātam idam viditvā sapta praśna nirṇaya dvāreṇa uktam artham samyak  avadhārya anuṣṭhāya yogī param prakṛṣṭam aiśvaram sthānam upaiti ca pratipadyate ādyam ādau bhavam kāraṇam brahma iti  arthaḥ atha rāja vidyā rāja guhya yogaḥ  nāma navamaḥ  adhyāyaḥ aṣṭame nāḍī ādi dvāreṇa dhāraṇā yogaḥ sa guṇa uktaḥ tasya ca phalam agni arcira ādi krameṇa kāla antare brahma prāpti lakṣaṇam eva anāvṛtti rūpam nirdiṣṭam tatra anena eva prakāreṇa mokṣa prāpti phalam adhigamyate na anyathā iti tad  āśaṅkāvyāvivartayiṣayā śrī bhagavān uvāca idam brahma jñānam vakṣyamāṇam uktam ca pūrveṣu adhyāyeṣu tad  buddhau saṃnidhīkṛtya idam iti  āha tuśabdaḥ  viśeṣa nirdhāraṇa arthaḥ idam eva tu samyak jñānam sākṣāt  mokṣa prāpti sādhanam vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti ātmā eva idam sarvam ekam eva advitīyam iti  ādi śruti smṛtibhyaḥ na anyat  atha te ye anyathā atas  viduḥ  anya rājānaḥ  te kṣayya lokā bhavanti iti  ādi śrutibhyaś ca te tubhyam guhyatamam gopyatamam pravakṣyāmi kathayiṣyāmi  anasūyave asūyā rahitāya kim tad  jñānam kiṃviśiṣṭam vijñāna sahitam anubhava yuktam yaj jñātvā prāpya mokṣyase aśubhāt  saṃsāra bandhanāt  tad ca rāja vidyā vidyānām rājā dīpti atiśayavat tvāt  dīpyate hi iyam atiśayena brahma vidyā sarva vidyānām tathā rāja guhyam guhyānām rājā pavitram pāvanam idam uttamam sarveṣām pāvanānām śuddhi kāraṇam brahma jñānam utkṛṣṭatamam aneka janma sahasra saṃcitam api dharma adharma ādi sa mūlam karma kṣaṇa mātrād eva bhasmīkaroti iti  atas  kim tasya pāvana tvam vaktavyam kim ca pratyakṣa avagamam pratyakṣeṇa sukha ādeḥ  iva avagamaḥ  yasya tad  pratyakṣa avagamam aneka guṇavataḥ  api dharma viruddha tvam dṛṣṭam na tathā ātma jñānam dharma virodhi kiṃtu dharmyam dharmāt  anapetam evam api syāt  duḥkha saṃpādyam iti  ata āha su sukham kartum yathā ratna viveka vijñānam tatra alpa āyāsānām anyeṣām karmaṇām sukha saṃpādyānām alpa phala tvam duṣkarāṇām ca mahā phala tvam dṛṣṭam iti idam tu sukha saṃpādya tvāt phala kṣayāt  vyeti iti prāpte āha avyayam iti na asya phalataḥ karmavat  vyayaḥ  asti iti  avyayam atas  śraddheyam ātma jñānam ye punar  aśraddadhānāḥ śraddhā virahitā ātma jñānasya dharmasya asya svarūpe tad phale ca nāstikāḥ pāpa kāriṇaḥ asurāṇām upaniṣadam deha mātra ātma darśanam eva pratipannāḥ asutṛpaḥ pāpāḥ puruṣā aśraddadhānāḥ paraṃtapa   aprāpya mām parameśvaram mad prāptau na eva āśaṅka iti mad prāpti mārga bheda bhakti mātram api  aprāpya iti  arthaḥ nivartante niścayena vartante kva mṛtyu saṃsāra vartmani mṛtyu yuktaḥ saṃsāraḥ  mṛtyu saṃsāra s tasya vartma naraka tiryak ādi prāpti mārgaḥ tasmin   eva vartanta iti  arthaḥ stutya arjunam abhimukhīkṛtya āha mayā mama yaḥ paraḥ  bhāvaḥ  tena tatam vyāptam sarvam idam jagad avyakta mūrtinā na vyaktā mūrtiḥ svarūpam yasya mama saḥ  aham avyakta mūrtis tena mayā avyakta mūrtinā karaṇa agocara svarūpeṇa iti  arthaḥ tasmin mayi  avyakta mūrtau sthitāni mad sthāni sarva bhūtāni brahma ādīni stamba paryantāni na hi nirātmakam kiṃcid  bhūtam vyavahārāya avakalpate atas  mad sthāni mayā ātmanā ātmavat tvena sthitāni atas  mayi sthitāni iti  ucyante teṣām bhūtānām aham eva ātmā iti  atas teṣu sthita iti mūḍha buddhīnām avabhāsate atas  bravīmi na ca aham teṣu bhūteṣu  avasthitaḥ mūrtavat  saṃśleṣa abhāvena ākāśasya api  antaratamaḥ  hi  aham na hi  asaṃsargi vastu kvacid  ādheya bhāvena avasthitam bhavati ata eva asaṃsargi tvān mama na ca mad sthāni bhūtāni brahma ādīni paśya me yogam yuktim ghaṭānam me mama aiśvaram īśvarasya imam aiśvaram yogam ātmanaḥ  yāthātmyam iti  arthaḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ  asaṃsargi tvāt  asaṅga tām darśayati asaṅgaḥ  na hi sajjate iti idam ca āścaryam anyat  paśya bhūtabhṛt  asaṅgaḥ  api san bhūtāni bibharti na ca bhūta sthaḥ yathā uktena nyāyena darśita tvāt  bhūta sthatva anupapatteḥ katham punar  ucyate asau mama ātmā iti vibhajya deha ādi saṅghātam tasmin   ahaṃkāram adhyāropya loka buddhim anusaran vyapadiśati mama ātmā iti na punar  ātmana ātmā anya iti lokavat  ajānan tathā bhūta bhāvanaḥ  bhūtāni bhāvayati  utpādayati vardhayati iti vā bhūtabhāvanaḥ yathā uktena śloka dvayena uktam artham dṛṣṭantena upapādayan   āha yathā loke ākāśa sthita ākāśe sthitaḥ  nityam sadā vāyuḥ sarvatra gacchati iti sarvatragaḥ mahān parimāṇataḥ tathā ākāśavat  sarva gate mayi  asaṃśleṣeṇa eva sthitāni iti  evam upadhāraya vijānīhi evam vāyuḥ  ākāśe iva mayi sthitāni sarva bhūtāni sthiti kāle tāni sarva bhūtāni kaunteya prakṛtim triguṇa ātmikām aparām nikṛṣṭam yānti māmikām madīyām kalpa kṣaye pralaya kāle punar  bhūyas  tāni bhūtāni utpatti kāle kalpa ādau visṛjāmi utpādayāmi  aham pūrvavat  evam avidyā lakṣaṇām prakṛtim svām svīyām avaṣṭabhya vaśīkṛtya visṛjāmi punar  punar  prakṛtitaḥ  jātam bhūta grāmam bhūta samudāyam imam vartamānam kṛtsnam avaśam asvatantram avidyā ādi doṣaiḥ para vaśīkṛtam prakṛteḥ  vaśāt  svabhāva vaśāt  tarhi tasya te parameśvarasya bhūta grāmam imam viṣamam vidadhataḥ tad nimittābhyām dharma adharmābhyām saṃbandhaḥ syāt  iti idam āha bhagavān na ca mām īśvaram tāni bhūta grāmasya viṣama sarga nimittāni karmāṇi nibadhnanti dhanaṃjaya tatra karmaṇām asaṃbandhi tve kāraṇam āha udāsīnavat  āsīnam yathā udīsīna upekṣakaḥ kaścid  tadvat  āsīnam ātmanaḥ  avikriya tvāt  asaktam phala āsaṅga rahitam abhimāna varjitam aham karomi iti teṣu karmasu atas  anyasya api kartṛtva abhimāna abhāvaḥ phala āsaṅga abhāvaḥ  ca asaṃbandha kāraṇam anyathā karmabhiḥ  badhyate mūḍhaḥ kośakāravat  iti  abhiprāyaḥ tatra bhūta grāmam imam visṛjāmi  udāsīnavat  āsīnam iti ca viruddham ucyate iti tad parihāra artham āha mayā adhyakṣeṇa sarvatas  dṛśi mātra svarupeṇa avikriyā ātmanā adhyakṣeṇa mayā mama māyā triguṇa ātmikā vidyā lakṣaṇā prakṛtiḥ sūyate utpādayati sacarācaram jagat  tathā ca mantra varṇaḥ ekaḥ  devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta antarātmā karma adhyakṣaḥ sarva bhūta adhivāsaḥ sākṣī cetā kevalaḥ  nirguṇaḥ  ca iti hetunā nimittena anena adhyakṣa tvena kaunteya jagat  sacarācaram vyakta avyakta ātmakam viparivartate sarva avasthāsu dṛśi karmatva apatti nimittā hi jagataḥ sarvā pravṛttiḥ aham idam bhokṣye paśyāmi idam śṛṇomi idam sukham anubhavāmi duḥkham anubhavāmi tad artham idam kariṣye idam jñāsyāmi iti  ādya avagati niṣṭhau  agati avasānā eva yaḥ  asya adhyakṣaḥ parame vyoman iti  ādayaś ca mantrā etam artham darśayanti tatas  ca ekasya devasya sarva adhyakṣa bhūta caitanya mātrasya paramārthataḥ sarva bhogān abhisaṃbandhinaḥ  anyasya cetanā antarasya abhāve bhoktuḥ  anyasya abhāvāt  kiṃnimittā iyam sṛṣṭiḥ  iti  atra praśna prativacane anupapanne kaḥ  addhā veda ka iha pravocat  kuta ājātā kuta iyam visṛṣṭiḥ iti  ādi mantra varṇebhyaḥ darśitam ca bhagavatā ajñānena āvṛtam jñānam tena muhyanti jantavaḥ iti evam mām nitya śuddha buddham ukta svabhāvam sarvajñam sarva jantūnām ātmānam api santam avajānanti  avajñām paribhavam kurvanti mām mūḍhā avivekinaḥ mānuṣīm manuṣya saṃbandhinīm tanum deham āśritam manuṣya dehena vyavaharantam iti  etad  param prakṛṣṭam bhāvam param ātma tattvam ākāśa kalpam ākāśāt  api  antaratamam ajānantaḥ  mama bhūta maheśvaram sarva bhūtānām mahāntam īśvaram sva ātmānam tatas  ca tasya mama avajñāna bhāvanena āhata aḥ  te varākāḥ katham mogha āśā vṛthā āśā āśiṣaḥ yeṣām te mogha āśāḥ tathā mogha karmāṇaḥ  yāni ca agnihotra ādīni taiḥ  anuṣṭhīyamānāni karmāṇi tāni ca teṣām bhagavat paribhavāt  sva ātma bhūtasya avajñānāt moghāni  eva niṣphalāni karmāṇi bhavanti iti mogha karmāṇaḥ tathā mogha jñānā mogham niṣphalam jñānam yeṣām te mogha jñānāḥ jñānam api teṣām niṣphalam eva syāt  vicetasaḥ  vigata viveka aḥ  ca te bhavanti iti  abhiprāyaḥ kim ca te bhavanti rākṣasīm rakṣasām prakṛtim svabhāvam āsurīm asurāṇām ca prakṛtim mohinīm moha karīm deha ātma vādinīm śritāḥ āśritāḥ chindhi bhindhi piba khāda para svam apahara iti  evam vadana śīlāḥ krūra karmāṇaḥ  bhavanti iti  arthaḥ asuryā nāma te lokāḥ iti śruteḥ ye punar  śraddadhānā bhagavat bhakti lakṣaṇe mokṣa mārge pravṛttāḥ mahātamānaḥ  tu  akṣudra cittāḥ mām īśvaram pārtha daivīm devānām prakṛtim śama damadayā śraddhā ādi lakṣaṇām āśritāḥ santaḥ  bhajanti sevante ananya manasaḥ  ananya cittā jñātvā bhūtādim bhūtānām viyat ādīnām prāṇinām ca ādim kāraṇam avyayam katham satatam sarvadā bhagavantam brahma svarūpam mām kīrtayantaḥ yatantaḥ  ca indriya upasaṃhāra śama dama dayā hiṃsā ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ  dharmaiḥ prayatantaḥ  ca dṛḍha vratā dṛḍham sthiram acālyam vratam yeṣām te dṛḍha vratā namasyantaś ca mām hṛdayeśayam ātmānam bhaktyā nitya yuktāḥ santa upāsate sevante te kena kena prakāreṇa upāsate iti  ucyate jñāna yajñena jñānam eva bhagavat viṣayam yajñas tena jñāna yajñena yajantaḥ pūjayantaḥ mām īśvaram ca api  anye anyām upāsanām parityajya upāsate tad  ca jñānam eka tvena ekam eva param brahma iti parama artha darśanena yajanta upāsate kecid  ca pṛthaktvena āditya candra ādi bhedena sa eva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ  avasthita iti  upāsate kecid  bahudhā avasthitaḥ sa eva bhagavān sarvatomukhaḥ  viśvarūpa iti tam viśvarūpam sarvatomukham bahudhā bahu prakāreṇa upāsate yadi bahubhiḥ prakāraiḥ  upāsate katham tvām eva upāsata iti ata āha aham kratuḥ śrauta karma bhedaḥ  aham eva aham yajñaḥ smārtaḥ kim ca svadhā annam aham pitṛbhyaḥ  yad  dīyate aham auṣadham sarva prāṇibhiḥ  yad  adyate tad  auṣadha śabda śabditam vrīhi yava ādi sādhāraṇam athavā svadhā iti sarva prāṇi sādhāraṇam annam auṣadham iti vyādhi upaśamana artham bheṣajam mantraḥ  aham yena pitṛbhyaḥ  devatā abhyaś ca havir dīyate aham eva ājyam haviś ca aham agniḥ yasmin hūte haviḥ saḥ  agniḥ  aham aham hutam havana karmaḥ  ca kiṃca pitā janayitā aham asya jagataḥ mātā janayitrī dhātā karma phalasya prāṇibhyaḥ  vidhātā pitāmahaḥ pituḥ pitā vedyam veditavyam pavitram pāvanam oṃkāraḥ ṛc  sāma yajue eva ca kiṃca gatiḥ karma phalam bhartā poṣṭā prabhuḥ svāmī sākṣī prāṇinām kṛta akṛtasya nivāsaḥ  yasmin prāṇinaḥ  nivasanti śaraṇam ārtānām prapannānām ārti haraḥ suhṛd  pratyupakāra anapekṣaḥ san   upakārī prabhava utpattiḥ  jagataḥ pralayaḥ pralīyate asmin iti tathā sthānam tiṣṭhati  asmin   iti nidhānam nikṣepaḥ kāla antara upabhogyam prāṇinām bījam praroha kāraṇam praroha dharmiṇām avyayam yāvat saṃsāra bhāvi tvāt avyayam na hi  abījam kiṃcid  prarohati nityam ca praroha darśanāt  bīja saṃtatiḥ  na vyeti iti gamyate kiṃca tapāmi  aham ādityaḥ  bhūtvā kaiścid  raśmibhiḥ  ulbaṇaiḥ aham varṣam kaiścid  raśmibhiḥ  utsṛjāmi utsṛjya punar  nigṛhṇāmi kaiścid  raśmibhiḥ  aṣṭabhiḥ  māsaiḥ punar  utsṛjāmi prāvṛṣi amṛtam ca eva devānām mṛtyuḥ  ca martyānām sat  yasya yad  saṃbandhi tayā vidyamānam tad  tad viparītam asac ca eva aham arjuna na punar  atyantam eva asad bhagavān svayam kārya kāraṇe vā sadasatī ye pūrva uktaiḥ  nivṛtti prakāraiḥ  ekatva pṛthaktva ādi vijñānaiḥ  yajñaiḥ  mām pūjayanta upāsate jñāna vidaḥ te yathā vijñānam mām eva prāpnuvanti ye punar  ajñāḥ kāma kāmāḥ traividyā ṛc yajuḥ sāma vidaḥ  mām vasu ādideva rūpiṇam somapāḥ somam pibanti iti somapāḥ tena eva soma pānena pūta pāpāḥ śuddha kilbiṣāḥ yajñaiḥ  agniṣṭoma ādibhiḥ  iṣṭvā pūjayitvā svargatim svarga gamanam svar eva gatiḥ svargatis tām prārthayante te ca puṇyam puṇya phalam āsādya saṃprāpya sura indra lokam śatakratoḥ sthānam aśnanti bhuñjate divyān divi bhavān aprākṛtān deva bhogān devānām bhogān te tam bhuktvā svarga lokam viśālam vistīrṇam kṣīṇe puṇye martya lokam viśanti āviśanti evam yathā uktena prakāreṇa trayī dharmam kevalam vaidikam karma anuprapannā gatāgatam gatam ca āgatam ca gatāgatam gamana āgamanam kāma kāmāḥ kāmān kāmayanta iti kāma kāmā labhante gatāgatam eva na tu svātantryam kvacid  labhanta iti  arthaḥ ye punar  niṣkāmāḥ samyak darśinaḥ ananyā apṛthak bhūtāḥ param devam nārāyaṇam ātma tvena gatāḥ santaś cintayantaḥ  mām ye janāḥ saṃnyāsinaḥ paryupāsate teṣām parama artha darśinām nitya abhiyuktānām satata abhiyoginām yogakṣemam yogaḥ  aprāptasya prāpaṇam kṣemaḥ  tad rakṣaṇam tad ubhayam vahāmi prāpayāmi  aham jñānī tu  ātmā eva me matam sa ca mama priyaḥ yasmāt  tasmāt  te mama ātma bhūtāḥ priyāḥ  ca iti nanu  anyeṣām api bhaktānām yogakṣemam vahati  eva bhagavān satyam vahati  eva kiṃtu  ayam viśeṣaḥ anye ye bhaktās te ātma artham svayam api yogakṣemam īhante ananya darśinaḥ  tu na ātma artham yogakṣemam īhante na hi te jīvite maraṇe vā ātmanaḥ  gṛddhim kurvanti kevalam eva bhagavat śaraṇās te atas  bhagavān eva teṣām yogakṣemam vahati iti nanu  anyā api devatā as tvam eva ced  tad bhaktāḥ  ca tvām eva yajante satyam evam ye api  anya devatā bhaktā anyāsu devatāsu bhaktā anya devatā bhaktāḥ santaḥ  yajante pūjayanti śraddhayā āstikya buddhyā anvitā anugatāḥ te api mām eva kaunteya yajanti  avidhi pūrvakam avidhiḥ  ajñānam tad pūrvakam yajanta iti  arthaḥ kasmāt  te avidhi pūrvakam yajanta iti  ucyate yasmāt  aham hi sarva yajñānām śrautānām smārtānām ca sarveṣām yajñānām devatā ātma tvena bhoktā ca prabhuḥ  eva ca mad svāmikaḥ  hi yajñaḥ adhiyajñaḥ  aham eva atra iti hi  uktam tathā na tu mām abhijānanti tattvena yathāvat  atas  ca avidhi pūrvakam iṣṭvā yāga phala āc cyavanti pracyavante te ye api  anya devatā bhaktimat tvena avidhi pūrvakam yajante teṣām api yāga phalam avaśyaṃbhāvi katham yānti gacchanti devavratā deveṣu vratam niyamaḥ  bhaktiḥ  ca yeṣām te devavratā devān yānti pitṝn agniṣu  ātta ādīn yānti pitṛ vratāḥ śrāddha ādi kriyā parāḥ pitṛ bhaktāḥ bhūtāni vināyaka mātṛ gaṇa catur bhaginī ādīni yānti bhūta ijyā bhūtānām pūjakāḥ yānti madya ajinaḥ  madya jana śīlā vaiṣṇavā mām eva yānti samāne api  āyāse mām eva na bhajante ajñānāt  tena te alpa phala bhājaḥ  bhavanti iti  arthaḥ na kevalam mad bhaktānām anāvṛtti lakṣaṇam ananta phalam sukha ārādhanaḥ  ca aham katham patram puṣpam phalam toyam udakam yaḥ me mahyam bhaktyā prayacchati tad  aham patra ādi bhaktyā upahṛtam bhakti pūrvakam prāpitam bhakti upahṛtam aśnāmi gṛhṇāmi prayata ātmanaḥ śuddha buddheḥ yatas  evam atas  yad  karoṣi svatas  prāptam yad  aśnāsi yad  ca juhoṣi havanam nirvartayasi śrautam smārtam vā yad  dadāsi prayacchasi brāhmaṇa ādibhyaḥ  hiraṇyāt na ājya ādi yad  tapasyasi tapaḥ  carasi kaunteya tad  kuruṣva mad arpaṇam mad samarpaṇam evam kurvatas tava yad  bhavati tad  sṛṇu śubha aśubha phalaiḥ śubha aśubhe iṣṭa aniṣṭe phale yeṣām tāni śubha aśubha phalāni karmāṇi taiḥ śubha aśubha phalaiḥ karma bandhanaiḥ karmāṇi  eva bandhanāni karma bandhanāni taiḥ karma bandhanaiḥ  evam mad arpaṇam kurvan mokṣyase saḥ  ayam saṃnyāsa yogaḥ  nāma saṃnyāsaḥ  ca asau mad samarpaṇa tayā karma tvāt  yogaḥ  ca asau   iti tena saṃnyāsa yogena yukta ātma
